# PHASE 6: PAD ENGINE ADVANCED

```cpp
// include/maestro/pad/pad_engine.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include <functional>
#include <memory>
#include <vector>

namespace maestro {

/**
 * @brief Pad assignment types
 */
enum class PadType {
    MidiNote,        // Single MIDI note
    MidiChord,       // Chord
    MidiCC,          // Control change
    MidiProgram,     // Program change
    Sample,          // Audio sample
    Phrase,          // MIDI phrase/pattern
    StyleSection,    // Style variation control
    Registration,    // Registration change
    Macro,           // Multiple actions
    Script           // Custom script
};

/**
 * @brief Pad trigger modes
 */
enum class PadTriggerMode {
    OneShot,         // Play once
    Gate,            // Play while held
    Toggle,          // Toggle on/off
    Retrigger,       // Restart on each press
    Latch            // Play until pressed again
};

/**
 * @brief Pad configuration
 */
struct PadConfig {
    std::string name;
    PadType type = PadType::MidiNote;
    PadTriggerMode triggerMode = PadTriggerMode::OneShot;
    QColor color = Qt::gray;
    
    // MIDI settings
    MidiNote note = 60;
    MidiChannel channel = 10;
    MidiVelocity velocity = 100;
    bool velocitySensitive = true;
    std::vector<MidiNote> chord;     // For chord type
    MidiCC ccNumber = 0;
    uint8_t ccValue = 127;
    
    // Sample settings
    std::string samplePath;
    float sampleGain = 1.0f;
    float samplePitch = 0.0f;        // Semitones
    bool sampleLoop = false;
    
    // Phrase settings
    std::vector<midi::MidiEvent> phrase;
    bool phraseSync = false;
    float phraseSpeed = 1.0f;
    
    // Quantization
    bool quantize = false;
    int quantizeValue = 4;           // Quarter note
    
    // Choke group
    int chokeGroup = 0;              // 0 = none
    
    // Actions
    int registrationNumber = 0;
    StyleEngine::Section styleSection;
    std::vector<std::string> macroActions;
};

/**
 * @brief Pad bank
 */
struct PadBank {
    std::string name;
    std::vector<PadConfig> pads;
    int rows = 4;
    int cols = 4;
};

/**
 * @brief Main pad engine
 */
class MAESTRO_API PadEngine {
public:
    PadEngine(MidiEngine& midi, AudioEngine& audio);
    ~PadEngine();
    
    void initialize();
    void process(uint32_t numFrames);
    
    // Bank management
    int createBank(const std::string& name, int rows = 4, int cols = 4);
    void deleteBank(int bankId);
    void setActiveBank(int bankId);
    int getActiveBank() const;
    PadBank& getBank(int bankId);
    std::vector<int> getBankIds() const;
    
    // Pad configuration
    void setPadConfig(int bankId, int padIndex, const PadConfig& config);
    PadConfig getPadConfig(int bankId, int padIndex) const;
    int getPadCount(int bankId) const;
    
    // Pad triggering
    void triggerPad(int padIndex, MidiVelocity velocity = 127);
    void releasePad(int padIndex);
    void stopPad(int padIndex);
    void stopAllPads();
    
    // State
    bool isPadActive(int padIndex) const;
    float getPadProgress(int padIndex) const;  // For phrases/samples
    
    // MIDI learn
    void startMidiLearn(int padIndex);
    void stopMidiLearn();
    bool isMidiLearning() const;
    int getMidiLearnPad() const;
    
    // External MIDI input
    void processMidiInput(const midi::MidiMessage& msg);
    
    // Pad grid settings
    void setGridSize(int rows, int cols);
    std::pair<int, int> getGridSize() const;
    
    // Quantization
    void setGlobalQuantize(bool enabled);
    void setQuantizeValue(int divisions);
    void setQuantizeStrength(float strength);
    
    // Recording
    void startRecording(int padIndex);
    void stopRecording();
    bool isRecording() const;
    
    // Sample management
    Result<void> assignSample(int bankId, int padIndex, 
                               const std::string& samplePath);
    Result<void> recordSample(int bankId, int padIndex, float duration);
    
    // Phrase management
    Result<void> assignPhrase(int bankId, int padIndex,
                               const std::vector<midi::MidiEvent>& phrase);
    void startPhraseCapture(int padIndex);
    void stopPhraseCapture();
    
    // Sequences
    struct PadSequenceStep {
        int padIndex;
        TickCount tick;
        MidiVelocity velocity;
    };
    
    void createSequence(const std::string& name, 
                        const std::vector<PadSequenceStep>& steps);
    void playSequence(const std::string& name);
    void stopSequence();
    
    // Performance modes
    enum class PerformanceMode {
        Normal,
        MPC,              // MPC-style 16-pad mode
        Keyboard,         // Chromatic keyboard mode
        ChordPads,        // Chord pad mode
        SlicePlayer       // Sample slicer mode
    };
    void setPerformanceMode(PerformanceMode mode);
    PerformanceMode getPerformanceMode() const;
    
    // Callbacks
    using PadCallback = std::function<void(int padIndex, bool active, 
                                           MidiVelocity velocity)>;
    void setPadCallback(PadCallback callback);
    
    // Preset management
    Result<void> savePreset(const std::string& path);
    Result<void> loadPreset(const std::string& path);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Sample slicer for pad assignment
 */
class MAESTRO_API SampleSlicer {
public:
    SampleSlicer();
    ~SampleSlicer();
    
    // Load sample
    Result<void> loadSample(const std::string& path);
    
    // Slicing methods
    enum class SliceMethod {
        Equal,           // Equal divisions
        Transient,       // Detect transients
        Beat,            // Beat detection
        Manual           // Manual markers
    };
    
    void sliceEqual(int numSlices);
    void sliceByTransients(float sensitivity = 0.5f);
    void sliceByBeats(double bpm);
    void addSliceMarker(uint32_t samplePosition);
    void removeSliceMarker(int index);
    
    // Get slices
    struct Slice {
        uint32_t start;
        uint32_t end;
        float gain = 1.0f;
    };
    std::vector<Slice> getSlices() const;
    
    // Assign to pads
    void assignToPadBank(PadEngine& engine, int bankId);
    
    // Playback
    void playSlice(int index);
    void stopPlayback();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief MPC-style pad controller
 */
class MAESTRO_API MPCController {
public:
    MPCController(PadEngine& pads);
    
    // Mode
    enum class Mode {
        PadMode,
        NoteRepeat,
        ChromaticMode,
        ProgressionMode,
        Pad16,
        Pad64
    };
    void setMode(Mode mode);
    Mode getMode() const { return mode_; }
    
    // Note repeat
    void setNoteRepeatEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setNoteRepeatRate(float hz);
    void setNoteRepeatGate(float gate);
    void setNoteRepeatSwing(float swing);
    
    // Swing
    void setSwing(float amount);
    void setSwingRate(int divisor);
    
    // Full level
    void setFullLevelEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setFullLevelVelocity(MidiVelocity velocity);
    
    // 16 Level
    void set16LevelEnabled(bool enabled);
    void set16LevelParameter(int param);  // 0=velocity, 1=tune, 2=filter, etc.
    
    // Timing correct
    void setTimingCorrect(bool enabled);
    void setTimingCorrectValue(int tc);  // 1/4, 1/8, 1/16, etc.
    
    // Process
    void process(TickCount currentTick);

private:
    PadEngine& pads_;
    Mode mode_ = Mode::PadMode;
    
    bool noteRepeatEnabled_ = false;
    float noteRepeatRate_ = 4.0f;
    float noteRepeatGate_ = 0.5f;
    
    bool fullLevelEnabled_ = false;
    MidiVelocity fullLevelVelocity_ = 127;
    
    bool level16Enabled_ = false;
    int level16Param_ = 0;
    
    bool timingCorrect_ = false;
    int timingCorrectValue_ = 16;
    
    float swing_ = 0.0f;
};

} // namespace maestro
```

# PHASE 7: PLUGIN SYSTEM

```cpp
// include/maestro/plugin/plugin_host.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <functional>

namespace maestro::plugin {

/**
 * @brief Plugin format types
 */
enum class PluginFormat {
    VST2,
    VST3,
    AU,
    CLAP,
    LV2,
    Internal
};

/**
 * @brief Plugin category
 */
enum class PluginCategory {
    Unknown,
    Effect,
    Instrument,
    Analyzer,
    Dynamics,
    EQ,
    Filter,
    Delay,
    Reverb,
    Modulation,
    Distortion,
    Utility
};

/**
 * @brief Plugin information
 */
struct PluginInfo {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string manufacturer;
    std::string version;
    std::string path;
    PluginFormat format;
    PluginCategory category;
    bool isInstrument;
    bool hasEditor;
    int numAudioInputs;
    int numAudioOutputs;
    int numMidiInputs;
    int numMidiOutputs;
    uint64_t uniqueId;
    
    // Cached info
    std::string description;
    std::vector<std::string> tags;
    int64_t fileSize;
    int64_t lastModified;
};

/**
 * @brief Plugin parameter
 */
struct PluginParameter {
    int index;
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string label;
    float defaultValue;
    float minValue;
    float maxValue;
    int numSteps;         // 0 = continuous
    bool isAutomatable;
    bool isBypass;
    
    std::string unit;
    std::function<std::string(float)> valueToString;
    std::function<float(const std::string&)> stringToValue;
};

/**
 * @brief Plugin instance interface
 */
class MAESTRO_API PluginInstance {
public:
    virtual ~PluginInstance() = default;
    
    // Info
    virtual const PluginInfo& getInfo() const = 0;
    virtual bool isInstrument() const = 0;
    
    // Lifecycle
    virtual Result<void> activate() = 0;
    virtual void deactivate() = 0;
    virtual bool isActive() const = 0;
    
    // Audio/MIDI
    virtual void prepare(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize) = 0;
    virtual void process(float* const* audioIn, float* const* audioOut,
                        int numChannels, int numFrames) = 0;
    virtual void processMidi(const midi::MidiMessage& msg) = 0;
    virtual void processEvents(const std::vector<midi::MidiEvent>& events) = 0;
    
    // Parameters
    virtual int getNumParameters() const = 0;
    virtual PluginParameter getParameterInfo(int index) const = 0;
    virtual float getParameter(int index) const = 0;
    virtual void setParameter(int index, float value) = 0;
    virtual std::string getParameterText(int index) const = 0;
    
    // State
    virtual std::vector<uint8_t> getState() const = 0;
    virtual Result<void> setState(const std::vector<uint8_t>& state) = 0;
    virtual std::string getStateAsXml() const = 0;
    virtual Result<void> setStateFromXml(const std::string& xml) = 0;
    
    // Presets
    virtual int getNumPresets() const = 0;
    virtual std::string getPresetName(int index) const = 0;
    virtual int getCurrentPreset() const = 0;
    virtual void setCurrentPreset(int index) = 0;
    
    // Editor
    virtual bool hasEditor() const = 0;
    virtual void openEditor(void* parentWindow) = 0;
    virtual void closeEditor() = 0;
    virtual std::pair<int, int> getEditorSize() const = 0;
    virtual void setEditorSize(int width, int height) = 0;
    virtual bool isEditorResizable() const = 0;
    
    // Bypass
    virtual void setBypass(bool bypass) = 0;
    virtual bool isBypassed() const = 0;
    
    // Latency
    virtual int getLatency() const = 0;
    virtual int getTailLength() const = 0;
};

/**
 * @brief Plugin scanner
 */
class MAESTRO_API PluginScanner {
public:
    PluginScanner();
    ~PluginScanner();
    
    // Scan directories
    void addSearchPath(const std::string& path);
    void removeSearchPath(const std::string& path);
    std::vector<std::string> getSearchPaths() const;
    
    // Scanning
    void startScan();
    void stopScan();
    bool isScanning() const;
    float getScanProgress() const;
    
    // Results
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getScannedPlugins() const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getFailedPlugins() const;
    
    // Cache
    void saveCache(const std::string& path);
    void loadCache(const std::string& path);
    void clearCache();
    
    // Filter
    std::vector<PluginInfo> findPlugins(const std::string& query) const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getPluginsByCategory(PluginCategory cat) const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getPluginsByFormat(PluginFormat format) const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getInstruments() const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getEffects() const;
    
    // Callbacks
    using ScanCallback = std::function<void(const PluginInfo&, bool success)>;
    using ProgressCallback = std::function<void(float progress, 
                                                 const std::string& current)>;
    void setScanCallback(ScanCallback callback);
    void setProgressCallback(ProgressCallback callback);
    
    // Blacklist
    void addToBlacklist(const std::string& id);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;

// include/maestro/network/network_midi.hpp
#pragma once

/**
 * @brief RTP-MIDI (Network MIDI) session
 */
class MAESTRO_API RTPMidiSession {
public:
    RTPMidiSession();
    ~RTPMidiSession();
    
    // Session management
    Result<void> create(const std::string& name, int port = 5004);
    void destroy();
    bool isActive() const;
    
    // Connections
    Result<void> connect(const std::string& host, int port);
    void disconnect(const std::string& host);
    std::vector<std::string> getConnectedHosts() const;
    
    // Discovery (Bonjour/mDNS)
    void startDiscovery();
    void stopDiscovery();
    struct DiscoveredSession {
        std::string name;
        std::string host;
        int port;
    };
    std::vector<DiscoveredSession> getDiscoveredSessions() const;
    
    // MIDI I/O
    void sendMidi(const midi::MidiMessage& msg);
    void sendSysEx(const midi::SysExMessage& msg);
    
    using MidiCallback = std::function<void(const midi::MidiMessage&, 
                                            const std::string& source)>;
    void setMidiCallback(MidiCallback callback);
    
    // Latency compensation
    void setLatencyCompensation(int ms);
    int getLatencyCompensation() const;
    
    // Statistics
    struct Statistics {
        uint64_t packetsSent;
        uint64_t packetsReceived;
        uint64_t packetsLost;
        double jitter;
        double latency;
    };
    Statistics getStatistics() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

    // Callbacks

                                            const std::string& editType,
                                            const std::vector<uint8_t>& data)>;
    using ChatCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& participantId,
                                            const std::string& message)>;
    using ParticipantCallback = std::function<void(const Participant&, 
                                                    bool joined)>;
    
    void setEditCallback(EditCallback callback);
    void setChatCallback(ChatCallback callback);
    void setParticipantCallback(ParticipantCallback callback);
    
    // Conflict resolution
    enum class ConflictStrategy { LastWrite, Merge, Prompt };
    void setConflictStrategy(ConflictStrategy strategy);

    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;

```cpp
// tests/unit/test_midi.cpp
#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"

using namespace maestro::midi;

TEST(MidiMessageTest, NoteOnCreation) {
    auto msg = MidiMessage::noteOn(0, 60, 100);
    
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.type(), MessageType::NoteOn);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.channel(), 0);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.note(), 60);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.velocity(), 100);
    EXPECT_TRUE(msg.isNoteOn());
    EXPECT_FALSE(msg.isNoteOff());
}

TEST(MidiMessageTest, NoteOffCreation) {
    auto msg = MidiMessage::noteOff(5, 72, 0);
    
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.type(), MessageType::NoteOff);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.channel(), 5);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.note(), 72);
    EXPECT_TRUE(msg.isNoteOff());
}

TEST(MidiMessageTest, ZeroVelocityIsNoteOff) {
    auto msg = MidiMessage::noteOn(0, 60, 0);
    
    EXPECT_TRUE(msg.isNoteOff());
    EXPECT_FALSE(msg.isNoteOn());
}

TEST(MidiMessageTest, ControlChange) {
    auto msg = MidiMessage::controlChange(2, CC::ModWheel, 64);
    
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.type(), MessageType::ControlChange);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.channel(), 2);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.ccNumber(), CC::ModWheel);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.ccValue(), 64);
    EXPECT_TRUE(msg.isCC());
}

TEST(MidiMessageTest, PitchBend) {
    auto msg = MidiMessage::pitchBend(0, 0);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.pitchBendValue(), 0);
    
    msg = MidiMessage::pitchBend(0, 8191);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.pitchBendValue(), 8191);
    
    msg = MidiMessage::pitchBend(0, -8192);
    EXPECT_EQ(msg.pitchBendValue(), -8192);
}

TEST(MidiMessageTest, ToString) {
    auto noteOn = MidiMessage::noteOn(0, 60, 100);
    EXPECT_FALSE(noteOn.toString().empty());
    EXPECT_NE(noteOn.toString().find("NoteOn"), std::string::npos);
    
    auto cc = MidiMessage::controlChange(0, 7, 127);
    EXPECT_NE(cc.toString().find("CC"), std::string::npos);
}

```cpp
// tests/unit/test_audio_dsp.cpp
#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include "maestro/audio/dsp/dsp_common.hpp"
#include <cmath>

using namespace maestro::dsp;

TEST(DSPUtilsTest, DbToGain) {
    EXPECT_NEAR(dbToGain(0.0f), 1.0f, 0.0001f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(dbToGain(-6.0f), 0.5011f, 0.001f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(dbToGain(-20.0f), 0.1f, 0.001f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(dbToGain(6.0f), 1.9953f, 0.001f);
}

TEST(DSPUtilsTest, GainToDb) {
    EXPECT_NEAR(gainToDb(1.0f), 0.0f, 0.001f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(gainToDb(0.5f), -6.02f, 0.01f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(gainToDb(2.0f), 6.02f, 0.01f);
}

TEST(DSPUtilsTest, MidiToFrequency) {
    EXPECT_NEAR(midiToFrequency(69), 440.0f, 0.01f);  // A4
    EXPECT_NEAR(midiToFrequency(60), 261.63f, 0.01f); // C4
    EXPECT_NEAR(midiToFrequency(81), 880.0f, 0.01f);  // A5
}

TEST(BiquadFilterTest, LowPassBasic) {
    BiquadFilter filter;
    filter.setCoefficients(BiquadFilter::Type::LowPass, 1000.0f, 0.707f, 
                           0.0f, 44100.0f);
    
    // Process impulse
    float output = filter.process(1.0f);
    EXPECT_NE(output, 0.0f);
    
    // Process silence
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
        output = filter.process(0.0f);
    }
    EXPECT_NEAR(output, 0.0f, 0.0001f);
}

TEST(BiquadFilterTest, Reset) {
    BiquadFilter filter;
    filter.setCoefficients(BiquadFilter::Type::LowPass, 1000.0f, 0.707f,
                           0.0f, 44100.0f);
    
    // Process some samples
    filter.process(1.0f);
    filter.process(0.5f);
    
    // Reset
    filter.reset();
    
    // Output should be zero for zero input after reset
    EXPECT_NEAR(filter.process(0.0f), 0.0f, 0.0001f);
}

TEST(CircularBufferTest, WriteRead) {
    CircularBuffer<float, 1024> buffer;
    buffer.clear();
    
    buffer.write(1.0f);
    buffer.write(2.0f);
    buffer.write(3.0f);
    
    EXPECT_EQ(buffer.read(1), 3.0f);
    EXPECT_EQ(buffer.read(2), 2.0f);
    EXPECT_EQ(buffer.read(3), 1.0f);
}

TEST(CircularBufferTest, InterpolatedRead) {
    CircularBuffer<float, 1024> buffer;
    buffer.clear();
    
    buffer.write(0.0f);
    buffer.write(1.0f);
    
    EXPECT_NEAR(buffer.readInterpolated(0.5f), 0.5f, 0.0001f);
}

TEST(EnvelopeFollowerTest, AttackRelease) {
    EnvelopeFollower follower;
    follower.setAttackTime(1.0f, 44100.0f);
    follower.setReleaseTime(10.0f, 44100.0f);
    follower.reset();
    
    // Attack phase
    float peak = 0.0f;
    for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        float env = follower.process(1.0f
# 🎹 MaestroStudio - Phase 2 Development (Continued)

## Continuing from Unit Tests...

```cpp
// tests/unit/test_audio_dsp.cpp (continued)

TEST(EnvelopeFollowerTest, AttackRelease) {
    EnvelopeFollower follower;
    follower.setAttackTime(1.0f, 44100.0f);
    follower.setReleaseTime(10.0f, 44100.0f);
    follower.reset();
    
    // Attack phase
    float peak = 0.0f;
    for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        float env = follower.process(1.0f);
        EXPECT_GE(env, peak);  // Should be increasing
        peak = env;
    }
    EXPECT_GT(peak, 0.9f);  // Should be close to 1.0
    
    // Release phase
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
        float env = follower.process(0.0f);
        EXPECT_LE(env, peak);  // Should be decreasing
        peak = env;
    }
    EXPECT_LT(peak, 0.1f);  // Should be close to 0
}

TEST(LFOTest, SineWave) {
    LFO lfo;
    lfo.setFrequency(1.0f, 1000.0f);  // 1Hz at 1kHz sample rate
    lfo.setWaveform(LFO::Waveform::Sine);
    lfo.reset();
    
    // Collect one complete cycle
    std::vector<float> samples;
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
        samples.push_back(lfo.process());
    }
    
    // Check that it oscillates between -1 and 1
    float minVal = *std::min_element(samples.begin(), samples.end());
    float maxVal = *std::max_element(samples.begin(), samples.end());
    
    EXPECT_NEAR(minVal, -1.0f, 0.01f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(maxVal, 1.0f, 0.01f);
    
    // Check periodicity (sample 0 should be close to sample 1000)
    EXPECT_NEAR(samples[0], samples[999], 0.1f);
}

TEST(LFOTest, TriangleWave) {
    LFO lfo;
    lfo.setFrequency(1.0f, 1000.0f);
    lfo.setWaveform(LFO::Waveform::Triangle);
    lfo.reset();
    
    std::vector<float> samples;
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
        samples.push_back(lfo.process());
    }
    
    // Triangle should still be bounded
    for (float s : samples) {
        EXPECT_GE(s, -1.0f);
        EXPECT_LE(s, 1.0f);
    }
}
```

#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include "maestro/style/style_engine.hpp"

    }

TEST(ChordInfoTest, MajorChord) {
    ChordInfo chord;
    chord.root = 60;  // C
    chord.type = ChordInfo::Type::Major;
    
    auto notes = chord.getNotes();
    ASSERT_EQ(notes.size(), 3);
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[0], 60);  // C
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[1], 64);  // E
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[2], 67);  // G
}

TEST(ChordInfoTest, MinorChord) {
    ChordInfo chord;
    chord.root = 60;  // C
    chord.type = ChordInfo::Type::Minor;
    
    auto notes = chord.getNotes();
    ASSERT_EQ(notes.size(), 3);
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[0], 60);  // C
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[1], 63);  // Eb
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[2], 67);  // G
}

TEST(ChordInfoTest, SeventhChord) {
    ChordInfo chord;
    chord.root = 60;  // C
    chord.type = ChordInfo::Type::Seventh;
    
    auto notes = chord.getNotes();
    ASSERT_EQ(notes.size(), 4);
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[0], 60);  // C
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[1], 64);  // E
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[2], 67);  // G
    EXPECT_EQ(notes[3], 70);  // Bb
}

TEST(ChordInfoTest, Detection) {
    std::vector<MidiNote> notes = {60, 64, 67};  // C major
    auto detected = ChordInfo::detect(notes);
    
    EXPECT_EQ(detected.root, 60);
    EXPECT_EQ(detected.type, ChordInfo::Type::Major);
}

TEST(ChordInfoTest, DetectionMinor) {
    std::vector<MidiNote> notes = {57, 60, 64};  // A minor
    auto detected = ChordInfo::detect(notes);
    
    EXPECT_EQ(detected.root, 57);
    EXPECT_EQ(detected.type, ChordInfo::Type::Minor);
}

TEST(ChordInfoTest, ToString) {
    ChordInfo chord;
    chord.root = 60;
    chord.type = ChordInfo::Type::Major;
    
    std::string str = chord.toString();
    EXPECT_EQ(str, "C");
    
    chord.type = ChordInfo::Type::Minor;
    str = chord.toString();
    EXPECT_EQ(str, "Cm");
    
    chord.type = ChordInfo::Type::Seventh;
    str = chord.toString();
    EXPECT_EQ(str, "C7");
}

```cpp
// tests/unit/test_effects.cpp
#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include "maestro/audio/effects/reverb.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/effects/delay.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/effects/dynamics.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/effects/eq.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <cmath>

using namespace maestro::effects;

class ReverbTest : public ::testing::Test {
protected:
    Reverb reverb;
    std::vector<float> inputL, inputR;
    std::vector<float> outputL, outputR;
    
    void SetUp() override {
        reverb.prepare(44100, 512);
        inputL.resize(512, 0.0f);
        inputR.resize(512, 0.0f);
        outputL.resize(512, 0.0f);
        outputR.resize(512, 0.0f);
    }
};

TEST_F(ReverbTest, SilenceInSilenceOut) {
    float* channels[2] = {outputL.data(), outputR.data()};
    
    // Process silence
    for (int block = 0; block < 100; block++) {
        reverb.process(channels, 2, 512);
    }
    
    // After many blocks of silence, output should be near zero
    float maxOutput = 0.0f;
    for (int i = 0; i < 512; i++) {
        maxOutput = std::max(maxOutput, std::abs(outputL[i]));
        maxOutput = std::max(maxOutput, std::abs(outputR[i]));
    }
    EXPECT_LT(maxOutput, 0.001f);
}

TEST_F(ReverbTest, ImpulseResponse) {
    // Create impulse
    inputL[0] = 1.0f;
    inputR[0] = 1.0f;
    
    std::copy(inputL.begin(), inputL.end(), outputL.begin());
    std::copy(inputR.begin(), inputR.end(), outputR.begin());
    
    float* channels[2] = {outputL.data(), outputR.data()};
    reverb.setWet(1.0f);
    reverb.setDry(0.0f);
    reverb.process(channels, 2, 512);
    
    // Should have some output after impulse
    float sumSquares = 0.0f;
    for (int i = 0; i < 512; i++) {
        sumSquares += outputL[i] * outputL[i];
        sumSquares += outputR[i] * outputR[i];
    }
    EXPECT_GT(sumSquares, 0.0f);
}

TEST_F(ReverbTest, PresetChange) {
    reverb.setPreset(Reverb::Preset::SmallRoom);
    EXPECT_LT(reverb.getRoomSize(), 0.5f);
    
    reverb.setPreset(Reverb::Preset::Cathedral);
    EXPECT_GT(reverb.getRoomSize(), 0.7f);
}

class CompressorTest : public ::testing::Test {
protected:
    Compressor comp;
    
    void SetUp() override {
        comp.prepare(44100, 512);
        comp.setThreshold(-20.0f);
        comp.setRatio(4.0f);
        comp.setAttack(10.0f);
        comp.setRelease(100.0f);
    }
};

TEST_F(CompressorTest, BelowThresholdNoCompression) {
    std::vector<float> input(512, 0.05f);  // About -26dB
    float* channels[2] = {input.data(), input.data()};
    
    comp.process(channels, 2, 512);
    
    // Should have minimal gain reduction
    EXPECT_NEAR(comp.getGainReduction(), 0.0f, 1.0f);
}

TEST_F(CompressorTest, AboveThresholdCompression) {
    std::vector<float> input(512, 0.5f);  // About -6dB, well above threshold
    float* channels[2] = {input.data(), input.data()};
    
    // Process multiple blocks to let attack settle
    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        std::fill(input.begin(), input.end(), 0.5f);
        comp.process(channels, 2, 512);
    }
    
    // Should have significant gain reduction
    EXPECT_GT(comp.getGainReduction(), 3.0f);
}

class ParametricEQTest : public ::testing::Test {
protected:
    ParametricEQ eq;
    
    void SetUp() override {
        eq.prepare(44100, 512);
    }
};

TEST_F(ParametricEQTest, FlatResponseAtUnity) {
    // All bands at 0dB should be flat
    for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
        ParametricEQ::Band band;
        band.gain = 0.0f;
        band.enabled = true;
        eq.setBand(i, band);
    }
    
    // Process unit impulse
    std::vector<float> input(512, 0.0f);
    input[0] = 1.0f;
    float* channels[2] = {input.data(), input.data()};
    
    eq.process(channels, 2, 512);
    
    // First sample should be close to 1.0 (some filter delay expected)
    // This is a simplified test - real test would check frequency response
    EXPECT_GT(std::abs(input[0]), 0.5f);
}
```

```cpp
// tests/integration/test_engine_integration.cpp
#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include "maestro/core/engine.hpp"
#include <thread>
#include <chrono>

using namespace maestro;

class EngineIntegrationTest : public ::testing::Test {
protected:
    void SetUp() override {
        // Reset engine state
    }
    
    void TearDown() override {
        MaestroEngine::instance().shutdown();
    }
};

TEST_F(EngineIntegrationTest, InitializeAndStart) {
    MaestroEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 44100;
    config.bufferSize = 512;
    config.audioDriver = "auto";
    
    auto result = MaestroEngine::instance().initialize(config);
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isSuccess());
    
    result = MaestroEngine::instance().start();
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isSuccess());
    EXPECT_TRUE(MaestroEngine::instance().isRunning());
    
    result = MaestroEngine::instance().stop();
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isSuccess());
    EXPECT_FALSE(MaestroEngine::instance().isRunning());
}

TEST_F(EngineIntegrationTest, MidiEngineBasic) {
    MaestroEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 44100;
    config.bufferSize = 512;
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(MaestroEngine::instance().initialize(config).isSuccess());
    
    auto& midi = MaestroEngine::instance().midi();
    auto inputs = midi.getInputPorts();
    auto outputs = midi.getOutputPorts();
    
    // Should have some ports (even if virtual)
    // This depends on the system, so just check it doesn't crash
    SUCCEED();
}

TEST_F(EngineIntegrationTest, AudioEnginePerformance) {
    MaestroEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 44100;
    config.bufferSize = 256;
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(MaestroEngine::instance().initialize(config).isSuccess());
    ASSERT_TRUE(MaestroEngine::instance().start().isSuccess());
    
    // Let it run for a bit
    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(500));
    
    auto perf = MaestroEngine::instance().getPerformance();
    
    // CPU usage should be reasonable
    EXPECT_LT(perf.cpuUsage, 50.0);
    
    // Latency should match buffer size
    double expectedLatency = (256.0 / 44100.0) * 1000.0;  // in ms
    EXPECT_NEAR(perf.audioLatency, expectedLatency, 1.0);
    
    // Should have no underruns in a short test
    EXPECT_EQ(perf.bufferUnderruns, 0);
}

## 10.2 CI/CD Configuration

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: MaestroStudio CI

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main, develop ]

env:
  BUILD_TYPE: Release
  QT_VERSION: '6.5.0'

jobs:
  build-linux:
    runs-on: ubuntu-22.04
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        submodules: recursive
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        sudo apt-get update
        sudo apt-get install -y \
          build-essential \
          cmake \
          ninja-build \
          libasound2-dev \
          libjack-jackd2-dev \
          libpulse-dev \
          libgl1-mesa-dev \
          libxkbcommon-dev \
          libxcb-*-dev \
          libfreetype6-dev \
          libfontconfig1-dev
    
    - name: Install Qt
      uses: jurplel/install-qt-action@v3
      with:
        version: ${{ env.QT_VERSION }}
        modules: 'qtmultimedia'
    
    - name: Configure CMake
      run: |
        cmake -B build -G Ninja \
          -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }} \
          -DMAESTRO_BUILD_TESTS=ON \
          -DMAESTRO_ENABLE_PLUGINS=ON
    
    - name: Build
      run: cmake --build build --config ${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }}
    
    - name: Run Tests
      working-directory: build
      run: ctest -C ${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }} --output-on-failure
    
    - name: Upload artifacts
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: maestro-linux
        path: build/MaestroStudio

  build-macos:
    runs-on: macos-13
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        submodules: recursive
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        brew install cmake ninja
    
    - name: Install Qt
      uses: jurplel/install-qt-action@v3
      with:
        version: ${{ env.QT_VERSION }}
        modules: 'qtmultimedia'
    
    - name: Configure CMake
      run: |
        cmake -B build -G Ninja \
          -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }} \
          -DMAESTRO_BUILD_TESTS=ON \
          -DCMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES="x86_64;arm64"
    
    - name: Build
      run: cmake --build build --config ${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }}
    
    - name: Run Tests
      working-directory: build
      run: ctest -C ${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }} --output-on-failure
    
    - name: Create DMG
      run: |
        cd build
        macdeployqt MaestroStudio.app -dmg
    
    - name: Upload artifacts
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: maestro-macos
        path: build/MaestroStudio.dmg

  build-windows:
    runs-on: windows-2022
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        submodules: recursive
    
    - name: Install Qt
      uses: jurplel/install-qt-action@v3
      with:
        version: ${{ env.QT_VERSION }}
        arch: win64_msvc2019_64
        modules: 'qtmultimedia'
    
    - name: Configure CMake
      run: |
        cmake -B build -G "Visual Studio 17 2022" -A x64 `
          -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }} `
          -DMAESTRO_BUILD_TESTS=ON
    
    - name: Build
      run: cmake --build build --config ${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }}
    
    - name: Run Tests
      working-directory: build
      run: ctest -C ${{ env.BUILD_TYPE }} --output-on-failure
    
    - name: Create Installer
      run: |
        cd build
        windeployqt --release MaestroStudio.exe
    
    - name: Upload artifacts
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: maestro-windows
        path: build/Release/

  build-mobile:
    runs-on: ubuntu-22.04
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        submodules: recursive
    
    - name: Setup Flutter
      uses: subosito/flutter-action@v2
      with:
        flutter-version: '3.16.0'
        channel: 'stable'
    
    - name: Setup Android SDK
      uses: android-actions/setup-android@v3
    
    - name: Build Android
      working-directory: mobile
      run: |
        flutter pub get
        flutter build apk --release
    
    - name: Upload Android APK
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: maestro-android
        path: mobile/build/app/outputs/flutter-apk/app-release.apk

  code-quality:
    runs-on: ubuntu-22.04
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
    - name: Install tools
      run: |
        sudo apt-get update
        sudo apt-get install -y clang-tidy cppcheck
    
    - name: Run clang-tidy
      run: |
        find src include -name '*.cpp' -o -name '*.hpp' | \
          xargs clang-tidy -p build --checks='-*,modernize-*,performance-*,bugprone-*'
    
    - name: Run cppcheck
      run: |
        cppcheck --enable=all --error-exitcode=1 \
          --suppress=missingInclude \
          src/ include/

  release:
    needs: [build-linux, build-macos, build-windows, build-mobile]
    runs-on: ubuntu-22.04
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' && github.event_name == 'push'
    
    steps:
    - name: Download all artifacts
      uses: actions/download-artifact@v3
    
    - name: Create Release
      uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v1
      with:
        tag_name: v${{ github.run_number }}
        name: Release v${{ github.run_number }}
        draft: true
        files: |
          maestro-linux/*
          maestro-macos/*
          maestro-windows/*
          maestro-android/*
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/nightly.yml
name: Nightly Build

on:
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 2 * * *'  # 2 AM UTC daily
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  nightly-build:
    runs-on: ${{ matrix.os }}
    strategy:
      matrix:
        os: [ubuntu-22.04, macos-13, windows-2022]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        submodules: recursive
    
    - name: Build and Test
      run: |
        cmake -B build -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Debug -DMAESTRO_BUILD_TESTS=ON
        cmake --build build
        cd build && ctest --output-on-failure
    
    - name: Run Sanitizers (Linux only)
      if: matrix.os == 'ubuntu-22.04'
      run: |
        cmake -B build-asan -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Debug \
          -DCMAKE_CXX_FLAGS="-fsanitize=address,undefined"
        cmake --build build-asan
        cd build-asan && ctest --output-on-failure
```

# PHASE 11: ADVANCED RECORDING & PLAYBACK

```cpp
// include/maestro/studio/recording.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <functional>
#include <atomic>

namespace maestro::studio {

/**
 * @brief Audio recording engine
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioRecorder {
public:
    AudioRecorder(AudioEngine& audio);
    ~AudioRecorder();
    
    // Configuration
    struct Config {
        std::string outputPath;
        enum Format { WAV, AIFF, FLAC, MP3, OGG } format = WAV;
        int bitDepth = 24;
        SampleRate sampleRate = 44100;
        int numChannels = 2;
        bool realtime = true;
        
        // File options
        bool createNewFileOnOverflow = true;
        size_t maxFileSizeMB = 2048;
        bool addTimestamp = true;
    };
    
    void setConfig(const Config& config);
    Config getConfig() const { return config_; }
    
    // Recording control
    Result<void> arm();
    Result<void> start();
    void stop();
    void pause();
    void resume();
    
    // State
    enum class State { Idle, Armed, Recording, Paused };
    State getState() const { return state_.load(); }
    bool isRecording() const { return state_ == State::Recording; }
    
    // Progress
    double getRecordedTime() const;
    uint64_t getRecordedSamples() const;
    size_t getFileSizeBytes() const;
    
    // Input monitoring
    void setInputMonitoring(bool enabled);
    bool isInputMonitoring() const;
    float getInputLevel(int channel) const;
    
    // Markers during recording
    void addMarker(const std::string& name);
    
    // Punch in/out
    void setPunchIn(double timeSeconds);
    void setPunchOut(double timeSeconds);
    void clearPunchPoints();
    
    // Callbacks
    using RecordingCallback = std::function<void(State, const std::string&)>;
    void setCallback(RecordingCallback callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
    AudioEngine& audio_;
    Config config_;
    std::atomic<State> state_{State::Idle};
};

/**
 * @brief MIDI recording engine
 */
class MAESTRO_API MidiRecorder {
public:
    MidiRecorder(MidiEngine& midi);
    ~MidiRecorder();
    
    // Recording
    void arm(int trackIndex);
    void disarm(int trackIndex);
    void start();
    void stop();
    
    // State
    bool isRecording() const;
    bool isArmed(int trackIndex) const;
    
    // Options
    void setQuantizeOnRecord(bool enabled);
    void setQuantizeValue(int divisions);
    void setCountIn(int bars);
    void setMetronome(bool enabled);
    
    // Overdub
    enum class OverdubMode { Replace, Merge, TakeLayer };
    void setOverdubMode(OverdubMode mode);
    
    // Step recording
    void setStepRecording(bool enabled);
    void setStepLength(int divisions);
    void stepForward();
    void stepBackward();
    
    // Loop recording
    void setLoopRecording(bool enabled);
    void setLoopRegion(TickCount start, TickCount end);
    int getLoopTakeCount() const;
    void selectLoopTake(int take);
    
    // Get recorded data
    std::vector<midi::MidiEvent> getRecordedEvents() const;
    void clearRecordedEvents();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Multi-take manager
 */
class MAESTRO_API TakeManager {
public:
    struct Take {
        int id;
        std::string name;
        TickCount startTick;
        TickCount endTick;
        std::vector<midi::MidiEvent> midiEvents;
        std::string audioFilePath;
        bool isComped = false;
        float rating = 0.0f;
        QColor color;
    };
    
    struct CompRegion {
        TickCount start;
        TickCount end;
        int takeId;
    };
    
    TakeManager();
    ~TakeManager();
    
    // Take management
    int createTake(const std::string& name);
    void deleteTake(int takeId);
    Take& getTake(int takeId);
    std::vector<int> getTakeIds() const;
    
    // Comping
    void addCompRegion(const CompRegion& region);
    void removeCompRegion(int index);
    std::vector<CompRegion> getCompRegions() const;
    
    // Generate comped result
    Take generateCompedTake();
    
    // Quick comp
    void compFromTake(int takeId, TickCount start, TickCount end);
    void quickSwipe(TickCount position, int takeId);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Audio file import/export
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioFileManager {
public:
    // Import
    struct ImportOptions {
        bool convertSampleRate = true;
        SampleRate targetSampleRate = 44100;
        bool normalize = false;
        bool removeDCOffset = true;
        bool detectTempo = true;
    };
    
    struct ImportResult {
        std::string path;
        SampleRate sampleRate;
        int numChannels;
        uint64_t numSamples;
        double duration;
        double detectedTempo;
        std::vector<uint32_t> transients;
    };
    
    static Result<ImportResult> importFile(const std::string& path,
                                            const ImportOptions& options = {});
    
    // Export
    struct ExportOptions {
        enum Format { WAV, AIFF, FLAC, MP3, OGG, AAC };
        Format format = WAV;
        int bitDepth = 24;  // For lossless
        int bitRate = 320;  // For lossy (kbps)
        SampleRate sampleRate = 44100;
        bool dither = true;
        bool normalize = false;
        float normalizeLevel = -0.3f;  // dB
        
        // Metadata
        std::string title;
        std::string artist;
        std::string album;
        std::string comment;
    };
    
    static Result<void> exportFile(const std::string& inputPath,
                                   const std::string& outputPath,
                                   const ExportOptions& options);
    
    // Batch export
    struct StemExport {
        std::string name;
        std::vector<int> trackIndices;
    };
    
    static Result<void> exportStems(const Project& project,
                                     const std::string& outputDir,
                                     const std::vector<StemExport>& stems,
                                     const ExportOptions& options);
    
    // Mixdown
    static Result<void> mixdown(const Project& project,
                                 const std::string& outputPath,
                                 const ExportOptions& options,
                                 TickCount startTick = 0,
                                 TickCount endTick = -1);
};

/**
 * @brief Timestretch and pitch shift
 */
class MAESTRO_API TimeStretchProcessor {
public:
    enum class Algorithm {
        SoundTouch,      // Good for speech/general
        RubberBand,      // High quality
        Elastique,       // Professional quality
        Simple           // Fast, lower quality
    };
    
    TimeStretchProcessor(Algorithm algorithm = Algorithm::RubberBand);
    ~TimeStretchProcessor();
    
    // Configuration
    void setAlgorithm(Algorithm algorithm);
    void prepare(SampleRate sampleRate, int numChannels);
    
    // Parameters
    void setTimeRatio(double ratio);     // 0.5 = half speed, 2.0 = double speed
    void setPitchSemitones(double semitones);
    void setFormantPreservation(bool preserve);
    
    // Processing
    void process(const float* input, float* output, int numFrames);
    void flush();
    void reset();
    
    // Latency
    int getLatency() const;
    
    // Offline processing
    static Result<void> processFile(const std::string& inputPath,
                                     const std::string& outputPath,
                                     double timeRatio,
                                     double pitchSemitones,
                                     Algorithm algorithm = Algorithm::RubberBand);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::studio

# PHASE 12: AUTOMATION SYSTEM

```cpp
// include/maestro/studio/automation.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <memory>
#include <functional>
#include <map>

namespace maestro::studio {

/**
 * @brief Automation point with curve information
 */
struct AutomationPoint {
    TickCount tick;
    double value;        // Normalized 0-1
    
    enum class Curve {
        Linear,
        Smooth,          // S-curve
        Fast,            // Exponential attack
        Slow,            // Logarithmic attack
        Step,            // Instant change
        SCurve,          // Bezier S-curve
        Pulse            // Impulse
    };
    Curve curve = Curve::Linear;
    
    // Bezier control points (for SCurve)
    double controlX = 0.5;
    double controlY = 0.5;
    
    bool operator<(const AutomationPoint& other) const {
        return tick < other.tick;
    }
};

/**
 * @brief Automation lane for a single parameter
 */
class MAESTRO_API AutomationLane {
public:
    AutomationLane(const std::string& parameterId);
    
    // Parameter info
    std::string getParameterId() const { return parameterId_; }
    void setDisplayName(const std::string& name) { displayName_ = name; }
    std::string getDisplayName() const { return displayName_; }
    
    // Range
    void setRange(double min, double max);
    double getMinValue() const { return minValue_; }
    double getMaxValue() const { return maxValue_; }
    
    // Points
    void addPoint(const AutomationPoint& point);
    void removePoint(int index);
    void movePoint(int index, TickCount newTick, double newValue);
    void setPointCurve(int index, AutomationPoint::Curve curve);
    
    int getPointCount() const { return points_.size(); }
    AutomationPoint& getPoint(int index) { return points_[index]; }
    const AutomationPoint& getPoint(int index) const { return points_[index]; }
    
    // Get value at time
    double getValueAt(TickCount tick) const;
    double getValueAtNormalized(TickCount tick) const;  // 0-1
    
    // Editing
    void clear();
    void scaleValues(double factor);
    void offsetValues(double offset);
    void thin(double tolerance);  // Remove redundant points
    
    // Region operations
    void deleteRegion(TickCount start, TickCount end);
    void copyRegion(TickCount start, TickCount end, 
                    AutomationLane& dest, TickCount destStart) const;
    
    // Drawing
    void drawLine(TickCount start, TickCount end, double startValue, 
                  double endValue, AutomationPoint::Curve curve);
    void drawFreehand(const std::vector<std::pair<TickCount, double>>& points);
    
    // State
    void setEnabled(bool enabled) { enabled_ = enabled; }
    bool isEnabled() const { return enabled_; }
    void setReadEnabled(bool read) { readEnabled_ = read; }
    bool isReadEnabled() const { return readEnabled_; }
    void setWriteEnabled(bool write) { writeEnabled_ = write; }
    bool isWriteEnabled() const { return writeEnabled_; }

private:
    std::string parameterId_;
    std::string displayName_;
    std::vector<AutomationPoint> points_;
    double minValue_ = 0.0;
    double maxValue_ = 1.0;
    bool enabled_ = true;
    bool readEnabled_ = true;
    bool writeEnabled_ = false;
    
    double interpolate(const AutomationPoint& a, const AutomationPoint& b,
                       TickCount tick) const;
};

/**
 * @brief Automation for a track or plugin
 */
class MAESTRO_API AutomationContainer {
public:
    AutomationContainer();
    ~AutomationContainer();
    
    // Lane management
    AutomationLane& addLane(const std::string& parameterId);
    void removeLane(const std::string& parameterId);
    AutomationLane* getLane(const std::string& parameterId);
    const AutomationLane* getLane(const std::string& parameterId) const;
    std::vector<std::string> getLaneIds() const;
    
    // Bulk operations
    void clearAll();
    void enableAll(bool read, bool write);
    
    // Snapshot
    void captureSnapshot(TickCount tick);
    void applySnapshot(TickCount tick);
    
    // Touch/latch automation
    enum class Mode { Off, Read, Touch, Latch, Write };
    void setMode(Mode mode) { mode_ = mode; }
    Mode getMode() const { return mode_; }
    
    // Callback for parameter changes
    using ParameterCallback = std::function<void(const std::string&, double)>;
    void setParameterCallback(ParameterCallback callback);
    
    // Process automation at tick
    void process(TickCount tick);

private:
    std::map<std::string, std::unique_ptr<AutomationLane>> lanes_;
    Mode mode_ = Mode::Read;
    ParameterCallback callback_;
};

/**
 * @brief Automation recording
 */
class MAESTRO_API AutomationRecorder {
public:
    AutomationRecorder(AutomationContainer& container);
    
    // Recording
    void startRecording();
    void stopRecording();
    bool isRecording() const { return recording_; }
    
    // Touch automation
    void touchParameter(const std::string& parameterId);
    void releaseParameter(const std::string& parameterId);
    
    // Write value
    void writeValue(const std::string& parameterId, double value, 
                    TickCount tick);
    
    // Options
    void setThinningEnabled(bool enabled) { thinning_ = enabled; }
    void setThinningTolerance(double tolerance) { tolerance_ = tolerance; }
    
    // Post-processing
    void thinRecordedData();
    void smoothRecordedData(int windowSize);

private:
    AutomationContainer& container_;
    bool recording_ = false;
    bool thinning_ = true;
    double tolerance_ = 0.01;
    
    std::map<std::string, std::vector<std::pair<TickCount, double>>> 
        recordBuffer_;
    std::set<std::string> touchedParams_;
};

/**
 * @brief LFO-based automation
 */
class MAESTRO_API AutomationLFO {
public:
    AutomationLFO();
    
    // Waveform
    enum class Waveform { Sine, Triangle, Square, Sawtooth, Random, Custom };
    void setWaveform(Waveform waveform);
    void setCustomWaveform(const std::vector<float>& samples);
    
    // Parameters
    void setRate(float hz);
    void setRateSync(float noteValue);  // 1.0 = quarter note
    void setSync(bool sync);
    void setDepth(float depth);         // 0-1
    void setPhase(float phase);         // 0-360
    void setOffset(float offset);       // -1 to 1
    
    // Tempo sync
    void setTempo(double bpm);
    
    // Generate values
    float process();
    void reset();
    
    // Apply to automation lane
    void generateToLane(AutomationLane& lane, TickCount start, 
                        TickCount length, int ppqn);

private:
    Waveform waveform_ = Waveform::Sine;
    float rate_ = 1.0f;
    float depth_ = 1.0f;
    float phase_ = 0.0f;
    float offset_ = 0.0f;
    bool sync_ = false;
    double tempo_ = 120.0;
    
    float currentPhase_ = 0.0f;
    std::vector<float> customWaveform_;
};

} // namespace maestro::studio

# PHASE 14: SCRIPTING & MACROS

```cpp
// include/maestro/scripting/script_engine.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <functional>
#include <map>
#include <variant>

namespace maestro::scripting {

using ScriptValue = std::variant<
    std::nullptr_t,
    bool,
    int64_t,
    double,
    std::string,
    std::vector<struct ScriptValue>,
    std::map<std::string, struct ScriptValue>
>;

/**
 * @brief Script execution context
 */
class MAESTRO_API ScriptContext {
public:
    ScriptContext();
    ~ScriptContext();
    
    // Variable access
    void setVariable(const std::string& name, const ScriptValue& value);
    ScriptValue getVariable(const std::string& name) const;
    bool hasVariable(const std::string& name) const;
    
    // Function registration
    using NativeFunction = std::function<ScriptValue(
        const std::vector<ScriptValue>&)>;
    void registerFunction(const std::string& name, NativeFunction func);
    
    // Object registration
    void registerObject(const std::string& name, void* object,
                        const std::string& typeName);
    
    // Output
    using OutputCallback = std::function<void(const std::string&)>;
    void setOutputCallback(OutputCallback callback);
    void print(const std::string& message);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Main script engine (Lua-based)
 */
class MAESTRO_API ScriptEngine {
public:
    ScriptEngine();
    ~ScriptEngine();
    
    // Initialization
    Result<void> initialize();
    void shutdown();
    
    // Script execution
    Result<ScriptValue> execute(const std::string& code);
    Result<ScriptValue> executeFile(const std::string& path);
    
    // Async execution
    void executeAsync(const std::string& code,
                      std::function<void(Result<ScriptValue>)> callback);
    
    // Context
    ScriptContext& getContext() { return *context_; }
    
    // API registration
    void registerMaestroAPI();
    void registerMidiAPI();
    void registerAudioAPI();
    void registerProjectAPI();
    
    // Error handling
    std::string getLastError() const;
    
    // Debug
    void setDebugMode(bool enabled);
    void setBreakpoint(const std::string& file, int line);
    void removeBreakpoint(const std::string& file, int line);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
    std::unique_ptr<ScriptContext> context_;
};

/**
 * @brief Macro recorder/player
 */
class MAESTRO_API MacroEngine {
public:
    struct MacroAction {
        enum Type {
            MidiSend,
            ParameterChange,
            MenuCommand,
            KeyPress,
            Wait,
            Script,
            Loop,
            Condition
        };
        
        Type type;
        std::map<std::string, ScriptValue> parameters;
        double timestamp = 0.0;  // For recording
    };
    
    struct Macro {
        std::string name;
        std::string description;
        std::string category;
        std::vector<MacroAction> actions;
        std::string keyBinding;
        bool recordedTiming = false;
    };
    
    MacroEngine();
    ~MacroEngine();
    
    // Recording
    void startRecording();
    void stopRecording();
    bool isRecording() const;
    void recordAction(const MacroAction& action);
    Macro getRecordedMacro() const;
    
    // Playback
    void play(const Macro& macro);
    void playByName(const std::string& name);
    void stop();
    bool isPlaying() const;
    void setPlaybackSpeed(float speed);
    
    // Management
    void saveMacro(const Macro& macro);
    void deleteMacro(const std::string& name);
    Macro* getMacro(const std::string& name);
    std::vector<std::string> getMacroNames() const;
    std::vector<Macro*> getMacrosByCategory(const std::string& category) const;
    
    // Import/Export
    Result<void> exportMacro(const std::string& name, 
                              const std::string& path);
    Result<void> importMacro(const std::string& path);
    
    // Key bindings
    void setKeyBinding(const std::string& macroName, 
                       const std::string& keySequence);
    void processKeyEvent(const std::string& keySequence);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Control surface scripting
 */
class MAESTRO_API ControlSurfaceScript {
public:

    ~ControlSurfaceScript();

    };

    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

```lua
-- scripts/examples/auto_harmonize.lua
-- Example Lua script for MaestroStudio

-- Register with the script system
maestro.script.name = "Auto Harmonizer"
maestro.script.version = "1.0"
maestro.script.author = "MaestroStudio"

-- Configuration
local config = {
    interval = 4,  -- Perfect fourth (in semitones)
    velocity_ratio = 0.8,
    enabled = true
}

-- State
local held_notes = {}

-- Called when script is loaded
function on_init()
    maestro.log("Auto Harmonizer initialized")
    
    -- Register MIDI callback
    maestro.midi.on_note_on(function(channel, note, velocity)
        if not config.enabled then return end
        
        -- Store original note
        held_notes[note] = true
        
        -- Play harmony note
        local harmony_note = note + config.interval
        local harmony_velocity = math.floor(velocity * config.velocity_ratio)
        
        if harmony_note <= 127 then
            maestro.midi.send_note_on(channel, harmony_note, harmony_velocity)
        end
    end)
    
    maestro.midi.on_note_off(function(channel, note, velocity)
        if not config.enabled then return end
        
        if held_notes[note] then
            held_notes[note] = nil
            
            local harmony_note = note + config.interval
            if harmony_note <= 127 then
                maestro.midi.send_note_off(channel, harmony_note, 0)
            end
        end
    end)
end

-- Called from UI
function set_interval(semitones)
    config.interval = semitones
    maestro.log("Harmony interval set to " .. semitones .. " semitones")
end

function set_enabled(enabled)
    config.enabled = enabled
    
    -- Release all harmony notes if disabling
    if not enabled then
        for note, _ in pairs(held_notes) do
            local harmony_note = note + config.interval
            if harmony_note <= 127 then
                maestro.midi.send_note_off(0, harmony_note, 0)
            end
        end
        held_notes = {}
    end
end

-- Register UI controls
function on_ui_setup()
    maestro.ui.add_checkbox("enabled", "Enable", config.enabled, set_enabled)
    maestro.ui.add_slider("interval", "Interval (semitones)", 
                          config.interval, -12, 12, set_interval)
    maestro.ui.add_slider("velocity", "Velocity Ratio", 
                          config.velocity_ratio * 100, 0, 100, 
                          function(v) config.velocity_ratio = v / 100 end)
end

-- Cleanup
function on_shutdown()
    set_enabled(false)
    maestro.log("Auto Harmonizer shutdown")
end
```

# PHASE 15: PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATION

```cpp
// include/maestro/core/memory_pool.hpp
#pragma once

#include <cstddef>
#include <vector>
#include <mutex>
#include <atomic>

namespace maestro {

/**
 * @brief Lock-free memory pool for real-time audio
 */
template<typename T, size_t BlockSize = 64>
class LockFreePool {
public:
    LockFreePool(size_t initialCapacity = 1024) {
        resize(initialCapacity);
    }
    
    T* allocate() {
        Node* node = freeList_.load(std::memory_order_acquire);
        
        while (node) {
            if (freeList_.compare_exchange_weak(node, node->next,
                    std::memory_order_release,
                    std::memory_order_relaxed)) {
                return reinterpret_cast<T*>(node->data);
            }
        }
        
        // Pool exhausted - allocate from overflow (not lock-free)
        return new T();
    }
    
    void deallocate(T* ptr) {
        if (!ptr) return;
        
        // Check if this is from our pool
        for (auto& block : blocks_) {
            if (ptr >= reinterpret_cast<T*>(block.data()) &&
                ptr < reinterpret_cast<T*>(block.data() + block.size())) {
                // Return to pool
                Node* node = reinterpret_cast<Node*>(ptr);
                Node* oldHead = freeList_.load(std::memory_order_relaxed);
                do {
                    node->next = oldHead;
                } while (!freeList_.compare_exchange_weak(oldHead, node,
                        std::memory_order_release,
                        std::memory_order_relaxed));
                return;
            }
        }
        
        // Not from our pool - regular delete
        delete ptr;
    }

private:
    struct Node {
        Node* next;
        alignas(T) char data[sizeof(T)];
    };
    
    std::atomic<Node*> freeList_{nullptr};
    std::vector<std::vector<char>> blocks_;
    std::mutex resizeMutex_;
    
    void resize(size_t newCapacity) {
        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(resizeMutex_);
        
        size_t numBlocks = (newCapacity + BlockSize - 1) / BlockSize;
        
        for (size_t b = blocks_.size(); b < numBlocks; ++b) {
            blocks_.emplace_back(BlockSize * sizeof(Node));
            
            // Add nodes to free list
            char* blockData = blocks_.back().data();
            for (size_t i = 0; i < BlockSize; ++i) {
                Node* node = reinterpret_cast<Node*>(
                    blockData + i * sizeof(Node));
                node->next = freeList_.load(std::memory_order_relaxed);
                freeList_.store(node, std::memory_order_release);
            }
        }
    }
};

/**
 * @brief SIMD-optimized audio buffer operations
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioBufferOps {
public:
    // Gain
    static void applyGain(float* buffer, size_t numSamples, float gain);
    static void applyGainRamp(float* buffer, size_t numSamples,
                               float startGain, float endGain);
    
    // Mix
    static void mix(float* dest, const float* src, size_t numSamples);
    static void mixWithGain(float* dest, const float* src, 
                            size_t numSamples, float gain);
    
    // Copy
    static void copy(float* dest, const float* src, size_t numSamples);
    static void copyWithGain(float* dest, const float* src,
                             size_t numSamples, float gain);
    
    // Clear
    static void clear(float* buffer, size_t numSamples);
    
    // Interleave/Deinterleave
    static void interleave(float* dest, const float* const* src,
                           int numChannels, size_t numSamples);
    static void deinterleave(float* const* dest, const float* src,
                             int numChannels, size_t numSamples);
    
    // Peak detection
    static float findPeak(const float* buffer, size_t numSamples);
    static std::pair<float, float> findPeakStereo(const float* left,
                                                   const float* right,
                                                   size_t numSamples);
    
    // RMS
    static float calculateRMS(const float* buffer, size_t numSamples);
    
    // Soft clip
    static void softClip(float* buffer, size_t numSamples, float threshold);
    
    // Convert
    static void floatToInt16(int16_t* dest, const float* src, 
                              size_t numSamples);
    static void int16ToFloat(float* dest, const int16_t* src,
                              size_t numSamples);
    static void floatToInt24(uint8_t* dest, const float* src,
                              size_t numSamples);
    static void floatToInt32(int32_t* dest, const float* src,
                              size_t numSamples);
    
private:
    static bool simdAvailable_;
    static void detectSIMD();
};

/**
 * @brief Real-time safe FIFO queue
 */
template<typename T, size_t Capacity>
class LockFreeFIFO {
public:
    bool push(const T& item) {
        size_t currentWrite = writeIndex_.load(std::memory_order_relaxed);
        size_t nextWrite = (currentWrite + 1) % Capacity;
        
        if (nextWrite == readIndex_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
            return false;  // Queue full
        }
        
        buffer_[currentWrite] = item;
        writeIndex_.store(nextWrite, std::memory_order_release);
        return true;
    }
    
    bool pop(T& item) {
        size_t currentRead = readIndex_.load(std::memory_order_relaxed);
        
        if (currentRead == writeIndex_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
            return false;  // Queue empty
        }
        
        item = buffer_[currentRead];
        readIndex_.store((currentRead + 1) % Capacity, 
                         std::memory_order_release);
        return true;
    }
    
    size_t size() const {
        size_t write = writeIndex_.load(std::memory_order_acquire);
        size_t read = readIndex_.load(std::memory_order_acquire);
        return (write - read + Capacity) % Capacity;
    }
    
    bool empty() const {
        return readIndex_.load(std::memory_order_acquire) ==
               writeIndex_.load(std::memory_order_acquire);
    }
    
    void clear() {
        readIndex_.store(0, std::memory_order_release);
        writeIndex_.store(0, std::memory_order_release);
    }

private:
    std::array<T, Capacity> buffer_;
    std::atomic<size_t> readIndex_{0};
    std::atomic<size_t> writeIndex_{0};
};

/**
 * @brief CPU affinity and priority management
 */
class MAESTRO_API ThreadPriority {
public:
    enum class Priority {
        Normal,
        AboveNormal,
        High,
        RealTime
    };
    
    static void setCurrentThreadPriority(Priority priority);
    static void setThreadAffinity(int coreIndex);
    static int getNumCores();
    
    // Audio thread setup
    static void configureAudioThread();
    
    // Disable denormals
    static void disableDenormals();
};

} // namespace maestro
```

```cpp
// src/core/simd_ops.cpp
#include "maestro/core/memory_pool.hpp"

#if defined(__x86_64__) || defined(_M_X64)
#include <immintrin.h>
#define MAESTRO_HAS_SSE
#define MAESTRO_HAS_AVX
#elif defined(__aarch64__) || defined(_M_ARM64)
#include <arm_neon.h>
#define MAESTRO_HAS_NEON
#endif

namespace maestro {

bool AudioBufferOps::simdAvailable_ = false;

void AudioBufferOps::detectSIMD() {
#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_AVX
    simdAvailable_ = true;
#elif defined(MAESTRO_HAS_NEON)
    simdAvailable_ = true;
#endif
}

void AudioBufferOps::applyGain(float* buffer, size_t numSamples, float gain) {
#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_AVX
    if (simdAvailable_) {
        __m256 gainVec = _mm256_set1_ps(gain);
        size_t i = 0;
        
        // Process 8 samples at a time
        for (; i + 8 <= numSamples; i += 8) {
            __m256 samples = _mm256_loadu_ps(buffer + i);
            samples = _mm256_mul_ps(samples, gainVec);
            _mm256_storeu_ps(buffer + i, samples);
        }
        
        // Handle remaining samples
        for (; i < numSamples; ++i) {
            buffer[i] *= gain;
        }
        return;
    }
#endif

#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_NEON
    if (simdAvailable_) {
        float32x4_t gainVec = vdupq_n_f32(gain);
        size_t i = 0;
        
        // Process 4 samples at a time
        for (; i + 4 <= numSamples; i += 4) {
            float32x4_t samples = vld1q_f32(buffer + i);
            samples = vmulq_f32(samples, gainVec);
            vst1q_f32(buffer + i, samples);
        }
        
        // Handle remaining samples
        for (; i < numSamples; ++i) {
            buffer[i] *= gain;
        }
        return;
    }
#endif

    // Scalar fallback
    for (size_t i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        buffer[i] *= gain;
    }
}

void AudioBufferOps::mix(float* dest, const float* src, size_t numSamples) {
#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_AVX
    if (simdAvailable_) {
        size_t i = 0;
        
        for (; i + 8 <= numSamples; i += 8) {
            __m256 destVec = _mm256_loadu_ps(dest + i);
            __m256 srcVec = _mm256_loadu_ps(src + i);
            destVec = _mm256_add_ps(destVec, srcVec);
            _mm256_storeu_ps(dest + i, destVec);
        }
        
        for (; i < numSamples; ++i) {
            dest[i] += src[i];
        }
        return;
    }
#endif

#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_NEON
    if (simdAvailable_) {
        size_t i = 0;
        
        for (; i + 4 <= numSamples; i += 4) {
            float32x4_t destVec = vld1q_f32(dest + i);
            float32x4_t srcVec = vld1q_f32(src + i);
            destVec = vaddq_f32(destVec, srcVec);
            vst1q_f32(dest + i, destVec);
        }
        
        for (; i < numSamples; ++i) {
            dest[i] += src[i];
        }
        return;
    }
#endif

    // Scalar fallback
    for (size_t i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        dest[i] += src[i];
    }
}

float AudioBufferOps::findPeak(const float* buffer, size_t numSamples) {
#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_AVX
    if (simdAvailable_) {
        __m256 maxVec = _mm256_setzero_ps();
        __m256 signMask = _mm256_set1_ps(-0.0f);
        size_t i = 0;
        
        for (; i + 8 <= numSamples; i += 8) {
            __m256 samples = _mm256_loadu_ps(buffer + i);
            samples = _mm256_andnot_ps(signMask, samples);  // abs
            maxVec = _mm256_max_ps(maxVec, samples);
        }
        
        // Reduce to single value
        __m128 lo = _mm256_castps256_ps128(maxVec);
        __m128 hi = _mm256_extractf128_ps(maxVec, 1);
        lo = _mm_max_ps(lo, hi);
        lo = _mm_max_ps(lo, _mm_shuffle_ps(lo, lo, _MM_SHUFFLE(2, 3, 0, 1)));
        lo = _mm_max_ps(lo, _mm_shuffle_ps(lo, lo, _MM_SHUFFLE(1, 0, 3, 2)));
        
        float peak = _mm_cvtss_f32(lo);
        
        // Check remaining
        for (; i < numSamples; ++i) {
            peak = std::max(peak, std::abs(buffer[i]));
        }
        
        return peak;
    }
#endif

    float peak = 0.0f;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        peak = std::max(peak, std::abs(buffer[i]));
    }
    return peak;
}

void AudioBufferOps::clear(float* buffer, size_t numSamples) {
    std::memset(buffer, 0, numSamples * sizeof(float));
}

void AudioBufferOps::copy(float* dest, const float* src, size_t numSamples) {
    std::memcpy(dest, src, numSamples * sizeof(float));
}

void ThreadPriority::configureAudioThread() {
    setCurrentThreadPriority(Priority::RealTime);
    disableDenormals();
}

void ThreadPriority::disableDenormals() {
#ifdef MAESTRO_HAS_SSE
    _mm_setcsr(_mm_getcsr() | 0x8040);  // DAZ and FTZ
#endif
}

void ThreadPriority::setCurrentThreadPriority(Priority priority) {
#ifdef _WIN32
    int winPriority = THREAD_PRIORITY_NORMAL;
    switch (priority) {
        case Priority::AboveNormal:
            winPriority = THREAD_PRIORITY_ABOVE_NORMAL;
            break;
        case Priority::High:
            winPriority = THREAD_PRIORITY_HIGHEST;
            break;
        case Priority::RealTime:
            winPriority = THREAD_PRIORITY_TIME_CRITICAL;
            break;
        default:
            break;
    }
    SetThreadPriority(GetCurrentThread(), winPriority);
#elif defined(__APPLE__) || defined(__linux__)
    int policy;
    struct sched_param param;
    pthread_getschedparam(pthread_self(), &policy, &param);
    
    switch (priority) {
        case Priority::RealTime:
            policy = SCHED_FIFO;
            param.sched_priority = sched_get_priority_max(SCHED_FIFO);
            break;
        case Priority::High:
            policy = SCHED_FIFO;
            param.sched_priority = sched_get_priority_max(SCHED_FIFO) - 10;
            break;
        default:
            policy = SCHED_OTHER;
            param.sched_priority = 0;
            break;
    }
    
    pthread_setschedparam(pthread_self(), policy, &param);
#endif
}

int ThreadPriority::getNumCores() {
    return std::thread::hardware_concurrency();
}

} // namespace maestro
```

/**
 * @mainpage MaestroStudio API Documentation
 * 
 * @section intro Introduction
 * 
 * MaestroStudio is an enterprise-grade music production suite that provides:
 * - Real-time MIDI processing with hardware instrument integration
 * - Professional audio engine with low-latency processing
 * - Style playback and arrangement features
 * - Multi-pad performance capabilities
 * - Full DAW/Studio functionality
 * - Cross-platform support (Windows, macOS, Linux, iOS, Android)
 * 
 * @section quick_start Quick Start
 * 
 * @code{.cpp}
 * #include <maestro/core/engine.hpp>
 * 
 * int main() {
 *     // Configure the engine
 *     maestro::MaestroEngine::Config config;
 *     config.sampleRate = 44100;
 *     config.bufferSize = 256;
 *     
 *     // Initialize
 *     auto& engine = maestro::MaestroEngine::instance();
 *     if (!engine.initialize(config)) {
 *         std::cerr << "Failed to initialize engine" << std::endl;
 *         return 1;
 *     }
 *     
 *     // Start audio/MIDI processing
 *     engine.start();
 *     
 *     // Access subsystems
 *     auto& midi = engine.midi();
 *     auto& audio = engine.audio();
 *     auto& styles = engine.styles();
 *     
 *     // ... your application code ...
 *     
 *     // Cleanup
 *     engine.stop();
 *     engine.shutdown();
 *     
 *     return 0;
 * }
 * @endcode
 * 
 * @section modules Modules
 * 
 * - @ref maestro::MaestroEngine "Core Engine" - Main engine coordinator
 * - @ref maestro::AudioEngine "Audio Engine" - Audio I/O and processing
 * - @ref maestro::MidiEngine "MIDI Engine" - MIDI I/O and routing
 * - @ref maestro::StyleEngine "Style Engine" - Style playback
 * - @ref maestro::VoiceEngine "Voice Engine" - Sound generation
 * - @ref maestro::PadEngine "Pad Engine" - Performance pads
 * - @ref maestro::studio "Studio" - DAW features
 * 
 * @section building Building
 * 
 * @subsection build_deps Dependencies
 * - CMake 3.20+
 * - C++20 compiler
 * - Qt 6.5+
 * - RtAudio, RtMidi
 * 
 * @subsection build_cmd Build Commands
 * @code{.bash}
 * mkdir build && cd build
 * cmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release
 * cmake --build .
 * @endcode
 */

```yaml
# deploy/docker/Dockerfile
FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder

RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
    build-essential \
    cmake \
    ninja-build \
    git \
    libgl1-mesa-dev \
    libasound2-dev \
    libjack-jackd2-dev \
    libpulse-dev \
    qt6-base-dev \
    qt6-multimedia-dev

WORKDIR /app
COPY . .

RUN cmake -B build -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
    -DMAESTRO_BUILD_TESTS=OFF
RUN cmake --build build

# Runtime image
FROM ubuntu:22.04

RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
    libasound2 \
    libjack-jackd2-0 \
    libpulse0 \
    libqt6core6 \
    libqt6gui6 \
    libqt6widgets6 \
    libqt6multimedia6

COPY --from=builder /app/build/MaestroStudio /usr/local/bin/
COPY --from=builder /app/resources /usr/local/share/maestro/

ENTRYPOINT ["MaestroStudio"]
```

# PHASE 3.1: MACHINE LEARNING FOR MUSIC GENERATION

## ML Core Framework

```cpp
// include/maestro/ml/ml_engine.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <functional>
#include <future>

namespace maestro::ml {

/**
 * @brief Tensor representation for ML operations
 */
class MAESTRO_API Tensor {
public:
    enum class DataType { Float32, Float16, Int32, Int64 };
    
    Tensor();
    Tensor(const std::vector<int64_t>& shape, DataType dtype = DataType::Float32);
    Tensor(const Tensor& other);
    Tensor(Tensor&& other) noexcept;
    ~Tensor();
    
    Tensor& operator=(const Tensor& other);
    Tensor& operator=(Tensor&& other) noexcept;
    
    // Shape and size
    const std::vector<int64_t>& shape() const { return shape_; }
    int64_t size() const;
    int64_t numDimensions() const { return shape_.size(); }
    DataType dataType() const { return dtype_; }
    
    // Data access
    float* data();
    const float* data() const;
    float& at(const std::vector<int64_t>& indices);
    const float& at(const std::vector<int64_t>& indices) const;
    
    // Operations
    Tensor reshape(const std::vector<int64_t>& newShape) const;
    Tensor transpose(const std::vector<int64_t>& axes) const;
    Tensor slice(int64_t dim, int64_t start, int64_t end) const;
    
    // Factory methods
    static Tensor zeros(const std::vector<int64_t>& shape);
    static Tensor ones(const std::vector<int64_t>& shape);
    static Tensor random(const std::vector<int64_t>& shape, float min = 0.0f, 
                         float max = 1.0f);
    
    // Serialization
    std::vector<uint8_t> serialize() const;
    static Tensor deserialize(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data);

private:
    std::vector<int64_t> shape_;
    DataType dtype_;
    std::vector<float> data_;
};

/**
 * @brief ML Model base class
 */
class MAESTRO_API MLModel {
public:
    virtual ~MLModel() = default;
    
    // Model info
    virtual std::string getName() const = 0;
    virtual std::string getVersion() const = 0;
    virtual std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::vector<int64_t>>> 
        getInputShapes() const = 0;
    virtual std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::vector<int64_t>>> 
        getOutputShapes() const = 0;
    
    // Inference
    virtual std::vector<Tensor> forward(const std::vector<Tensor>& inputs) = 0;
    
    // Loading
    virtual Result<void> load(const std::string& path) = 0;
    virtual Result<void> loadFromMemory(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data) = 0;
    
    // Device
    enum class Device { CPU, CUDA, Metal, DirectML };
    virtual void setDevice(Device device) = 0;
    virtual Device getDevice() const = 0;
    
    // Optimization
    virtual void optimize() = 0;
    virtual void quantize(int bits = 8) = 0;
};

/**
 * @brief ONNX Runtime model wrapper
 */
class MAESTRO_API ONNXModel : public MLModel {
public:
    ONNXModel();
    ~ONNXModel();
    
    std::string getName() const override;
    std::string getVersion() const override;
    std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::vector<int64_t>>> 
        getInputShapes() const override;
    std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::vector<int64_t>>> 
        getOutputShapes() const override;
    
    std::vector<Tensor> forward(const std::vector<Tensor>& inputs) override;
    
    Result<void> load(const std::string& path) override;
    Result<void> loadFromMemory(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data) override;
    
    void setDevice(Device device) override;
    Device getDevice() const override;
    
    void optimize() override;
    void quantize(int bits = 8) override;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief TensorFlow Lite model wrapper
 */
class MAESTRO_API TFLiteModel : public MLModel {
public:
    TFLiteModel();
    ~TFLiteModel();
    
    std::string getName() const override;
    std::string getVersion() const override;
    std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::vector<int64_t>>> 
        getInputShapes() const override;
    std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::vector<int64_t>>> 
        getOutputShapes() const override;
    
    std::vector<Tensor> forward(const std::vector<Tensor>& inputs) override;
    
    Result<void> load(const std::string& path) override;
    Result<void> loadFromMemory(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data) override;
    
    void setDevice(Device device) override;
    Device getDevice() const override;
    
    void optimize() override;
    void quantize(int bits = 8) override;
    
    // TFLite specific
    void setNumThreads(int threads);
    void enableXNNPACK(bool enable);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief ML Engine - manages models and inference
 */
class MAESTRO_API MLEngine {
public:
    static MLEngine& instance();
    
    // Initialization
    Result<void> initialize();
    void shutdown();
    
    // Device detection
    struct DeviceInfo {
        MLModel::Device type;
        std::string name;
        size_t memoryMB;
        bool available;
    };
    std::vector<DeviceInfo> getAvailableDevices() const;
    void setDefaultDevice(MLModel::Device device);
    
    // Model management
    std::shared_ptr<MLModel> loadModel(const std::string& path);
    std::shared_ptr<MLModel> getModel(const std::string& name);
    void unloadModel(const std::string& name);
    
    // Async inference
    std::future<std::vector<Tensor>> inferAsync(
        std::shared_ptr<MLModel> model,
        const std::vector<Tensor>& inputs);
    
    // Batch inference
    std::vector<std::vector<Tensor>> inferBatch(
        std::shared_ptr<MLModel> model,
        const std::vector<std::vector<Tensor>>& batchInputs);
    
    // Model caching
    void setCacheDirectory(const std::string& path);
    void clearCache();

private:
    MLEngine();
    ~MLEngine();
    
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::ml
