## Chord Generation

```cpp
// include/maestro/ml/chord_generator.hpp
#pragma once

#include "ml_engine.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include "maestro/style/style_engine.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <memory>

namespace maestro::ml {

/**
 * @brief AI-powered chord progression generator
 */
class MAESTRO_API ChordGenerator {
public:
    ChordGenerator();
    ~ChordGenerator();
    
    // Initialization
    Result<void> loadModel(const std::string& modelPath);
    bool isReady() const;
    
    // Generation settings
    struct GenerationConfig {
        // Musical parameters
        std::string key = "C";           // Root key (C, D, E, etc.)
        std::string mode = "major";      // major, minor, dorian, etc.
        int numChords = 8;               // Number of chords to generate
        int beatsPerChord = 4;           // Duration of each chord
        
        // Style hints
        std::string genre = "pop";       // pop, jazz, classical, etc.
        float complexity = 0.5f;         // 0-1, chord complexity
        float tension = 0.5f;            // 0-1, harmonic tension
        float repetition = 0.3f;         // 0-1, pattern repetition
        
        // Generation parameters
        float temperature = 0.8f;        // Randomness (0.1-2.0)
        int topK = 10;                   // Top-k sampling
        float topP = 0.9f;               // Nucleus sampling threshold
        
        // Constraints
        bool avoidChord = false;
        std::vector<ChordInfo> avoidChords;
        bool forceStart = false;
        ChordInfo startChord;
        bool forceEnd = false;
        ChordInfo endChord;
    };
    
    // Generate chord progression
    std::vector<ChordInfo> generate(const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Continue from existing progression
    std::vector<ChordInfo> continueProgression(
        const std::vector<ChordInfo>& existing,
        int numNewChords,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Harmonize melody
    std::vector<ChordInfo> harmonizeMelody(
        const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& melody,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Reharmonize existing progression
    std::vector<ChordInfo> reharmonize(
        const std::vector<ChordInfo>& original,
        float creativity = 0.5f);
    
    // Suggest next chord
    struct ChordSuggestion {
        ChordInfo chord;
        float probability;
        std::string explanation;
    };
    std::vector<ChordSuggestion> suggestNextChord(
        const std::vector<ChordInfo>& context,
        int numSuggestions = 5);
    
    // Analyze progression
    struct ProgressionAnalysis {
        std::string key;
        std::string mode;
        std::vector<std::string> romanNumerals;
        std::vector<std::string> functions;  // T, S, D (tonic, subdominant, dominant)
        float complexity;
        float tension;
        std::vector<std::string> commonGenres;
    };
    ProgressionAnalysis analyzeProgression(const std::vector<ChordInfo>& chords);
    
    // Training (for custom models)
    struct TrainingConfig {
        std::string dataPath;
        int epochs = 100;
        float learningRate = 0.001f;
        int batchSize = 32;
        std::string outputPath;
    };
    Result<void> trainCustomModel(const TrainingConfig& config,
        std::function<void(int epoch, float loss)> callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Real-time chord suggestion during performance
 */
class MAESTRO_API LiveChordAssistant {
public:
    LiveChordAssistant(ChordGenerator& generator);
    ~LiveChordAssistant();
    
    // Start/stop
    void start();
    void stop();
    bool isRunning() const;
    
    // Input current chord
    void setCurrentChord(const ChordInfo& chord);
    
    // Get suggestions (call periodically for UI update)
    std::vector<ChordGenerator::ChordSuggestion> getSuggestions() const;
    
    // Callbacks
    using SuggestionCallback = std::function<void(
        const std::vector<ChordGenerator::ChordSuggestion>&)>;
    void setSuggestionCallback(SuggestionCallback callback);
    
    // Settings
    void setLookahead(int numChords);
    void setGenre(const std::string& genre);
    void setCreativity(float level);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::ml
```

## Melody Generation

```cpp
// include/maestro/ml/melody_generator.hpp
#pragma once

#include "ml_engine.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <memory>

namespace maestro::ml {

/**
 * @brief AI-powered melody generator
 */
class MAESTRO_API MelodyGenerator {
public:
    MelodyGenerator();
    ~MelodyGenerator();
    
    // Initialization
    Result<void> loadModel(const std::string& modelPath);
    bool isReady() const;
    
    // Generation settings
    struct GenerationConfig {
        // Musical parameters
        std::string key = "C";
        std::string scale = "major";
        int numBars = 4;
        TimeSignature timeSignature = {4, 4};
        double tempo = 120.0;
        
        // Melodic characteristics
        float density = 0.5f;            // Note density (0-1)
        float range = 0.5f;              // Pitch range usage (0-1)
        float stepwise = 0.7f;           // Preference for stepwise motion
        float rhythmicVariety = 0.5f;    // Rhythmic complexity
        
        // Expression
        float velocityVariation = 0.3f;
        float articulationVariety = 0.3f;
        
        // Style
        std::string style = "classical";  // classical, jazz, pop, etc.
        float repetition = 0.4f;         // Motif repetition
        
        // Generation parameters
        float temperature = 0.9f;
        int topK = 20;
        float topP = 0.95f;
        
        // Range constraints
        MidiNote lowestNote = 48;        // C3
        MidiNote highestNote = 84;       // C6
    };
    
    // Generate melody
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> generate(const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Generate with chord progression
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> generateWithChords(
        const std::vector<ChordInfo>& chords,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Continue existing melody
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> continueMelody(
        const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& existing,
        int numBars,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Generate variation
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> generateVariation(
        const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& original,
        float variation = 0.5f);
    
    // Generate countermelody
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> generateCountermelody(
        const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& mainMelody,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Generate bass line
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> generateBassLine(
        const std::vector<ChordInfo>& chords,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Motif-based generation
    struct Motif {
        std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> notes;
        std::string name;
    };
    
    Motif extractMotif(const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& melody,
                       TickCount start, TickCount length);
    
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> developMotif(
        const Motif& motif,
        int numBars,
        const GenerationConfig& config);
    
    // Real-time generation
    struct RealTimeConfig {
        int lookbackBars = 2;
        int generateAheadBeats = 4;
        float humanization = 0.2f;
    };
    
    void startRealTimeGeneration(const RealTimeConfig& config);
    void stopRealTimeGeneration();
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> getNextEvents(TickCount currentTick);
    void feedInput(const midi::NoteEvent& event);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};
```

## ML Implementation

```cpp
// src/ml/melody_generator.cpp
#include "maestro/ml/melody_generator.hpp"
#include "maestro/ml/ml_engine.hpp"
#include <random>
#include <algorithm>
#include <cmath>

namespace maestro::ml {

class MelodyGenerator::Impl {
public:
    std::shared_ptr<MLModel> model;
    std::shared_ptr<MLModel> encoderModel;
    bool ready = false;
    
    // Tokenization
    struct Token {
        enum Type { NOTE_ON, NOTE_OFF, TIME_SHIFT, VELOCITY, REST };
        Type type;
        int value;
    };
    
    std::vector<Token> tokenizeMelody(const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& notes) {
        std::vector<Token> tokens;
        
        // Sort by start time
        auto sorted = notes;
        std::sort(sorted.begin(), sorted.end(), 
            [](const auto& a, const auto& b) { return a.startTick < b.startTick; });
        
        TickCount currentTick = 0;
        
        for (const auto& note : sorted) {
            // Time shift
            if (note.startTick > currentTick) {
                TickCount shift = note.startTick - currentTick;
                while (shift > 0) {
                    int shiftAmount = std::min(static_cast<int>(shift), 100);
                    tokens.push_back({Token::TIME_SHIFT, shiftAmount});
                    shift -= shiftAmount;
                }
                currentTick = note.startTick;
            }
            
            // Velocity
            tokens.push_back({Token::VELOCITY, note.velocity / 4}); // 0-31
            
            // Note on
            tokens.push_back({Token::NOTE_ON, note.note});
            
            // Time shift for duration
            TickCount duration = note.duration;
            while (duration > 0) {
                int shiftAmount = std::min(static_cast<int>(duration), 100);
                tokens.push_back({Token::TIME_SHIFT, shiftAmount});
                duration -= shiftAmount;
            }
            currentTick += note.duration;
            
            // Note off
            tokens.push_back({Token::NOTE_OFF, note.note});
        }
        
        return tokens;
    }
    
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> detokenize(const std::vector<Token>& tokens) {
        std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> notes;
        std::map<int, std::pair<TickCount, MidiVelocity>> activeNotes;
        
        TickCount currentTick = 0;
        MidiVelocity currentVelocity = 100;
        
        for (const auto& token : tokens) {
            switch (token.type) {
                case Token::TIME_SHIFT:
                    currentTick += token.value;
                    break;
                    
                case Token::VELOCITY:
                    currentVelocity = token.value * 4;
                    break;
                    
                case Token::NOTE_ON:
                    activeNotes[token.value] = {currentTick, currentVelocity};
                    break;
                    
                case Token::NOTE_OFF:
                    if (activeNotes.count(token.value)) {
                        auto& [startTick, velocity] = activeNotes[token.value];
                        midi::NoteEvent event;
                        event.note = token.value;
                        event.velocity = velocity;
                        event.startTick = startTick;
                        event.duration = currentTick - startTick;
                        event.channel = 0;
                        notes.push_back(event);
                        activeNotes.erase(token.value);
                    }
                    break;
                    
                default:
                    break;
            }
        }
        
        return notes;
    }
    
    Tensor tokensToTensor(const std::vector<Token>& tokens, int maxLen) {
        Tensor tensor({1, maxLen, 2});  // [batch, seq, features]
        float* data = tensor.data();
        
        for (int i = 0; i < maxLen && i < static_cast<int>(tokens.size()); ++i) {
            data[i * 2] = static_cast<float>(tokens[i].type);
            data[i * 2 + 1] = static_cast<float>(tokens[i].value);
        }
        
        // Pad remaining
        for (int i = tokens.size(); i < maxLen; ++i) {
            data[i * 2] = 0.0f;
            data[i * 2 + 1] = 0.0f;
        }
        
        return tensor;
    }
    
    std::vector<Token> sampleFromLogits(const Tensor& logits, 
                                         float temperature,
                                         int topK,
                                         float topP) {
        std::vector<Token> result;
        const float* data = logits.data();
        int vocabSize = logits.shape()[2];
        
        std::random_device rd;
        std::mt19937 gen(rd());
        
        for (int t = 0; t < logits.shape()[1]; ++t) {
            std::vector<std::pair<float, int>> probs;
            
            // Apply temperature and compute softmax
            float maxLogit = *std::max_element(
                data + t * vocabSize, 
                data + (t + 1) * vocabSize);
            
            float sumExp = 0.0f;
            for (int i = 0; i < vocabSize; ++i) {
                float p = std::exp((data[t * vocabSize + i] - maxLogit) / temperature);
                probs.push_back({p, i});
                sumExp += p;
            }
            
            // Normalize
            for (auto& p : probs) {
                p.first /= sumExp;
            }
            
            // Sort by probability
            std::sort(probs.begin(), probs.end(), std::greater<>());
            
            // Top-K filtering
            if (topK > 0 && topK < vocabSize) {
                probs.resize(topK);
            }
            
            // Top-P (nucleus) filtering
            float cumSum = 0.0f;
            int cutoff = probs.size();
            for (int i = 0; i < static_cast<int>(probs.size()); ++i) {
                cumSum += probs[i].first;
                if (cumSum > topP) {
                    cutoff = i + 1;
                    break;
                }
            }
            probs.resize(cutoff);
            
            // Re-normalize
            sumExp = 0.0f;
            for (const auto& p : probs) sumExp += p.first;
            for (auto& p : probs) p.first /= sumExp;
            
            // Sample
            std::uniform_real_distribution<float> dist(0.0f, 1.0f);
            float r = dist(gen);
            cumSum = 0.0f;
            int selected = probs[0].second;
            for (const auto& p : probs) {
                cumSum += p.first;
                if (r < cumSum) {
                    selected = p.second;
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            // Decode token
            Token token;
            token.type = static_cast<Token::Type>(selected / 128);
            token.value = selected % 128;
            result.push_back(token);
            
            // Check for end token
            if (token.type == Token::REST && token.value == 0) {
                break;
            }
        }
        
        return result;
    }
    
    MidiNote constrainToScale(MidiNote note, const std::string& key, 
                               const std::string& scale) {
        // Scale intervals
        std::map<std::string, std::vector<int>> scales = {
            {"major", {0, 2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 11}},
            {"minor", {0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 8, 10}},
            {"dorian", {0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 9, 10}},
            {"mixolydian", {0, 2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 10}},
            {"pentatonic", {0, 2, 4, 7, 9}},
            {"blues", {0, 3, 5, 6, 7, 10}}
        };
        
        // Key offsets
        std::map<std::string, int> keys = {
            {"C", 0}, {"C#", 1}, {"Db", 1}, {"D", 2}, {"D#", 3}, {"Eb", 3},
            {"E", 4}, {"F", 5}, {"F#", 6}, {"Gb", 6}, {"G", 7}, {"G#", 8},
            {"Ab", 8}, {"A", 9}, {"A#", 10}, {"Bb", 10}, {"B", 11}
        };
        
        int keyOffset = keys.count(key) ? keys[key] : 0;
        const auto& scaleNotes = scales.count(scale) ? scales[scale] : scales["major"];
        
        int noteInOctave = (note - keyOffset + 12) % 12;
        int octave = (note - keyOffset) / 12;
        
        // Find closest scale note
        int minDist = 12;
        int closestScaleNote = 0;
        for (int sn : scaleNotes) {
            int dist = std::abs(noteInOctave - sn);
            if (dist < minDist) {
                minDist = dist;
                closestScaleNote = sn;
            }
        }
        
        return octave * 12 + closestScaleNote + keyOffset;
    }
};

MelodyGenerator::MelodyGenerator() : impl_(std::make_unique<Impl>()) {}
MelodyGenerator::~MelodyGenerator() = default;

Result<void> MelodyGenerator::loadModel(const std::string& modelPath) {
    try {
        impl_->model = MLEngine::instance().loadModel(modelPath);
        if (!impl_->model) {
            return Result<void>("Failed to load melody model");
        }
        impl_->ready = true;
        return Result<void>();
    } catch (const std::exception& e) {
        return Result<void>(std::string("Model loading error: ") + e.what());
    }
}

bool MelodyGenerator::isReady() const {
    return impl_->ready;
}

std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> MelodyGenerator::generate(const GenerationConfig& config) {
    if (!impl_->ready) {
        return {};
    }
    
    // Create conditioning tensor
    Tensor conditioning({1, 10});
    float* condData = conditioning.data();
    
    // Encode parameters
    condData[0] = config.density;
    condData[1] = config.range;
    condData[2] = config.stepwise;
    condData[3] = config.rhythmicVariety;
    condData[4] = static_cast<float>(config.lowestNote) / 127.0f;
    condData[5] = static_cast<float>(config.highestNote) / 127.0f;
    condData[6] = config.tempo / 200.0f;
    condData[7] = config.temperature;
    condData[8] = config.velocityVariation;
    condData[9] = config.repetition;
    
    // Generate
    int maxTokens = config.numBars * config.timeSignature.numerator * 16;  // 16th note resolution
    Tensor startToken({1, 1, 2});
    startToken.data()[0] = 0.0f;  // START token
    startToken.data()[1] = 0.0f;
    
    std::vector<Tensor> inputs = {startToken, conditioning};
    auto outputs = impl_->model->forward(inputs);
    
    // Sample from output
    auto tokens = impl_->sampleFromLogits(
        outputs[0], 
        config.temperature,
        config.topK,
        config.topP);
    
    // Convert to notes
    auto notes = impl_->detokenize(tokens);
    
    // Post-process: constrain to scale
    for (auto& note : notes) {
        note.note = impl_->constrainToScale(note.note, config.key, config.scale);
        
        // Constrain to range
        while (note.note < config.lowestNote) note.note += 12;
        while (note.note > config.highestNote) note.note -= 12;
    }
    
    return notes;
}

std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> MelodyGenerator::generateWithChords(
    const std::vector<ChordInfo>& chords,
    const GenerationConfig& config) {
    
    if (!impl_->ready || chords.empty()) {
        return {};
    }
    
    // Encode chord progression
    Tensor chordTensor({1, static_cast<int64_t>(chords.size()), 12});
    float* chordData = chordTensor.data();
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < chords.size(); ++i) {
        auto notes = chords[i].getNotes();
        for (MidiNote n : notes) {
            int pitch = n % 12;
            chordData[i * 12 + pitch] = 1.0f;
        }
    }
    
    // Create conditioning with chord info
    Tensor conditioning({1, 10 + static_cast<int64_t>(chords.size()) * 12});
    // ... fill conditioning ...
    
    std::vector<Tensor> inputs = {Tensor::zeros({1, 1, 2}), conditioning, chordTensor};
    auto outputs = impl_->model->forward(inputs);
    
    auto tokens = impl_->sampleFromLogits(outputs[0], config.temperature, 
                                           config.topK, config.topP);
    return impl_->detokenize(tokens);
}

std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> MelodyGenerator::continueMelody(
    const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& existing,
    int numBars,
    const GenerationConfig& config) {
    
    if (!impl_->ready || existing.empty()) {
        return {};
    }
    
    // Tokenize existing melody
    auto existingTokens = impl_->tokenizeMelody(existing);
    
    // Prepare context tensor
    int maxContext = 512;
    int contextLen = std::min(static_cast<int>(existingTokens.size()), maxContext);
    
    std::vector<Impl::Token> context(
        existingTokens.end() - contextLen,
        existingTokens.end());
    
    Tensor contextTensor = impl_->tokensToTensor(context, maxContext);
    
    // Generate continuation
    Tensor conditioning({1, 10});
    // ... fill with config parameters ...
    
    std::vector<Tensor> inputs = {contextTensor, conditioning};
    auto outputs = impl_->model->forward(inputs);
    
    auto newTokens = impl_->sampleFromLogits(outputs[0], config.temperature,
                                              config.topK, config.topP);
    
    // Combine and convert
    context.insert(context.end(), newTokens.begin(), newTokens.end());
    return impl_->detokenize(newTokens);
}

std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> MelodyGenerator::generateVariation(
    const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& original,
    float variation) {
    
    if (!impl_->ready || original.empty()) {
        return original;
    }
    
    auto tokens = impl_->tokenizeMelody(original);
    Tensor inputTensor = impl_->tokensToTensor(tokens, 512);
    
    // Variation amount tensor
    Tensor varTensor({1, 1});
    varTensor.data()[0] = variation;
    
    std::vector<Tensor> inputs = {inputTensor, varTensor};
    auto outputs = impl_->model->forward(inputs);
    
    // Interpolate between original and generated
    // based on variation amount
    auto generated = impl_->sampleFromLogits(outputs[0], 0.8f, 10, 0.9f);
    
    return impl_->detokenize(generated);
}

std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> MelodyGenerator::generateCountermelody(
    const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& mainMelody,
    const GenerationConfig& config) {
    
    if (!impl_->ready || mainMelody.empty()) {
        return {};
    }
    
    // Analyze main melody
    auto tokens = impl_->tokenizeMelody(mainMelody);
    Tensor melodyTensor = impl_->tokensToTensor(tokens, 512);
    
    // Countermelody conditioning
    Tensor conditioning({1, 12});
    float* cond = conditioning.data();
    cond[0] = config.density;
    cond[1] = config.range;
    cond[2] = 0.3f;  // Lower stepwise for counter
    cond[3] = 0.5f;  // Counter-rhythmic
    cond[4] = static_cast<float>(config.lowestNote) / 127.0f;
    cond[5] = static_cast<float>(config.highestNote) / 127.0f;
    cond[6] = config.tempo / 200.0f;
    cond[7] = 1.0f;  // Counter flag
    // ... more conditioning ...
    
    std::vector<Tensor> inputs = {melodyTensor, conditioning};
    auto outputs = impl_->model->forward(inputs);
    
    auto counterTokens = impl_->sampleFromLogits(outputs[0], config.temperature,
                                                  config.topK, config.topP);
    
    auto counterMelody = impl_->detokenize(counterTokens);
    
    // Post-process to avoid unisons with main melody
    for (auto& note : counterMelody) {
        for (const auto& mainNote : mainMelody) {
            if (note.startTick >= mainNote.startTick &&
                note.startTick < mainNote.startTick + mainNote.duration) {
                // Check for unison/octave
                int interval = std::abs(note.note - mainNote.note) % 12;
                if (interval == 0) {
                    // Shift by third
                    note.note += (note.note > mainNote.note) ? 4 : -3;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    return counterMelody;
}

std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> MelodyGenerator::generateBassLine(
    const std::vector<ChordInfo>& chords,
    const GenerationConfig& config) {
    
    std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> bassLine;
    TickCount ppqn = 480;
    TickCount currentTick = 0;
    
    std::random_device rd;
    std::mt19937 gen(rd());
    std::uniform_real_distribution<float> dist(0.0f, 1.0f);
    
    for (const auto& chord : chords) {
        TickCount chordDuration = ppqn * 4;  // 1 bar
        
        // Root note
        MidiNote root = chord.root;
        while (root >= config.lowestNote + 12) root -= 12;
        while (root < config.lowestNote) root += 12;
        
        // Different patterns based on complexity
        if (config.density < 0.3f) {
            // Whole notes
            midi::NoteEvent event;
            event.note = root;
            event.velocity = 100;
            event.startTick = currentTick;
            event.duration = chordDuration;
            event.channel = 0;
            bassLine.push_back(event);
        } else if (config.density < 0.6f) {
            // Half notes with fifth
            std::vector<int> notes = {root, root + 7};  // root, fifth
            for (int i = 0; i < 2; ++i) {
                midi::NoteEvent event;
                event.note = notes[i % 2];
                event.velocity = i == 0 ? 100 : 85;
                event.startTick = currentTick + i * chordDuration / 2;
                event.duration = chordDuration / 2 - ppqn / 8;
                event.channel = 0;
                bassLine.push_back(event);
            }
        } else {
            // Walking bass
            auto chordNotes = chord.getNotes();
            std::vector<int> walkingNotes;
            walkingNotes.push_back(root);
            
            for (int i = 1; i < 4; ++i) {
                if (dist(gen) < 0.6f && !chordNotes.empty()) {
                    // Chord tone
                    MidiNote ct = chordNotes[i % chordNotes.size()];
                    while (ct >= root + 12) ct -= 12;
                    walkingNotes.push_back(ct);
                } else {
                    // Passing/chromatic tone
                    int lastNote = walkingNotes.back();
                    int nextRoot = root;  // Will be updated for next chord
                    int direction = (nextRoot > lastNote) ? 1 : -1;
                    walkingNotes.push_back(lastNote + direction);
                }
            }
            
            for (int i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
                midi::NoteEvent event;
                event.note = walkingNotes[i];
                event.velocity = (i == 0) ? 100 : 85;
                event.startTick = currentTick + i * ppqn;
                event.duration = ppqn - ppqn / 8;
                event.channel = 0;
                bassLine.push_back(event);
            }
        }
        
        currentTick += chordDuration;
    }
    
    return bassLine;
}

} // namespace maestro::ml
```

```cpp
// include/maestro/cloud/cloud_library.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <functional>
#include <future>

namespace maestro::cloud {

/**
 * @brief Sound/sample metadata
 */
struct SoundAsset {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string description;
    std::string category;
    std::vector<std::string> tags;
    std::string author;
    std::string license;
    
    // Technical info
    enum class Type { 
        Sample, 
        SoundFont, 
        Preset, 
        Style, 
        MidiFile,
        Loop,
        OneShot,
        Multisample,
        IRResponse
    };
    Type type;
    
    uint64_t sizeBytes;
    double durationSeconds;
    SampleRate sampleRate;
    int channels;
    int bitDepth;
    
    // BPM/key for loops
    double bpm;
    std::string musicalKey;
    
    // Quality and ratings
    float rating;
    int downloadCount;
    bool premium;
    double priceUSD;
    
    // URLs
    std::string previewUrl;
    std::string downloadUrl;
    std::string thumbnailUrl;
    
    // Timestamps
    std::string createdAt;
    std::string updatedAt;
};

/**
 * @brief Sound pack/collection
 */
struct SoundPack {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string description;
    std::string author;
    std::string thumbnailUrl;
    
    std::vector<std::string> assetIds;
    uint64_t totalSizeBytes;
    int assetCount;
    
    bool premium;
    double priceUSD;
    bool owned;
    bool downloaded;
    
    std::vector<std::string> genres;
    std::vector<std::string> instruments;
};

/**
 * @brief Search/filter parameters
 */
struct SearchParams {
    std::string query;
    std::vector<SoundAsset::Type> types;
    std::vector<std::string> categories;
    std::vector<std::string> tags;
    
    // Range filters
    double minDuration = 0.0;
    double maxDuration = 0.0;
    double minBpm = 0.0;
    double maxBpm = 0.0;
    std::string key;
    
    // Quality filters
    float minRating = 0.0f;
    bool freeOnly = false;
    bool includeOwned = true;
    bool includeDownloaded = true;
    
    // Sorting
    enum class SortBy { Relevance, Date, Rating, Downloads, Name };
    SortBy sortBy = SortBy::Relevance;
    bool sortDescending = true;
    
    // Pagination
    int offset = 0;
    int limit = 50;
};

/**
 * @brief Search results
 */
struct SearchResults {
    std::vector<SoundAsset> assets;
    int totalCount;
    int offset;
    bool hasMore;
    std::string nextPageToken;
};

/**
 * @brief Download progress
 */
struct DownloadProgress {
    std::string assetId;
    uint64_t bytesDownloaded;
    uint64_t totalBytes;
    float progress;           // 0-1
    double speedBytesPerSec;
    double estimatedSecondsRemaining;
    
    enum class Status { 
        Queued, 
        Downloading, 
        Processing, 
        Completed, 
        Failed, 
        Cancelled 
    };
    Status status;
    std::string errorMessage;
};

/**
 * @brief User library state
 */
struct UserLibrary {
    std::vector<std::string> ownedPacks;
    std::vector<std::string> downloadedAssets;
    std::vector<std::string> favorites;
    std::vector<std::string> recentlyUsed;
    
    uint64_t totalDownloadedBytes;
    uint64_t storageQuotaBytes;
    uint64_t usedQuotaBytes;
};

/**
 * @brief Cloud Sound Library client
 */
class MAESTRO_API CloudLibrary {
public:
    CloudLibrary();
    ~CloudLibrary();
    
    // Authentication
    struct AuthCredentials {
        std::string email;
        std::string password;
    };
    
    struct AuthToken {
        std::string accessToken;
        std::string refreshToken;
        int64_t expiresAt;
    };
    
    std::future<Result<AuthToken>> login(const AuthCredentials& creds);
    std::future<Result<AuthToken>> loginWithOAuth(const std::string& provider);
    void logout();
    bool isAuthenticated() const;
    std::string getCurrentUserId() const;
    
    // Token management
    void setAuthToken(const AuthToken& token);
    AuthToken getAuthToken() const;
    std::future<Result<AuthToken>> refreshToken();
    
    // Browsing
    std::future<SearchResults> search(const SearchParams& params);
    std::future<Result<SoundAsset>> getAsset(const std::string& id);
    std::future<Result<SoundPack>> getPack(const std::string& id);
    
    // Categories and tags
    std::future<std::vector<std::string>> getCategories();
    std::future<std::vector<std::string>> getPopularTags(int limit = 50);
    std::future<std::vector<SoundPack>> getFeaturedPacks();
    std::future<std::vector<SoundAsset>> getRecommendations(int limit = 20);
    
    // Downloads
    std::future<Result<std::string>> downloadAsset(
        const std::string& assetId,
        const std::string& localPath);
    std::future<Result<std::string>> downloadPack(
        const std::string& packId,
        const std::string& localDir);
    
    void pauseDownload(const std::string& assetId);
    void resumeDownload(const std::string& assetId);
    void cancelDownload(const std::string& assetId);
    
    std::vector<DownloadProgress> getActiveDownloads() const;
    DownloadProgress getDownloadProgress(const std::string& assetId) const;
    
    // Download callbacks
    using ProgressCallback = std::function<void(const DownloadProgress&)>;
    void setProgressCallback(ProgressCallback callback);
    
    // Local library
    UserLibrary getUserLibrary() const;
    std::vector<SoundAsset> getDownloadedAssets() const;
    std::vector<SoundAsset> getFavorites() const;
    
    void addToFavorites(const std::string& assetId);
    void removeFromFavorites(const std::string& assetId);
    
    // Purchases
    std::future<Result<void>> purchasePack(const std::string& packId);
    std::future<Result<void>> purchaseAsset(const std::string& assetId);
    std::future<std::vector<SoundPack>> getPurchasedPacks();
    
    // Uploads (for content creators)
    struct UploadParams {
        std::string filePath;
        SoundAsset metadata;
        bool makePublic = true;
    };
    std::future<Result<std::string>> uploadAsset(const UploadParams& params);
    
    // Streaming preview
    std::future<Result<std::vector<float>>> streamPreview(
        const std::string& assetId,
        double startSeconds = 0.0,
        double durationSeconds = 30.0);
    
    // Cache management
    void setCacheDirectory(const std::string& path);
    void setCacheMaxSize(uint64_t bytes);
    void clearCache();
    uint64_t getCacheSize() const;
    
    // Offline mode
    void setOfflineMode(bool offline);
    bool isOfflineMode() const;
    std::vector<SoundAsset> getOfflineAvailable() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Local sound library indexer
 */
class MAESTRO_API LocalLibraryIndex {
public:
    LocalLibraryIndex();
    ~LocalLibraryIndex();
    
    // Indexing
    void addSearchPath(const std::string& path);
    void removeSearchPath(const std::string& path);

    void startIndexing();

    // Search

    // Quick access

    std::vector<SoundAsset> getByCategory(const std::string& category) const;
    std::vector<SoundAsset> getByInstrument(const std::string& instrument) const;
    
    // Auto-tagging with ML
    void enableAutoTagging(bool enable);
    std::future<std::vector<std::string>> autoTag(const std::string& filePath);
    std::future<double> detectBPM(const std::string& filePath);
    std::future<std::string> detectKey(const std::string& filePath);
    
    // User organization
    void createCollection(const std::string& name);
    void addToCollection(const std::string& collection, const std::string& assetId);
    std::vector<std::string> getCollections() const;
    std::vector<SoundAsset> getCollectionAssets(const std::string& name) const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Sample streaming for large libraries
 */
class MAESTRO_API SampleStreamer {
public:
    SampleStreamer();
    ~SampleStreamer();
    
    // Configuration
    void setBufferSize(size_t frames);
    void setMaxConcurrentStreams(int count);
    void setMaxMemoryUsage(size_t bytes);
    
    // Streaming
    struct StreamHandle {
        uint64_t id;
        bool valid;
    };
    
    StreamHandle openStream(const std::string& filePath);
    StreamHandle openCloudStream(const std::string& assetId);
    void closeStream(StreamHandle handle);
    
    // Reading
    size_t read(StreamHandle handle, float* buffer, size_t frames);
    void seek(StreamHandle handle, size_t frame);
    size_t getPosition(StreamHandle handle) const;
    size_t getTotalFrames(StreamHandle handle) const;
    
    // Preloading
    void preload(StreamHandle handle, size_t startFrame, size_t frames);
    void preloadAll(StreamHandle handle);
    bool isFullyLoaded(StreamHandle handle) const;
    
    // Memory management
    void releaseUnusedMemory();
    size_t getMemoryUsage() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::cloud
```

```cpp
// src/cloud/cloud_library.cpp
#include "maestro/cloud/cloud_library.hpp"
#include <curl/curl.h>
#include <nlohmann/json.hpp>
#include <sqlite3.h>
#include <fstream>
#include <thread>
#include <queue>
#include <mutex>
#include <condition_variable>

namespace maestro::cloud {

using json = nlohmann::json;

class CloudLibrary::Impl {
public:
    // Configuration
    std::string apiBaseUrl = "https://api.maestrostudio.com/v1";
    std::string cacheDir;
    uint64_t cacheMaxSize = 10ULL * 1024 * 1024 * 1024;  // 10GB
    
    // Authentication
    AuthToken authToken;
    std::string userId;
    bool authenticated = false;
    
    // Download management
    struct DownloadTask {
        std::string assetId;
        std::string url;
        std::string localPath;
        std::atomic<uint64_t> bytesDownloaded{0};
        uint64_t totalBytes = 0;
        std::atomic<bool> paused{false};
        std::atomic<bool> cancelled{false};
        DownloadProgress::Status status = DownloadProgress::Status::Queued;
        std::string error;
    };
    
    std::map<std::string, std::shared_ptr<DownloadTask>> downloads;
    std::mutex downloadsMutex;
    std::thread downloadThread;
    std::atomic<bool> downloadThreadRunning{false};
    std::queue<std::string> downloadQueue;
    std::condition_variable downloadCv;
    
    ProgressCallback progressCallback;
    
    // HTTP helpers
    CURL* curlHandle = nullptr;
    std::mutex curlMutex;
    
    void initCurl() {
        curl_global_init(CURL_GLOBAL_ALL);
        curlHandle = curl_easy_init();
    }
    
    void cleanupCurl() {
        if (curlHandle) {
            curl_easy_cleanup(curlHandle);
            curlHandle = nullptr;
        }
        curl_global_cleanup();
    }
    
    struct HttpResponse {
        int statusCode;
        std::string body;
        std::map<std::string, std::string> headers;
    };
    
    static size_t writeCallback(void* contents, size_t size, size_t nmemb, 
                                 std::string* userp) {
        userp->append(static_cast<char*>(contents), size * nmemb);
        return size * nmemb;
    }
    
    HttpResponse httpGet(const std::string& url) {
        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(curlMutex);
        
        HttpResponse response;
        std::string responseBody;
        
        curl_easy_reset(curlHandle);
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_URL, url.c_str());
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, writeCallback);
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, &responseBody);
        
        // Set auth header
        struct curl_slist* headers = nullptr;
        if (authenticated) {
            std::string authHeader = "Authorization: Bearer " + authToken.accessToken;
            headers = curl_slist_append(headers, authHeader.c_str());
            curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);
        }
        
        CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curlHandle);
        
        if (res == CURLE_OK) {
            curl_easy_getinfo(curlHandle, CURLINFO_RESPONSE_CODE, &response.statusCode);
            response.body = responseBody;
        } else {
            response.statusCode = -1;
            response.body = curl_easy_strerror(res);
        }
        
        if (headers) {
            curl_slist_free_all(headers);
        }
        
        return response;
    }
    
    HttpResponse httpPost(const std::string& url, const std::string& body) {
        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(curlMutex);
        
        HttpResponse response;
        std::string responseBody;
        
        curl_easy_reset(curlHandle);
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_URL, url.c_str());
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, body.c_str());
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, writeCallback);
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, &responseBody);
        
        struct curl_slist* headers = nullptr;
        headers = curl_slist_append(headers, "Content-Type: application/json");
        if (authenticated) {
            std::string authHeader = "Authorization: Bearer " + authToken.accessToken;
            headers = curl_slist_append(headers, authHeader.c_str());
        }
        curl_easy_setopt(curlHandle, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);
        
        CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curlHandle);
        
        if (res == CURLE_OK) {
            curl_easy_getinfo(curlHandle, CURLINFO_RESPONSE_CODE, &response.statusCode);
            response.body = responseBody;
        } else {
            response.statusCode = -1;
            response.body = curl_easy_strerror(res);
        }
        
        curl_slist_free_all(headers);
        return response;
    }
    
    static int downloadProgressCallback(void* clientp, curl_off_t dltotal, 
                                         curl_off_t dlnow, curl_off_t ultotal, 
                                         curl_off_t ulnow) {
        auto* task = static_cast<DownloadTask*>(clientp);
        
        if (task->cancelled) {
            return 1;  // Abort
        }
        
        if (task->paused) {
            return CURL_READFUNC_PAUSE;
        }
        
        task->bytesDownloaded = dlnow;
        task->totalBytes = dltotal;
        
        return 0;
    }
    
    void downloadFile(std::shared_ptr<DownloadTask> task) {
        CURL* dlHandle = curl_easy_init();
        if (!dlHandle) {
            task->status = DownloadProgress::Status::Failed;
            task->error = "Failed to initialize download";
            return;
        }
        
        std::ofstream file(task->localPath, std::ios::binary);
        if (!file.is_open()) {
            task->status = DownloadProgress::Status::Failed;
            task->error = "Failed to open output file";
            curl_easy_cleanup(dlHandle);
            return;
        }
        
        task->status = DownloadProgress::Status::Downloading;
        
        curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_URL, task->url.c_str());
        curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, 
            [](void* ptr, size_t size, size_t nmemb, void* stream) -> size_t {
                auto* file = static_cast<std::ofstream*>(stream);
                file->write(static_cast<char*>(ptr), size * nmemb);
                return size * nmemb;
            });
        curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, &file);
        curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_XFERINFOFUNCTION, downloadProgressCallback);
        curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_XFERINFODATA, task.get());
        curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_NOPROGRESS, 0L);
        
        // Auth header
        struct curl_slist* headers = nullptr;
        if (authenticated) {
            std::string authHeader = "Authorization: Bearer " + authToken.accessToken;
            headers = curl_slist_append(headers, authHeader.c_str());
            curl_easy_setopt(dlHandle, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);
        }
        
        CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(dlHandle);
        file.close();
        
        if (res == CURLE_OK) {
            task->status = DownloadProgress::Status::Completed;
        } else if (task->cancelled) {
            task->status = DownloadProgress::Status::Cancelled;
            std::remove(task->localPath.c_str());
        } else {
            task->status = DownloadProgress::Status::Failed;
            task->error = curl_easy_strerror(res);
            std::remove(task->localPath.c_str());
        }
        
        if (headers) {
            curl_slist_free_all(headers);
        }
        curl_easy_cleanup(dlHandle);
        
        // Notify
        if (progressCallback) {
            DownloadProgress progress;
            progress.assetId = task->assetId;
            progress.bytesDownloaded = task->bytesDownloaded;
            progress.totalBytes = task->totalBytes;
            progress.progress = task->totalBytes > 0 ? 
                static_cast<float>(task->bytesDownloaded) / task->totalBytes : 0.0f;
            progress.status = task->status;
            progress.errorMessage = task->error;
            progressCallback(progress);
        }
    }
    
    void downloadThreadFunc() {
        while (downloadThreadRunning) {
            std::string assetId;
            
            {
                std::unique_lock<std::mutex> lock(downloadsMutex);
                downloadCv.wait(lock, [this] {
                    return !downloadQueue.empty() || !downloadThreadRunning;
                });
                
                if (!downloadThreadRunning) break;
                
                if (!downloadQueue.empty()) {
                    assetId = downloadQueue.front();
                    downloadQueue.pop();
                }
            }
            
            if (!assetId.empty()) {
                auto it = downloads.find(assetId);
                if (it != downloads.end()) {
                    downloadFile(it->second);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    SoundAsset parseAsset(const json& j) {
        SoundAsset asset;
        asset.id = j.value("id", "");
        asset.name = j.value("name", "");
        asset.description = j.value("description", "");
        asset.category = j.value("category", "");
        
        if (j.contains("tags") && j["tags"].is_array()) {
            for (const auto& tag : j["tags"]) {
                asset.tags.push_back(tag.get<std::string>());
            }
        }
        
        asset.author = j.value("author", "");
        asset.license = j.value("license", "");
        
        std::string typeStr = j.value("type", "sample");
        if (typeStr == "soundfont") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::SoundFont;
        else if (typeStr == "preset") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::Preset;
        else if (typeStr == "style") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::Style;
        else if (typeStr == "midi") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::MidiFile;
        else if (typeStr == "loop") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::Loop;
        else if (typeStr == "oneshot") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::OneShot;
        else if (typeStr == "multisample") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::Multisample;
        else if (typeStr == "ir") asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::IRResponse;
        else asset.type = SoundAsset::Type::Sample;
        
        asset.sizeBytes = j.value("size_bytes", 0ULL);
        asset.durationSeconds = j.value("duration", 0.0);
        asset.sampleRate = j.value("sample_rate", 44100);
        asset.channels = j.value("channels", 2);
        asset.bitDepth = j.value("bit_depth", 16);
        asset.bpm = j.value("bpm", 0.0);
        asset.musicalKey = j.value("key", "");
        asset.rating = j.value("rating", 0.0f);
        asset.downloadCount = j.value("download_count", 0);
        asset.premium = j.value("premium", false);
        asset.priceUSD = j.value("price", 0.0);
        asset.previewUrl = j.value("preview_url", "");
        asset.downloadUrl = j.value("download_url", "");
        asset.thumbnailUrl = j.value("thumbnail_url", "");
        asset.createdAt = j.value("created_at", "");
        asset.updatedAt = j.value("updated_at", "");
        
        return asset;
    }
};

CloudLibrary::CloudLibrary() : impl_(std::make_unique<Impl>()) {
    impl_->initCurl();
}

CloudLibrary::~CloudLibrary() {
    impl_->downloadThreadRunning = false;
    impl_->downloadCv.notify_all();
    if (impl_->downloadThread.joinable()) {
        impl_->downloadThread.join();
    }
    impl_->cleanupCurl();
}

std::future<Result<CloudLibrary::AuthToken>> CloudLibrary::login(
    const AuthCredentials& creds) {
    
    return std::async(std::launch::async, [this, creds]() -> Result<AuthToken> {
        json body = {
            {"email", creds.email},
            {"password", creds.password}
        };
        
        auto response = impl_->httpPost(
            impl_->apiBaseUrl + "/auth/login",
            body.dump());
        
        if (response.statusCode != 200) {
            return Result<AuthToken>("Login failed: " + response.body);
        }
        
        try {
            auto j = json::parse(response.body);
            AuthToken token;
            token.accessToken = j["access_token"];
            token.refreshToken = j["refresh_token"];
            token.expiresAt = j["expires_at"];
            
            impl_->authToken = token;
            impl_->userId = j["user_id"];
            impl_->authenticated = true;
            
            return Result<AuthToken>(token);
        } catch (const std::exception& e) {
            return Result<AuthToken>(std::string("Parse error: ") + e.what());
        }
    });
}

void CloudLibrary::logout() {
    impl_->authenticated = false;
    impl_->authToken = {};
    impl_->userId = "";
}

bool CloudLibrary::isAuthenticated() const {
    return impl_->authenticated;
}

std::future<SearchResults> CloudLibrary::search(const SearchParams& params) {
    return std::async(std::launch::async, [this, params]() -> SearchResults {
        std::string url = impl_->apiBaseUrl + "/sounds/search?";
        url += "q=" + params.query;
        url += "&offset=" + std::to_string(params.offset);
        url += "&limit=" + std::to_string(params.limit);
        
        if (!params.categories.empty()) {
            url += "&categories=";
            for (size_t i = 0; i < params.categories.size(); ++i) {
                if (i > 0) url += ",";
                url += params.categories[i];
            }
        }
        
        if (params.minBpm > 0) url += "&min_bpm=" + std::to_string(params.minBpm);
        if (params.maxBpm > 0) url += "&max_bpm=" + std::to_string(params.maxBpm);
        if (!params.key.empty()) url += "&key=" + params.key;
        if (params.freeOnly) url += "&free=true";
        
        auto response = impl_->httpGet(url);
        
        SearchResults results;
        if (response.statusCode == 200) {
            try {
                auto j = json::parse(response.body);
                results.totalCount = j["total"];
                results.offset = j["offset"];
                results.hasMore = j["has_more"];
                
                for (const auto& item : j["items"]) {
                    results.assets.push_back(impl_->parseAsset(item));
                }
            } catch (...) {
                // Parse error
            }
        }
        
        return results;
    });
}

std::future<Result<std::string>> CloudLibrary::downloadAsset(
    const std::string& assetId,
    const std::string& localPath) {
    
    return std::async(std::launch::async, [this, assetId, localPath]() 
        -> Result<std::string> {
        
        // Get download URL
        auto response = impl_->httpGet(
            impl_->apiBaseUrl + "/sounds/" + assetId + "/download");
        
        if (response.statusCode != 200) {
            return Result<std::string>("Failed to get download URL");
        }
        
        try {
            auto j = json::parse(response.body);
            std::string downloadUrl = j["url"];
            
            // Create download task
            auto task = std::make_shared<Impl::DownloadTask>();
            task->assetId = assetId;
            task->url = downloadUrl;
            task->localPath = localPath;
            
            {
                std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(impl_->downloadsMutex);
                impl_->downloads[assetId] = task;
                impl_->downloadQueue.push(assetId);
            }
            
            // Start download thread if not running
            if (!impl_->downloadThreadRunning) {
                impl_->downloadThreadRunning = true;
                impl_->downloadThread = std::thread(
                    &Impl::downloadThreadFunc, impl_.get());
            }
            
            impl_->downloadCv.notify_one();
            
            // Wait for completion
            while (task->status != DownloadProgress::Status::Completed &&
                   task->status != DownloadProgress::Status::Failed &&
                   task->status != DownloadProgress::Status::Cancelled) {
                std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(100));
            }
            
            if (task->status == DownloadProgress::Status::Completed) {
                return Result<std::string>(localPath);
            } else {
                return Result<std::string>("Download failed: " + task->error);
            }
            
        } catch (const std::exception& e) {
            return Result<std::string>(std::string("Error: ") + e.what());
        }
    });
}

void CloudLibrary::pauseDownload(const std::string& assetId) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(impl_->downloadsMutex);
    auto it = impl_->downloads.find(assetId);
    if (it != impl_->downloads.end()) {
        it->second->paused = true;
    }
}

void CloudLibrary::resumeDownload(const std::string& assetId) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(impl_->downloadsMutex);
    auto it = impl_->downloads.find(assetId);
    if (it != impl_->downloads.end()) {
        it->second->paused = false;
    }
}

void CloudLibrary::cancelDownload(const std::string& assetId) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(impl_->downloadsMutex);
    auto it = impl_->downloads.find(assetId);
    if (it != impl_->downloads.end()) {
        it->second->cancelled = true;
    }
}

std::vector<DownloadProgress> CloudLibrary::getActiveDownloads() const {
    std::vector<DownloadProgress> result;
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(impl_->downloadsMutex);
    
    for (const auto& [id, task] : impl_->downloads) {
        if (task->status == DownloadProgress::Status::Downloading ||
            task->status == DownloadProgress::Status::Queued) {
            DownloadProgress progress;
            progress.assetId = task->assetId;
            progress.bytesDownloaded = task->bytesDownloaded;
            progress.totalBytes = task->totalBytes;
            progress.progress = task->totalBytes > 0 ?
                static_cast<float>(task->bytesDownloaded) / task->totalBytes : 0.0f;
            progress.status = task->status;
            result.push_back(progress);
        }
    }
    
    return result;
}

void CloudLibrary::setProgressCallback(ProgressCallback callback) {
    impl_->progressCallback = std::move(callback);
}

} // namespace maestro::cloud
```

# PHASE 3.3: VIDEO SYNC CAPABILITIES

```cpp
// include/maestro/video/video_engine.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <functional>
#include <string>

namespace maestro::video {

/**
 * @brief Timecode formats
 */
enum class TimecodeFormat {
    SMPTE_24,      // Film
    SMPTE_25,      // PAL
    SMPTE_29_97_DF, // NTSC drop-frame
    SMPTE_29_97_NDF,// NTSC non-drop-frame
    SMPTE_30,      // 30 fps
    SMPTE_30_DF,   // 30 fps drop-frame
    SMPTE_60,      // 60 fps
    Milliseconds,
    Samples,
    Feet_Frames    // Film footage
};

/**
 * @brief Timecode representation
 */
struct Timecode {
    int hours = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    int frames = 0;
    bool dropFrame = false;
    TimecodeFormat format = TimecodeFormat::SMPTE_24;
    
    // Conversion
    double toSeconds() const;
    int64_t toFrames() const;
    int64_t toSamples(SampleRate sampleRate) const;
    TickCount toTicks(int ppqn, double tempo) const;
    
    static Timecode fromSeconds(double seconds, TimecodeFormat format);
    static Timecode fromFrames(int64_t frames, TimecodeFormat format);
    static Timecode fromSamples(int64_t samples, SampleRate rate, 
                                 TimecodeFormat format);
    
    std::string toString() const;
    static Timecode fromString(const std::string& str, TimecodeFormat format);
    
    bool operator<(const Timecode& other) const;
    bool operator==(const Timecode& other) const;
    Timecode operator+(const Timecode& other) const;
    Timecode operator-(const Timecode& other) const;
};

/**
 * @brief Video file information
 */
struct VideoInfo {
    std::string path;
    std::string codec;
    int width;
    int height;
    double frameRate;
    int64_t frameCount;
    double duration;
    bool hasAudio;
    int audioChannels;
    SampleRate audioSampleRate;
    Timecode startTimecode;
};

/**
 * @brief Video frame
 */
struct VideoFrame {
    int width;
    int height;
    enum class Format { RGB24, RGBA32, YUV420P, NV12 } format;
    std::vector<uint8_t> data;
    int64_t frameNumber;
    Timecode timecode;
    double timestamp;
};

/**
 * @brief Video player for scoring to picture
 */
class MAESTRO_API VideoPlayer {
public:
    VideoPlayer();
    ~VideoPlayer();
    
    // File operations
    Result<VideoInfo> open(const std::string& path);
    void close();
    bool isOpen() const;
    VideoInfo getInfo() const;
    
    // Playback control
    void play();
    void pause();
    void stop();
    void seek(const Timecode& position);
    void seekToFrame(int64_t frame);
    void seekToSeconds(double seconds);
    
    bool isPlaying() const;
    Timecode getPosition() const;
    int64_t getCurrentFrame() const;
    double getCurrentTime() const;
    
    // Playback speed
    void setPlaybackRate(double rate);  // 1.0 = normal
    double getPlaybackRate() const;
    
    // Loop
    void setLoopRegion(const Timecode& start, const Timecode& end);
    void clearLoopRegion();
    void setLoopEnabled(bool enabled);
    
    // Frame access
    VideoFrame getFrame(int64_t frameNumber);
    VideoFrame getCurrentVideoFrame();
    
    // Thumbnail generation
    std::vector<VideoFrame> generateThumbnails(int count);
    VideoFrame getThumbnailAt(double seconds);
    
    // Audio extraction
    std::vector<float> extractAudio(double startSeconds, double duration);
    Result<void> extractAudioToFile(const std::string& outputPath);
    
    // Rendering callbacks
    using FrameCallback = std::function<void(const VideoFrame&)>;
    void setFrameCallback(FrameCallback callback);
    
    // Display
    void setRenderTarget(void* windowHandle);
    void setRenderSize(int width, int height);
    void setMaintainAspectRatio(bool maintain);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Sync to external timecode
 */
class MAESTRO_API TimecodeSync {
public:
    TimecodeSync();
    ~TimecodeSync();
    
    // Source configuration
    enum class Source {
        Internal,        // Free-running
        MTC,            // MIDI Timecode
        LTC,            // Linear Timecode (audio)
        VideoFile,      // From video file
        Network,        // Network sync (PTP/NTP)
        Manual          // Manual entry
    };
    
    void setSource(Source source);
    Source getSource() const;
    
    // MIDI Timecode
    void setMTCInput(const std::string& midiPortId);
    void processMTCMessage(const midi::MidiMessage& msg);
    
    // LTC (Linear Timecode)
    void setLTCInput(int audioInputChannel);
    void processLTCAudio(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Format
    void setTimecodeFormat(TimecodeFormat format);
    TimecodeFormat getTimecodeFormat() const;
    
    // Offset
    void setOffset(const Timecode& offset);
    Timecode getOffset() const;
    
    // Current position
    Timecode getCurrentTimecode() const;
    bool isLocked() const;  // True if receiving valid timecode
    
    // Generate timecode
    void startGenerator();
    void stopGenerator();
    void setGeneratorPosition(const Timecode& position);
    
    // MTC output
    void setMTCOutput(const std::string& midiPortId);
    void sendMTCFullFrame();
    
    // LTC output
    void setLTCOutput(int audioOutputChannel);
    void generateLTCAudio(float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Callbacks
    using TimecodeCallback = std::function<void(const Timecode&)>;
    void setTimecodeCallback(TimecodeCallback callback);
    using LockCallback = std::function<void(bool locked)>;
    void setLockCallback(LockCallback callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Video scoring / cue management
 */
class MAESTRO_API VideoScoring {
public:
    struct Cue {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        std::string description;
        Timecode inPoint;
        Timecode outPoint;
        QColor color;
        
        enum class Type { 
            Hit,         // Precise sync point
            Region,      // Time region
            Marker,      // Reference marker
            Dialog,      // Dialog section
            Music,       // Music cue
            SFX          // Sound effect
        };
        Type type;
        
        // Musical settings
        double tempo;
        TimeSignature timeSignature;
        std::string key;
        
        // Notes
        std::string notes;
        std::vector<std::string> tags;
    };
    
    VideoScoring();
    ~VideoScoring();
    
    // Cue management
    std::string addCue(const Cue& cue);
    void removeCue(const std::string& id);
    void updateCue(const Cue& cue);
    Cue getCue(const std::string& id) const;
    std::vector<Cue> getAllCues() const;
    std::vector<Cue> getCuesInRange(const Timecode& start, 
                                     const Timecode& end) const;
    
    // Hit point detection
    std::vector<Timecode> detectHitPoints(VideoPlayer& video,
                                           float sensitivity = 0.5f);
    std::vector<Timecode> detectSceneCuts(VideoPlayer& video);
    
    // Tempo mapping
    struct TempoChange {
        Timecode position;
        double tempo;
        enum class Type { Immediate, Linear, Smooth } type;
    };
    
    void addTempoChange(const TempoChange& change);
    void removeTempoChange(const Timecode& position);
    std::vector<TempoChange> getTempoMap() const;
    double getTempoAt(const Timecode& position) const;
    
    // Click track generation
    struct ClickTrackSettings {
        int accentPattern = 4;    // Accent every N beats
        bool countIn = true;
        int countInBars = 1;
        float clickVolume = 0.8f;
        std::string clickSound;   // Sample path
        std::string accentSound;
    };
    
    std::vector<float> generateClickTrack(const Timecode& start,
                                           const Timecode& end,
                                           const ClickTrackSettings& settings);
    
    // Streamers and punches
    struct Streamer {
        Timecode start;
        Timecode end;
        QColor color;
        int duration;  // frames
    };
    
    void addStreamer(const Streamer& streamer);
    std::vector<Streamer> getStreamers() const;
    void addPunch(const Timecode& position);
    std::vector<Timecode> getPunches() const;
    
    // Import/Export
    Result<void> importCMX3600(const std::string& path);  // EDL format
    Result<void> exportCMX3600(const std::string& path);
    Result<void> importXML(const std::string& path);      // Final Cut XML
    Result<void> exportXML(const std::string& path);
    Result<void> importAAF(const std::string& path);      // Avid AAF
    Result<void> exportOMF(const std::string& path);      // OMF/AAF
    
    // Markers to/from DAW
    void importMarkersFromProject(const studio::Project& project);
    void exportMarkersToProject(studio::Project& project);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief ADR (Automated Dialog Replacement) tools
 */
class MAESTRO_API ADRSession {

    struct Take {
        std::string id;

    // Loop playback
    void startLoopPlayback(const Take& take);
    void stopLoopPlayback();
    
    // Walla/Group recording
    void setGroupMode(bool enabled);
    int getGroupTakeCount() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};
```

# PHASE 3.4: ADVANCED NOTATION EDITOR

```cpp
// include/maestro/notation/notation_engine.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

namespace maestro::notation {

/**
 * @brief Note value (duration)
 */
enum class NoteValue {
    Maxima,
    Longa,
    DoubleWhole,  // Breve
    Whole,        // Semibreve
    Half,         // Minim
    Quarter,      // Crotchet
    Eighth,       // Quaver
    Sixteenth,    // Semiquaver
    ThirtySecond, // Demisemiquaver
    SixtyFourth,  // Hemidemisemiquaver
    HundredTwentyEighth
};

/**
 * @brief Note accidental
 */
enum class Accidental {
    None,
    Natural,
    Sharp,
    Flat,
    DoubleSharp,
    DoubleFlat,
    QuarterSharp,
    QuarterFlat
};

/**
 * @brief Articulation marks
 */
enum class Articulation {
    None,
    Staccato,
    Staccatissimo,
    Accent,
    Marcato,
    Tenuto,
    Fermata,
    Trill,
    Mordent,
    Turn,
    Tremolo,
    Arpeggio
};

/**
 * @brief Dynamic marking
 */
enum class Dynamic {
    PPPP, PPP, PP, P, MP, MF, F, FF, FFF, FFFF,
    FP, SF, SFZ, SFFZ, FZ, RF, RFZ,
    Crescendo, Decrescendo, 
    CrescendoHairpin, DecrescendoHairpin
};

/**
 * @brief Clef types
 */
enum class Clef {
    Treble,
    Bass,
    Alto,
    Tenor,
    Soprano,
    MezzoSoprano,
    Baritone,
    Percussion,
    Tab,
    Treble8va,
    Treble8vb,
    Bass8va,
    Bass8vb
};

/**
 * @brief Key signature
 */
struct KeySignature {
    enum class Mode { Major, Minor, Dorian, Phrygian, Lydian, 
                      Mixolydian, Locrian, Custom };
    
    int fifths = 0;  // -7 to +7 (flats to sharps)
    Mode mode = Mode::Major;
    
    std::string toString() const;
    static KeySignature fromString(const std::string& str);
    
    static KeySignature CMajor() { return {0, Mode::Major}; }
    static KeySignature AMinor() { return {0, Mode::Minor}; }
    static KeySignature GMajor() { return {1, Mode::Major}; }
    // ... etc
};

/**
 * @brief Musical note in notation
 */
struct NotationNote {
    // Pitch
    int step;              // 0-6 (C-B)
    int octave;            // -1 to 9
    Accidental accidental;
    int alterCents;        // Microtonal adjustment
    
    // Duration
    NoteValue value;
    int dots;              // 0-3
    bool isTied;
    
    // Display
    int voice;             // 1-4 typically
    int staff;             // For grand staff
    bool stemUp;
    bool beamStart;
    bool beamEnd;
    int beamLevel;
    
    // Articulations
    std::vector<Articulation> articulations;
    
    // Ornaments
    bool hasTrill;
    bool hasTremolo;
    int tremoloBeams;
    
    // Lyrics
    std::string lyric;
    int syllableType;      // 0=single, 1=begin, 2=middle, 3=end
    
    // Technical
    int fingering;
    std::string technique;
    
    // Position info
    TickCount tick;
    TickCount duration;
    MidiNote midiPitch;
    
    // Convert to/from MIDI
    static NotationNote fromMidi(const midi::NoteEvent& event, 
                                  const KeySignature& key);
    midi::NoteEvent toMidi() const;
};

/**
 * @brief Rest
 */
struct Rest {
    NoteValue value;
    int dots;
    int voice;
    int staff;
    TickCount tick;
    TickCount duration;
    bool isWholeBarRest;
    int multiRestBars;     // For multi-measure rests
};

/**
 * @brief Measure/bar
 */
struct Measure {
    int number;
    TickCount startTick;
    TickCount duration;
    
    TimeSignature timeSignature;
    KeySignature keySignature;
    bool keySignatureChange;
    bool timeSignatureChange;
    
    std::vector<Clef> clefs;
    bool clefChange;
    
    std::vector<NotationNote> notes;
    std::vector<Rest> rests;
    
    // Barlines
    enum class Barline { 
        Regular, Double, Final, RepeatStart, RepeatEnd, 
        RepeatBoth, Dashed, None 
    };
    Barline leftBarline;
    Barline rightBarline;
    
    // Repeats
    bool hasRepeatStart;
    bool hasRepeatEnd;
    int repeatCount;
    
    // Endings
    int ending;            // 0 = none, 1 = first ending, etc.
    
    // Rehearsal marks
    std::string rehearsalMark;
    
    // Tempo
    double tempo;
    std::string tempoText;
    bool tempoChange;
    
    // Dynamics
    std::vector<std::pair<TickCount, Dynamic>> dynamics;
    
    // Text
    std::vector<std::pair<TickCount, std::string>> expressions;
    std::vector<std::pair<TickCount, std::string>> techniques;
};

/**
 * @brief Staff definition
 */
struct Staff {
    std::string name;
    std::string abbreviation;
    Clef defaultClef;
    int transpose;         // Semitones (for transposing instruments)
    int staffLines;        // Usually 5, can be 1 for percussion
    bool isTab;
    std::vector<int> tabStrings;  // MIDI pitches for tab
    
    // Brackets/bracing
    enum class Bracket { None, Brace, Bracket, Square, Line };
    Bracket bracket;
    int bracketSpan;
    
    // Sound
    std::string midiInstrument;
    int midiChannel;
    int midiProgram;
};

/**
 * @brief Part (instrument) in score
 */
struct Part {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string abbreviation;
    std::vector<Staff> staves;
    std::vector<Measure> measures;
    
    // MIDI mapping
    int midiChannel;
    int midiProgram;
    
    // Part-specific settings
    bool visible;
    bool printable;
};

/**
 * @brief Complete musical score
 */
class MAESTRO_API Score {
public:
    Score();
    ~Score();
    
    // Metadata
    void setTitle(const std::string& title);
    void setComposer(const std::string& composer);
    void setArranger(const std::string& arranger);
    void setLyricist(const std::string& lyricist);
    void setCopyright(const std::string& copyright);
    
    std::string getTitle() const;
    std::string getComposer() const;
    
    // Score structure
    void addPart(const Part& part);
    void removePart(const std::string& id);
    Part& getPart(const std::string& id);
    std::vector<Part>& getParts();
    int getPartCount() const;
    
    // Measures
    void addMeasure();
    void insertMeasure(int position);
    void deleteMeasure(int position);
    int getMeasureCount() const;
    
    // Global settings
    void setDefaultTimeSignature(const TimeSignature& ts);
    void setDefaultKeySignature(const KeySignature& ks);
    void setDefaultTempo(double bpm);
    
    // Layout
    struct PageSettings {
        double width;        // mm
        double height;       // mm
        double marginLeft;
        double marginRight;
        double marginTop;
        double marginBottom;
        double staffDistance;
        double systemDistance;
    };
    void setPageSettings(const PageSettings& settings);
    PageSettings getPageSettings() const;
    
    // Import
    static Result<Score> importMIDI(const std::string& path);
    static Result<Score> importMusicXML(const std::string& path);
    static Result<Score> importMXL(const std::string& path);  // Compressed MusicXML
    static Result<Score> importLilypond(const std::string& path);
    static Result<Score> importABC(const std::string& path);
    
    // Export
    Result<void> exportMusicXML(const std::string& path) const;
    Result<void> exportPDF(const std::string& path) const;
    Result<void> exportPNG(const std::string& path, int dpi = 300) const;
    Result<void> exportSVG(const std::string& path) const;
    Result<void> exportLilypond(const std::string& path) const;
    Result<void> exportMIDI(const std::string& path) const;
    
    // MIDI conversion
    void fromMidiFile(const MidiFile& midi, const QuantizeSettings& settings);
    MidiFile toMidiFile() const;
    
    // Transposition
    void transpose(int semitones);
    void transposePart(const std::string& partId, int semitones);
    
    // Part extraction
    Score extractPart(const std::string& partId) const;
    Score extractParts(const std::vector<std::string>& partIds) const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief MIDI to notation quantization
 */
struct QuantizeSettings {
    // Minimum note value to consider
    NoteValue minimumDuration = NoteValue::ThirtySecond;
    
    // Tuplet detection
    bool detectTuplets = true;
    std::vector<int> allowedTuplets = {3, 5, 6, 7};
    
    // Voice separation
    int maxVoices = 4;
    bool separateByPitch = true;
    MidiNote voiceSplitPoint = 60;
    
    // Tied notes
    bool createTiedNotes = true;
    
    // Rest detection
    bool detectRests = true;
    
    // Articulation detection
    bool detectStaccato = true;
    float staccatoThreshold = 0.5f;
    bool detectAccents = true;
    
    // Spelling
    bool useKeySignature = true;
    bool preferFlats = false;
    bool preferSharps = false;
};

/**
 * @brief Notation quantizer
 */
class MAESTRO_API NotationQuantizer {
public:
    NotationQuantizer();
    ~NotationQuantizer();
    
    void setSettings(const QuantizeSettings& settings);
    QuantizeSettings getSettings() const;
    
    // Quantize MIDI to notation
    std::vector<NotationNote> quantize(
        const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& events,
        const TimeSignature& timeSignature,
        const KeySignature& keySignature,
        int ppqn = 480);
    
    // Rhythm analysis
    struct RhythmAnalysis {
        std::vector<NoteValue> detectedValues;
        std::vector<std::pair<int, float>> tupletConfidence;
        float swingAmount;
        bool isSwung;
    };
    RhythmAnalysis analyzeRhythm(const std::vector<midi::NoteEvent>& events);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Notation rendering engine
 */
class MAESTRO_API NotationRenderer {
public:
    NotationRenderer();
    ~NotationRenderer();
    
    // Font settings
    void setMusicFont(const std::string& fontPath);
    void setTextFont(const std::string& fontPath);
    void setFontSize(float size);
    
    // Rendering
    struct RenderSettings {
        int width;
        int height;
        float scale;
        bool antialiasing;
        QColor backgroundColor;
        QColor foregroundColor;
        bool showMeasureNumbers;
        bool showPageNumbers;
        bool showInstrumentNames;
    };
    
    void setSettings(const RenderSettings& settings);
    
    // Render to image
    QImage renderPage(const Score& score, int pageNumber);
    std::vector<QImage> renderAllPages(const Score& score);
    
    // Render to widget (for live editing)
    void renderToWidget(const Score& score, QWidget* widget,
                        int startMeasure, int endMeasure);
    
    // Layout calculation
    struct LayoutInfo {
        int pageCount;
        std::vector<int> measuresPerSystem;
        std::vector<int> systemsPerPage;
    };
    LayoutInfo calculateLayout(const Score& score);
    
    // Hit testing
    struct HitResult {
        enum class Type { 
            None, Note, Rest, Clef, KeySignature, TimeSignature,
            Barline, Dynamic, Text, Articulation 
        };
        Type type;
        std::string partId;
        int measureNumber;
        int voice;
        int noteIndex;
    };
    HitResult hitTest(const Score& score, int pageNumber, 
                      int x, int y);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Notation editor
 */
class MAESTRO_API NotationEditor {
public:
    NotationEditor();
    ~NotationEditor();
    
    // Document
    void setScore(Score* score);
    Score* getScore() const;
    
    // Selection
    struct Selection {
        std::string partId;
        int startMeasure;
        int endMeasure;
        int startBeat;
        int endBeat;
        int voice;
        std::vector<int> noteIndices;
    };
    
    void setSelection(const Selection& selection);
    Selection getSelection() const;
    void clearSelection();
    
    // Input mode
    enum class InputMode {
        Select,
        Note,
        Rest,
        Chord,
        Text,
        Dynamic,
        Articulation
    };
    void setInputMode(InputMode mode);
    void setInputNoteValue(NoteValue value);
    void setInputDots(int dots);
    void setInputVoice(int voice);
    
    // Note entry
    void enterNote(int step, int octave, Accidental accidental = Accidental::None);
    void enterChordNote(int step, int octave, Accidental accidental = Accidental::None);
    void enterRest();
    void advanceCursor();
    void moveCursorBack();
    
    // Editing
    void deleteSelection();
    void cut();
    void copy();
    void paste();
    
    void transposeSelection(int semitones);
    void changeNoteValue(NoteValue newValue);
    void addDot();
    void removeDot();
    void toggleTie();
    void addArticulation(Articulation art);
    void removeArticulation(Articulation art);
    
    // Slurs and ties
    void startSlur();
    void endSlur();
    void startCrescendo();
    void endCrescendo();
    void startDecrescendo();
    void endDecrescendo();
    
    // Text
    void addDynamic(Dynamic dynamic);
    void addExpression(const std::string& text);
    void addTechnique(const std::string& text);
    void addLyric(const std::string& text);
    void addRehearsalMark(const std::string& text);
    
    // Playback from notation
    void playFromSelection();
    void playMeasure(int measureNumber);
    void stopPlayback();
    
    // Undo/redo
    void undo();
    void redo();
    bool canUndo() const;
    bool canRedo() const;
    
    // Callbacks
    using SelectionCallback = std::function<void(const Selection&)>;
    void setSelectionCallback(SelectionCallback callback);
    
    using ModificationCallback = std::function<void()>;
    void setModificationCallback(ModificationCallback callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::notation
```
