# PHASE 3.5: HARDWARE CONTROLLER INTEGRATION

```cpp
// include/maestro/controllers/controller_manager.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <functional>
#include <map>

namespace maestro::controllers {

/**
 * @brief Controller element types
 */
enum class ElementType {
    Button,
    Fader,
    Knob,
    Encoder,       // Endless rotary
    Pad,
    XYPad,
    Jog,           // Jog wheel
    Touchstrip,
    Display,
    LED,
    LEDRing,
    Motor,         // Motorized fader
    PitchBend,
    ModWheel,
    Expression,
    Aftertouch
};

/**
 * @brief Controller element definition
 */
struct ControllerElement {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    ElementType type;
    
    // MIDI mapping
    MidiChannel channel;
    uint8_t ccNumber;
    uint8_t noteNumber;
    bool usesNRPN;
    uint16_t nrpnNumber;
    bool uses14bit;
    
    // Value range
    int minValue;
    int maxValue;
    int defaultValue;
    bool isBipolar;      // Center at 64
    
    // Physical properties
    bool hasMotor;
    bool hasTouchSense;
    bool hasLED;
    int ledColors;       // Number of colors
    bool hasDisplay;
    
    // Behavior
    bool isMomentary;    // For buttons
    bool isRelative;     // For encoders
    int resolution;      // For encoders
};

/**
 * @brief Controller profile/definition
 */
struct ControllerProfile {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string manufacturer;
    std::string model;
    std::string version;
    
    // Connection
    enum class ConnectionType { USB, MIDI, Bluetooth, Network };
    ConnectionType connection;
    std::string usbVendorId;
    std::string usbProductId;
    
    // Elements
    std::vector<ControllerElement> elements;
    
    // Modes/Banks
    int numBanks;
    std::vector<std::string> bankNames;
    
    // Display capabilities
    bool hasDisplay;
    int displayWidth;
    int displayHeight;
    int displayColors;
    
    // Motor fader calibration
    bool hasMotorFaders;
    int motorFaderResolution;
    float motorFaderSpeed;
    
    // SysEx
    std::vector<uint8_t> initSysEx;
    std::vector<uint8_t> exitSysEx;
    
    // Scripts
    std::string scriptPath;
};

/**
 * @brief Control mapping
 */
struct ControlMapping {
    std::string elementId;
    std::string targetType;     // "parameter", "action", "midi", "script"
    std::string targetId;
    
    // Scaling
    float inputMin;
    float inputMax;
    float outputMin;
    float outputMax;
    enum class Curve { Linear, Log, Exp, SCurve } curve;
    
    // Options
    bool relative;
    float acceleration;
    bool takeover;              // Pickup mode
    enum class TakeoverMode { Jump, Pickup, Scale } takeoverMode;
    
    // Feedback
    bool feedbackEnabled;
    
    // Conditions
    std::string condition;      // Expression for conditional mapping
    int bank;                   // Active only in specific bank
};

/**
 * @brief Connected controller instance
 */
class MAESTRO_API ControllerInstance {
public:
    ControllerInstance(const ControllerProfile& profile);
    ~ControllerInstance();
    
    // Connection
    Result<void> connect(const std::string& midiInPort, 
                         const std::string& midiOutPort);
    void disconnect();
    bool isConnected() const;
    
    // Profile
    const ControllerProfile& getProfile() const;
    
    // Banks
    void setBank(int bank);
    int getBank() const;
    void nextBank();
    void previousBank();
    
    // Element values
    int getElementValue(const std::string& elementId) const;
    void setElementValue(const std::string& elementId, int value);
    
    // LED control
    void setLED(const std::string& elementId, int color);
    void setLEDRing(const std::string& elementId, int value, int mode);
    void blinkLED(const std::string& elementId, int color, int rate);
    
    // Display
    void setDisplayText(int line, const std::string& text);
    void setDisplayText(int line, int column, const std::string& text);
    void setDisplayBrightness(float brightness);
    void setDisplayContrast(float contrast);
    void clearDisplay();
    void drawOnDisplay(int x, int y, int width, int height, 
                       const uint8_t* pixels);
    
    // Motor faders
    void moveMotorFader(const std::string& elementId, int position);
    void enableMotors(bool enable);
    void setMotorSpeed(float speed);
    
    // Callbacks
    using ElementCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& elementId, 
                                                int value, int velocity)>;
    void setElementCallback(ElementCallback callback);
    
    using TouchCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& elementId, 
                                              bool touched)>;
    void setTouchCallback(TouchCallback callback);
    
    // Raw MIDI
    void sendSysEx(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data);
    void sendMidi(const midi::MidiMessage& msg);
    
    // State
    void saveState();
    void restoreState();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Controller manager
 */
class MAESTRO_API ControllerManager {
public:
    static ControllerManager& instance();
    
    // Profile management
    void loadProfiles(const std::string& directory);
    void addProfile(const ControllerProfile& profile);
    void removeProfile(const std::string& id);
    std::vector<ControllerProfile> getProfiles() const;
    ControllerProfile* getProfile(const std::string& id);
    
    // Auto-detection
    void startAutoDetect();
    void stopAutoDetect();
    std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>> getDetectedControllers() const;
    
    // Instance management
    std::shared_ptr<ControllerInstance> createInstance(const std::string& profileId);
    void destroyInstance(std::shared_ptr<ControllerInstance> instance);
    std::vector<std::shared_ptr<ControllerInstance>> getInstances() const;
    
    // Mapping
    void addMapping(const ControlMapping& mapping);
    void removeMapping(const std::string& elementId);
    void clearMappings();
    std::vector<ControlMapping> getMappings() const;
    
    // Learn mode
    void startLearn(const std::string& targetType, const std::string& targetId);
    void stopLearn();
    bool isLearning() const;
    
    // Presets
    void saveMappingPreset(const std::string& name, const std::string& path);
    void loadMappingPreset(const std::string& path);
    std::vector<std::string> getMappingPresets() const;
    
    // Callbacks
    using ControllerConnectedCallback = std::function<void(
        std::shared_ptr<ControllerInstance>)>;
    void setConnectedCallback(ControllerConnectedCallback callback);
    
    using ControllerDisconnectedCallback = std::function<void(const std::string&)>;
    void setDisconnectedCallback(ControllerDisconnectedCallback callback);

private:
    ControllerManager();
    ~ControllerManager();
    
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Specific controller implementations
 */
namespace controllers {

/**
 * @brief Mackie Control Universal protocol
 */
class MAESTRO_API MackieControl : public ControllerInstance {

    MackieControl();

    void setFaderBankRight();
    void setChannelLeft();
    void setChannelRight();

    void setVPotLED(int channel, bool on);
    
    // Scribble strips
    void setScribbleStrip(int channel, const std::string& topText,
                          const std::string& bottomText);
    void setScribbleStripColor(int channel, int color);
    
    // Time display
    void setTimeDisplay(const std::string& time);
    void setAssignmentDisplay(const std::string& text);
    
    // Transport LEDs
    void setTransportLED(const std::string& name, bool on);
    
    // Meters
    void setMeter(int channel, int level);
    void setMeterMode(int mode);

    void handleMackieMessage(const midi::MidiMessage& msg);
};

/**
 * @brief HUI (Human User Interface) protocol
 */
class MAESTRO_API HUIController : public ControllerInstance {

    HUIController();
    
    // HUI zones
    void setLED(int zone, int port, bool on);
    void setVPot(int channel, int value);
    void setFader(int channel, int value);
    void setMeter(int channel, int value);

    void setTimeDisplay(const std::string& time);

    void setSelectDisplay(int channel, const std::string& text);

};

/**
 * @brief Ableton Push integration
 */
class MAESTRO_API AbletonPush : public ControllerInstance {
public:
    AbletonPush(int version = 2);  // 1, 2, or 3
    
    // Pads
    void setPadColor(int row, int col, int r, int g, int b);
    void setPadColorPalette(int row, int col, int paletteIndex);
    void setPadBrightness(float brightness);
    void animatePad(int row, int col, int animation);
    
    // Display
    void setDisplayMode(int mode);  // Session, Note, Drum, etc.
    void setDisplayLine(int line, const std::string& text);
    void setDisplayGraph(int col, int value);
    
    // Touch strip
    void setTouchStripLEDs(const std::vector<int>& leds);
    void setTouchStripMode(int mode);
    
    // Encoders
    void setEncoderMode(int mode);
    
    // Button LEDs
    void setButtonLED(const std::string& button, int color);

private:
    int version_;
    void initPush();
};

/**
 * @brief Native Instruments controllers
 */
class MAESTRO_API NIController : public ControllerInstance {
public:
    enum class Model {
        MaschineStudio,
        MaschineMK3,
        KompleteKontrolS49,
        KompleteKontrolS61,
        KompleteKontrolS88,
        KompleteKontrolA49,
        KompleteKontrolA61,
        KompleteKontrolM32
    };
    
    NIController(Model model);

    // Display

                         int width, int height);
    
    // Browser

    // Smart Strip

 */
class MAESTRO_API OSCController {

    ~OSCController();

                         int receivePort);

    void unmapOSCPath(const std::string& path);
    
    // Send OSC

    void sendInt(const std::string& path, int value);
    void sendString(const std::string& path, const std::string& value);
    void sendColor(const std::string& path, int r, int g, int b);
    
    // Receive callback

                                            const std::vector<std::variant<
                                                int, float, std::string>>& args)>;
    void setCallback(OSCCallback callback);
    
    // TouchOSC templates
    void loadTouchOSCTemplate(const std::string& path);
    void sendTouchOSCUpdate();

    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};
```

# PHASE 3.6: SPATIAL AUDIO

```cpp
// include/maestro/spatial/spatial_audio.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <array>

namespace maestro::spatial {

/**
 * @brief 3D position
 */
struct Position3D {
    float x = 0.0f;  // Left/Right
    float y = 0.0f;  // Up/Down
    float z = 0.0f;  // Front/Back
    
    float distance() const;
    float azimuth() const;   // Horizontal angle (-180 to 180)
    float elevation() const; // Vertical angle (-90 to 90)
    
    static Position3D fromSpherical(float azimuth, float elevation, 
                                     float distance);
};

/**
 * @brief Audio object for object-based audio
 */
struct AudioObject {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    Position3D position;
    float gain = 1.0f;
    float size = 0.0f;       // Object size (for spreading)
    bool isLFE = false;      // Low-frequency content
    int priority = 0;        // For rendering priority
    
    // Movement
    Position3D velocity;
    bool doppler = false;
    
    // Divergence
    float divergence = 0.0f;  // Object spreading
    
    // Distance attenuation
    enum class Attenuation { None, Linear, Logarithmic, Custom };
    Attenuation attenuation = Attenuation::Logarithmic;
    float attenuationMin = 1.0f;
    float attenuationMax = 100.0f;
};

/**
 * @brief Speaker layout/configuration
 */
struct SpeakerLayout {
    std::string name;
    
    struct Speaker {
        std::string label;
        float azimuth;
        float elevation;
        float distance;
        bool isLFE;
        int outputChannel;
    };
    std::vector<Speaker> speakers;
    
    // Standard layouts
    static SpeakerLayout Stereo();
    static SpeakerLayout Quad();
    static SpeakerLayout Surround51();
    static SpeakerLayout Surround71();
    static SpeakerLayout Atmos714();   // 7.1.4
    static SpeakerLayout Atmos916();   // 9.1.6
    static SpeakerLayout Auro3D();
    static SpeakerLayout MPEG_H();
    static SpeakerLayout Binaural();
    
    int getChannelCount() const;
    int getLFECount() const;
};

/**
 * @brief Ambisonics format
 */
class MAESTRO_API Ambisonics {
public:
    enum class Order { First = 1, Second = 2, Third = 3, Fourth = 4, 
                       Fifth = 5, Sixth = 6, Seventh = 7 };
    enum class Normalization { SN3D, N3D, FuMa };
    enum class ChannelOrder { ACN, FuMa };
    
    Ambisonics(Order order = Order::Third);
    ~Ambisonics();
    
    // Configuration
    void setOrder(Order order);
    Order getOrder() const;
    void setNormalization(Normalization norm);
    void setChannelOrder(ChannelOrder order);
    
    int getChannelCount() const;
    
    // Encoding
    void encode(const float* input, float* output, int numFrames,
                float azimuth, float elevation, float distance = 1.0f);
    
    void encodeMultiple(const std::vector<const float*>& inputs,
                        const std::vector<Position3D>& positions,
                        float* output, int numFrames);
    
    // Decoding
    void decode(const float* ambiInput, float* const* speakerOutputs,
                int numFrames, const SpeakerLayout& layout);
    
    void decodeBinaural(const float* ambiInput, float* leftOut, 
                        float* rightOut, int numFrames);
    
    // Rotation
    void rotate(float* ambiData, int numFrames, 
                float yaw, float pitch, float roll);
    
    // Room simulation
    void applyRoomReflections(float* ambiData, int numFrames,
                              float roomWidth, float roomDepth, 
                              float roomHeight,
                              float reflectionCoeff = 0.5f);
    
    // Conversion
    void convertACNToFuMa(float* data, int numFrames);
    void convertFuMaToACN(float* data, int numFrames);
    void convertNormalization(float* data, int numFrames,
                               Normalization from, Normalization to);
    
    // Load HRTF for binaural
    Result<void> loadHRTF(const std::string& path);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Dolby Atmos renderer
 */
class MAESTRO_API AtmosRenderer {
public:
    AtmosRenderer();
    ~AtmosRenderer();
    
    // Initialization
    Result<void> initialize(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize);
    void shutdown();
    
    // Output configuration
    void setOutputLayout(const SpeakerLayout& layout);
    void setBinauralMode(bool binaural);
    void setHeadTracking(bool enabled);
    void setHeadPosition(float yaw, float pitch, float roll);
    
    // Objects
    int addObject(const AudioObject& object);
    void removeObject(int objectId);
    void updateObject(int objectId, const AudioObject& object);
    void updateObjectPosition(int objectId, const Position3D& position);
    
    // Bed channels (static speaker feeds)
    void setBedInput(int channel, const SpeakerLayout::Speaker& speaker);
    
    // Processing
    void processObject(int objectId, const float* input, int numFrames);
    void processBed(const float* const* inputs, int numChannels, int numFrames);
    void render(float* const* outputs, int numFrames);
    
    // Metadata
    struct RenderMetadata {
        int objectCount;
        std::vector<Position3D> objectPositions;
        float lfeLevel;
        float dialogLevel;
        double timestamp;
    };
    RenderMetadata getMetadata() const;
    
    // ADM (Audio Definition Model) export
    Result<void> exportADM(const std::string& path);
    Result<void> exportDolbyAtmos(const std::string& path);  // .atmos file
    
    // Re-render
    void setReRenderMode(bool enabled);
    void setReRenderLayout(const SpeakerLayout& layout);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Binaural processor with HRTF
 */
class MAESTRO_API BinauralProcessor {
public:
    BinauralProcessor();
    ~BinauralProcessor();
    
    // Initialization
    Result<void> initialize(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize);
    
    // HRTF loading
    Result<void> loadHRTF(const std::string& path);  // SOFA format
    Result<void> loadDefaultHRTF();
    std::vector<std::string> getAvailableHRTFs() const;
    void setHRTFInterpolation(bool enabled);
    
    // Single source spatialization
    void process(const float* monoInput, float* leftOutput, float* rightOutput,
                 int numFrames, float azimuth, float elevation, 
                 float distance = 1.0f);
    
    // Multiple sources
    void processMultiple(const std::vector<const float*>& inputs,
                         const std::vector<Position3D>& positions,
                         float* leftOutput, float* rightOutput,
                         int numFrames);
    
    // Room simulation
    void enableRoomSimulation(bool enabled);
    void setRoomSize(float width, float depth, float height);
    void setRoomMaterials(float absorption, float diffusion);
    void setReflectionOrder(int order);  // Number of reflection iterations
    
    // ITD/ILD
    void setITDEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setILDEnabled(bool enabled);
    
    // Near-field
    void setNearFieldEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setNearFieldDistance(float distance);
    
    // Head tracking
    void setHeadTrackingEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setHeadOrientation(float yaw, float pitch, float roll);
    
    // Crossfeed (for speaker to headphone)
    void enableCrossfeed(bool enabled);
    void setCrossfeedLevel(float level);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Audio panner for spatial positioning
 */
class MAESTRO_API SpatialPanner {
public:
    SpatialPanner();
    ~SpatialPanner();
    
    // Algorithm
    enum class Algorithm {
        VBAP,        // Vector Base Amplitude Panning
        DBAP,        // Distance-Based Amplitude Panning
        VBIP,        // Vector Base Intensity Panning
        Ambisonics,  // HOA-based
        Binaural     // HRTF-based
    };
    
    void setAlgorithm(Algorithm algorithm);
    Algorithm getAlgorithm() const;
    
    // Speaker setup
    void setSpeakerLayout(const SpeakerLayout& layout);
    
    // Panning
    void pan(const float* monoInput, float* const* outputs,
             int numFrames, const Position3D& position);
    
    void panStereo(const float* leftInput, const float* rightInput,
                   float* const* outputs, int numFrames,
                   const Position3D& position, float width = 0.0f);
    
    // Automation
    void panWithPath(const float* monoInput, float* const* outputs,
                     int numFrames,
                     const std::vector<std::pair<int, Position3D>>& path);
    
    // Focus/spread
    void setSpread(float spread);  // 0 = point source, 1 = full sphere
    void setFocus(float focus);    // Source directivity
    
    // Distance simulation
    void setDistanceModel(AudioObject::Attenuation model);
    void setReferenceDistance(float distance);
    void setMaxDistance(float distance);
    void setRolloffFactor(float factor);
    
    // Air absorption
    void setAirAbsorption(bool enabled);
    void setAirAbsorptionHF(float coeff);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Spatial reverb
 */
class MAESTRO_API SpatialReverb {
public:
    SpatialReverb();
    ~SpatialReverb();
    
    void initialize(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize);
    
    // Room geometry
    void setRoomDimensions(float width, float depth, float height);
    void setListenerPosition(const Position3D& position);
    
    // Surface materials
    struct Material {
        std::string name;
        std::array<float, 6> absorption;  // Per frequency band
        std::array<float, 6> scattering;
    };
    void setWallMaterial(int wall, const Material& material);
    
    // Reverb parameters
    void setRT60(float rt60);
    void setEarlyReflections(float level);
    void setLateReverb(float level);
    void setPreDelay(float ms);
    void setDiffusion(float diffusion);
    void setModulation(float rate, float depth);
    
    // Processing
    void process(const float* input, float* const* outputs,
                 int numFrames, const Position3D& sourcePosition);
    
    // Ambisonics output
    void processAmbisonic(const float* input, float* ambiOutput,
                          int numFrames, const Position3D& sourcePosition,
                          Ambisonics::Order order);
    
    // Impulse response
    std::vector<std::vector<float>> generateImpulseResponse(
        const Position3D& sourcePosition, const Position3D& listenerPosition,
        float duration = 2.0f);
    
    // Presets
    void loadPreset(const std::string& presetName);
    static std::vector<std::string> getPresetNames();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};
```

## Integration Points

All Phase 3 modules integrate with existing Phase 1 & 2 systems:
- ML generators connect to MIDI/Style engines
- Cloud library integrates with Voice/Sampler engines
- Video sync uses existing transport/sequencer
- Notation connects to MIDI file/sequencer
- Controllers map to mixer/effects/transport
- Spatial audio plugs into audio engine/mixer

```cpp
// include/maestro/ai/ai_mixing.hpp
#pragma once

/**
 * @brief Audio feature extraction for AI analysis
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioFeatureExtractor {
public:
    AudioFeatureExtractor();
    ~AudioFeatureExtractor();
    
    void prepare(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize);
    
    // Feature types
    struct SpectralFeatures {
        std::vector<float> spectrum;           // Magnitude spectrum
        std::vector<float> melSpectrum;        // Mel-scaled spectrum
        std::vector<float> mfcc;               // Mel-frequency cepstral coefficients
        float spectralCentroid;                // Brightness
        float spectralSpread;                  // Width
        float spectralFlux;                    // Change over time
        float spectralRolloff;                 // High-frequency cutoff
        float spectralFlatness;                // Tonality vs noise
        float spectralContrast;                // Peak vs valley
        std::vector<float> chromagram;         // Pitch class distribution
    };
    
    struct DynamicFeatures {
        float rmsLevel;
        float peakLevel;
        float crestFactor;
        float dynamicRange;
        float loudnessLUFS;
        float loudnessLRA;                     // Loudness range
        float truePeak;
        std::vector<float> envelope;
        std::vector<float> onsetStrength;
    };
    
    struct TemporalFeatures {
        double estimatedTempo;
        float tempoConfidence;
        std::vector<float> beatPositions;
        std::vector<float> downbeatPositions;
        float groove;                          // Swing/feel
        std::vector<float> rhythmPattern;
    };
    
    struct TimbralFeatures {
        float brightness;
        float warmth;
        float presence;
        float airiness;
        float muddiness;
        float harshness;
        float punchiness;
        float fullness;
        std::vector<float> harmonicContent;
        std::vector<float> noiseContent;
    };
    
    // Extraction
    SpectralFeatures extractSpectral(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    DynamicFeatures extractDynamic(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    TemporalFeatures extractTemporal(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    TimbralFeatures extractTimbral(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Full analysis
    struct AudioAnalysis {
        SpectralFeatures spectral;
        DynamicFeatures dynamic;
        TemporalFeatures temporal;
        TimbralFeatures timbral;
        
        // Classification
        std::string predictedGenre;
        std::string predictedInstrument;
        float instrumentConfidence;
        std::vector<std::pair<std::string, float>> genreProbabilities;
    };
    
    AudioAnalysis analyzeAudio(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    AudioAnalysis analyzeFile(const std::string& filePath);
    
    // Real-time analysis
    void processBlock(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    SpectralFeatures getCurrentSpectral() const;
    DynamicFeatures getCurrentDynamic() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief AI-powered mix analysis

class MAESTRO_API MixAnalyzer {
public:
    MixAnalyzer();
    ~MixAnalyzer();
    
    Result<void> loadModels(const std::string& modelsPath);
    
    // Mix analysis
    struct MixAnalysis {
        // Overall quality
        float overallScore;                    // 0-100
        float productionQuality;
        float mixBalance;
        float masteringReadiness;
        
        // Frequency balance
        struct FrequencyBalance {
            float subBass;      // 20-60 Hz
            float bass;         // 60-250 Hz
            float lowMid;       // 250-500 Hz
            float mid;          // 500-2000 Hz
            float highMid;      // 2000-4000 Hz
            float presence;     // 4000-8000 Hz
            float brilliance;   // 8000-20000 Hz
            
            std::string assessment;
            std::vector<std::string> issues;
        };
        FrequencyBalance frequencyBalance;
        
        // Stereo image
        struct StereoAnalysis {
            float width;
            float balance;                     // L/R balance
            float correlation;                 // Phase correlation
            float monoCompatibility;
            std::vector<std::pair<float, float>> stereoField;  // Freq, width
            std::string assessment;
        };
        StereoAnalysis stereo;
        
        // Dynamics
        struct DynamicsAnalysis {
            float dynamicRange;
            float compression;
            float transientPreservation;
            float punchiness;
            std::string assessment;
        };
        DynamicsAnalysis dynamics;
        
        // Loudness
        struct LoudnessAnalysis {
            float integratedLUFS;
            float shortTermMax;
            float momentaryMax;
            float truePeakdB;
            float loudnessRange;
            std::string targetCompliance;      // "Spotify", "Apple Music", etc.
            std::map<std::string, bool> platformCompliance;
        };
        LoudnessAnalysis loudness;
        
        // Issues detected
        struct Issue {
            enum class Severity { Info, Warning, Error };
            Severity severity;
            std::string category;
            std::string description;
            std::string suggestion;
            double timeStart;
            double timeEnd;
            std::vector<int> affectedTracks;
        };
        std::vector<Issue> issues;
        
        // Suggestions
        struct Suggestion {
            std::string category;
            std::string description;
            float priority;                    // 0-1
            std::string action;
            std::map<std::string, float> parameters;
        };
        std::vector<Suggestion> suggestions;
    };
    
    MixAnalysis analyzeMix(const studio::Project& project);
    MixAnalysis analyzeMixdown(const std::string& audioPath);
    
    // Track-level analysis
    struct TrackAnalysis {
        int trackIndex;
        std::string trackName;
        std::string instrumentType;
        
        float levelContribution;
        float frequencyOccupancy;
        float stereoPosition;
        
        std::vector<int> conflictingTracks;
        std::vector<std::string> suggestions;
    };
    std::vector<TrackAnalysis> analyzeIndividualTracks(const studio::Project& project);
    
    // Reference comparison
    struct ReferenceComparison {
        std::string referenceName;
        float similarityScore;
        
        std::map<std::string, float> frequencyDifferences;
        std::map<std::string, float> dynamicDifferences;
        float loudnessDifference;
        float stereoDifference;
        
        std::vector<std::string> suggestions;
    };
    ReferenceComparison compareToReference(const std::string& mixPath,
                                            const std::string& referencePath);
    
    // Genre-specific analysis
    void setTargetGenre(const std::string& genre);
    std::vector<std::string> getSupportedGenres() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

        std::string targetVibe;                // "punchy", "warm", "clean", etc.

            float compRatio;
            float compAttack;
            float compRelease;
            float compMakeup;
            
            // Other
            float reverbSend;
            float delaySend;
            std::string explanation;
        };
        std::vector<TrackSettings> trackSettings;
        
        // Master settings
        struct MasterSettings {
            std::vector<EQBand> eq;
            float compThreshold;
            float compRatio;
            float limiterCeiling;
            std::string explanation;
        };
        MasterSettings master;
        
        float predictedLoudness;
        float confidenceScore;
    };

                          const MixSettings& settings);
    
    // Apply mix to project
    void applyMix(studio::Project& project, const MixResult& result);

    struct LiveSuggestion {

        std::string processingStyle;
        float intensity = 0.5f;
    };
    
    MixResult::TrackSettings processStem(const float* audio, int numSamples,
                                          const StemMixSettings& settings);
    
    // Learn from user decisions
    void recordUserDecision(const std::string& suggestionId, bool accepted);
    void trainFromProject(const studio::Project& project);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

```

```cpp
// src/ai/ai_mixing.cpp
#include "maestro/ai/ai_mixing.hpp"
#include "maestro/ml/ml_engine.hpp"
#include <algorithm>
#include <cmath>
#include <numeric>

namespace maestro::ai {

class AudioFeatureExtractor::Impl {
public:
    SampleRate sampleRate = 44100;
    BufferSize bufferSize = 2048;
    int hopSize = 512;
    int melBands = 128;
    int mfccCoeffs = 13;
    
    // FFT
    std::unique_ptr<dsp::FFTProcessor> fft;
    std::vector<float> window;
    std::vector<float> fftBuffer;
    std::vector<std::complex<float>> spectrum;
    
    // Mel filterbank
    std::vector<std::vector<float>> melFilterbank;
    
    // Feature buffers for smoothing
    std::vector<float> previousSpectrum;
    float previousRMS = 0.0f;
    
    void initMelFilterbank() {
        melFilterbank.resize(melBands);
        
        float fMin = 20.0f;
        float fMax = sampleRate / 2.0f;
        
        // Convert to mel scale
        auto hzToMel = [](float hz) { return 2595.0f * std::log10(1.0f + hz / 700.0f); };
        auto melToHz = [](float mel) { return 700.0f * (std::pow(10.0f, mel / 2595.0f) - 1.0f); };
        
        float melMin = hzToMel(fMin);
        float melMax = hzToMel(fMax);
        
        std::vector<float> melPoints(melBands + 2);
        for (int i = 0; i < melBands + 2; ++i) {
            melPoints[i] = melToHz(melMin + (melMax - melMin) * i / (melBands + 1));
        }
        
        int fftBins = bufferSize / 2 + 1;
        for (int m = 0; m < melBands; ++m) {
            melFilterbank[m].resize(fftBins, 0.0f);
            
            float fLeft = melPoints[m];
            float fCenter = melPoints[m + 1];
            float fRight = melPoints[m + 2];
            
            for (int k = 0; k < fftBins; ++k) {
                float freq = static_cast<float>(k) * sampleRate / bufferSize;
                
                if (freq >= fLeft && freq <= fCenter) {
                    melFilterbank[m][k] = (freq - fLeft) / (fCenter - fLeft);
                } else if (freq > fCenter && freq <= fRight) {
                    melFilterbank[m][k] = (fRight - freq) / (fRight - fCenter);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    std::vector<float> computeMelSpectrum(const std::vector<float>& powerSpectrum) {
        std::vector<float> melSpectrum(melBands);
        
        for (int m = 0; m < melBands; ++m) {
            float sum = 0.0f;
            for (size_t k = 0; k < powerSpectrum.size(); ++k) {
                sum += powerSpectrum[k] * melFilterbank[m][k];
            }
            melSpectrum[m] = sum > 0 ? std::log(sum + 1e-10f) : -10.0f;
        }
        
        return melSpectrum;
    }
    
    std::vector<float> computeMFCC(const std::vector<float>& melSpectrum) {
        std::vector<float> mfcc(mfccCoeffs);
        
        // DCT-II
        for (int i = 0; i < mfccCoeffs; ++i) {
            float sum = 0.0f;
            for (int j = 0; j < melBands; ++j) {
                sum += melSpectrum[j] * std::cos(M_PI * i * (2 * j + 1) / (2 * melBands));
            }
            mfcc[i] = sum * std::sqrt(2.0f / melBands);
        }
        
        return mfcc;
    }
    
    float computeSpectralCentroid(const std::vector<float>& spectrum) {
        float weightedSum = 0.0f;
        float totalMag = 0.0f;
        
        for (size_t i = 0; i < spectrum.size(); ++i) {
            float freq = static_cast<float>(i) * sampleRate / bufferSize;
            weightedSum += freq * spectrum[i];
            totalMag += spectrum[i];
        }
        
        return totalMag > 0 ? weightedSum / totalMag : 0.0f;
    }
    
    float computeSpectralFlux(const std::vector<float>& spectrum) {
        if (previousSpectrum.empty()) {
            previousSpectrum = spectrum;
            return 0.0f;
        }
        
        float flux = 0.0f;
        for (size_t i = 0; i < spectrum.size(); ++i) {
            float diff = spectrum[i] - previousSpectrum[i];
            flux += diff > 0 ? diff * diff : 0.0f;
        }
        
        previousSpectrum = spectrum;
        return std::sqrt(flux);
    }
    
    float computeSpectralRolloff(const std::vector<float>& spectrum, 
                                  float percentage = 0.85f) {
        float totalEnergy = 0.0f;
        for (float s : spectrum) totalEnergy += s * s;
        
        float threshold = totalEnergy * percentage;
        float cumulative = 0.0f;
        
        for (size_t i = 0; i < spectrum.size(); ++i) {
            cumulative += spectrum[i] * spectrum[i];
            if (cumulative >= threshold) {
                return static_cast<float>(i) * sampleRate / bufferSize;
            }
        }
        
        return sampleRate / 2.0f;
    }
    
    float computeSpectralFlatness(const std::vector<float>& spectrum) {
        float logSum = 0.0f;
        float linearSum = 0.0f;
        int count = 0;
        
        for (float s : spectrum) {
            if (s > 1e-10f) {
                logSum += std::log(s);
                linearSum += s;
                count++;
            }
        }
        
        if (count == 0) return 0.0f;
        
        float geometricMean = std::exp(logSum / count);
        float arithmeticMean = linearSum / count;
        
        return geometricMean / (arithmeticMean + 1e-10f);
    }
    
    std::vector<float> computeChromagram(const std::vector<float>& spectrum) {
        std::vector<float> chromagram(12, 0.0f);
        
        for (size_t i = 1; i < spectrum.size(); ++i) {
            float freq = static_cast<float>(i) * sampleRate / bufferSize;
            if (freq < 20.0f || freq > 5000.0f) continue;
            
            // Convert to MIDI note and then to pitch class
            float midiNote = 69.0f + 12.0f * std::log2(freq / 440.0f);
            int pitchClass = static_cast<int>(std::round(midiNote)) % 12;
            if (pitchClass < 0) pitchClass += 12;
            
            chromagram[pitchClass] += spectrum[i] * spectrum[i];
        }
        
        // Normalize
        float maxVal = *std::max_element(chromagram.begin(), chromagram.end());
        if (maxVal > 0) {
            for (float& c : chromagram) c /= maxVal;
        }
        
        return chromagram;
    }
};

AudioFeatureExtractor::AudioFeatureExtractor() : impl_(std::make_unique<Impl>()) {}
AudioFeatureExtractor::~AudioFeatureExtractor() = default;

void AudioFeatureExtractor::prepare(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize) {
    impl_->sampleRate = sampleRate;
    impl_->bufferSize = bufferSize;
    impl_->fft = std::make_unique<dsp::FFTProcessor>(bufferSize);
    
    // Create Hann window
    impl_->window.resize(bufferSize);
    for (int i = 0; i < bufferSize; ++i) {
        impl_->window[i] = 0.5f * (1.0f - std::cos(2.0f * M_PI * i / (bufferSize - 1)));
    }
    
    impl_->fftBuffer.resize(bufferSize);
    impl_->spectrum.resize(bufferSize / 2 + 1);
    impl_->initMelFilterbank();
}

AudioFeatureExtractor::SpectralFeatures AudioFeatureExtractor::extractSpectral(
    const float* samples, int numSamples) {
    
    SpectralFeatures features;
    
    // Apply window and compute FFT
    for (int i = 0; i < impl_->bufferSize && i < numSamples; ++i) {
        impl_->fftBuffer[i] = samples[i] * impl_->window[i];
    }
    
    impl_->fft->process(impl_->fftBuffer.data(), impl_->spectrum.data());
    
    // Compute magnitude spectrum
    features.spectrum.resize(impl_->spectrum.size());
    for (size_t i = 0; i < impl_->spectrum.size(); ++i) {
        features.spectrum[i] = std::abs(impl_->spectrum[i]);
    }
    
    // Mel spectrum and MFCC
    features.melSpectrum = impl_->computeMelSpectrum(features.spectrum);
    features.mfcc = impl_->computeMFCC(features.melSpectrum);
    
    // Spectral features
    features.spectralCentroid = impl_->computeSpectralCentroid(features.spectrum);
    features.spectralFlux = impl_->computeSpectralFlux(features.spectrum);
    features.spectralRolloff = impl_->computeSpectralRolloff(features.spectrum);
    features.spectralFlatness = impl_->computeSpectralFlatness(features.spectrum);
    
    // Spread (variance around centroid)
    float variance = 0.0f;
    float totalMag = 0.0f;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < features.spectrum.size(); ++i) {
        float freq = static_cast<float>(i) * impl_->sampleRate / impl_->bufferSize;
        float diff = freq - features.spectralCentroid;
        variance += diff * diff * features.spectrum[i];
        totalMag += features.spectrum[i];
    }
    features.spectralSpread = totalMag > 0 ? std::sqrt(variance / totalMag) : 0.0f;
    
    // Chromagram
    features.chromagram = impl_->computeChromagram(features.spectrum);
    
    return features;
}

AudioFeatureExtractor::DynamicFeatures AudioFeatureExtractor::extractDynamic(
    const float* samples, int numSamples) {
    
    DynamicFeatures features;
    
    // RMS and peak
    float sumSquares = 0.0f;
    float peak = 0.0f;
    
    for (int i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        float absVal = std::abs(samples[i]);
        sumSquares += samples[i] * samples[i];
        peak = std::max(peak, absVal);
    }
    
    features.rmsLevel = std::sqrt(sumSquares / numSamples);
    features.peakLevel = peak;
    features.crestFactor = peak / (features.rmsLevel + 1e-10f);
    
    // Convert to dB
    float rmsDB = 20.0f * std::log10(features.rmsLevel + 1e-10f);
    float peakDB = 20.0f * std::log10(peak + 1e-10f);
    features.dynamicRange = peakDB - rmsDB;
    
    // Simple LUFS approximation (proper implementation would need K-weighting)
    features.loudnessLUFS = rmsDB - 0.691f;  // Simplified
    
    // Envelope
    features.envelope.resize(numSamples / impl_->hopSize);
    for (size_t i = 0; i < features.envelope.size(); ++i) {
        int start = i * impl_->hopSize;
        int end = std::min(start + impl_->hopSize, numSamples);
        
        float localRMS = 0.0f;
        for (int j = start; j < end; ++j) {
            localRMS += samples[j] * samples[j];
        }
        features.envelope[i] = std::sqrt(localRMS / (end - start));
    }
    
    // Onset strength (derivative of envelope)
    features.onsetStrength.resize(features.envelope.size());
    for (size_t i = 1; i < features.envelope.size(); ++i) {
        float diff = features.envelope[i] - features.envelope[i - 1];
        features.onsetStrength[i] = std::max(0.0f, diff);
    }
    features.onsetStrength[0] = 0.0f;
    
    return features;
}

AudioFeatureExtractor::TimbralFeatures AudioFeatureExtractor::extractTimbral(
    const float* samples, int numSamples) {
    
    TimbralFeatures features;
    
    auto spectral = extractSpectral(samples, numSamples);
    
    // Frequency bands for timbral analysis
    auto getEnergyInRange = [&](float lowHz, float highHz) {
        float energy = 0.0f;
        int lowBin = static_cast<int>(lowHz * impl_->bufferSize / impl_->sampleRate);
        int highBin = static_cast<int>(highHz * impl_->bufferSize / impl_->sampleRate);
        
        for (int i = lowBin; i <= highBin && i < static_cast<int>(spectral.spectrum.size()); ++i) {
            energy += spectral.spectrum[i] * spectral.spectrum[i];
        }
        return energy;
    };
    
    float totalEnergy = getEnergyInRange(20, impl_->sampleRate / 2);
    
    // Timbral descriptors
    features.brightness = getEnergyInRange(4000, 20000) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.warmth = getEnergyInRange(200, 500) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.presence = getEnergyInRange(2000, 5000) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.airiness = getEnergyInRange(8000, 20000) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.muddiness = getEnergyInRange(200, 400) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.harshness = getEnergyInRange(2500, 5000) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.fullness = getEnergyInRange(100, 1000) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    features.punchiness = getEnergyInRange(60, 200) / (totalEnergy + 1e-10f);
    
    return features;
}

AudioFeatureExtractor::AudioAnalysis AudioFeatureExtractor::analyzeAudio(
    const float* samples, int numSamples) {
    
    AudioAnalysis analysis;
    analysis.spectral = extractSpectral(samples, numSamples);
    analysis.dynamic = extractDynamic(samples, numSamples);
    analysis.timbral = extractTimbral(samples, numSamples);
    analysis.temporal = extractTemporal(samples, numSamples);
    
    return analysis;
}

// MixAnalyzer implementation
class MixAnalyzer::Impl {

    std::shared_ptr<ml::MLModel> genreModel;
    AudioFeatureExtractor featureExtractor;

            {"brilliance", 0.05f}, {"loudness", -12.0f}

            {"mid", 0.16f}, {"highMid", 0.14f}, {"presence", 0.10f},
            {"brilliance", 0.06f}, {"loudness", -10.0f}
        }},
        {"jazz", {

            {"mid", 0.20f}, {"highMid", 0.16f}, {"presence", 0.11f},
            {"brilliance", 0.06f}, {"loudness", -18.0f}
        }},
        {"classical", {
            {"subBass", 0.08f}, {"bass", 0.15f}, {"lowMid", 0.18f},
            {"mid", 0.22f}, {"highMid", 0.18f}, {"presence", 0.12f},
            {"brilliance", 0.07f}, {"loudness", -23.0f}
        }}
    };
};

MixAnalyzer::MixAnalyzer() : impl_(std::make_unique<Impl>()) {}
MixAnalyzer::~MixAnalyzer() = default;

Result<void> MixAnalyzer::loadModels(const std::string& modelsPath) {
    try {
        impl_->analysisModel = ml::MLEngine::instance().loadModel(
            modelsPath + "/mix_analysis.onnx");
        impl_->genreModel = ml::MLEngine::instance().loadModel(
            modelsPath + "/genre_classifier.onnx");
        
        impl_->featureExtractor.prepare(44100, 2048);
        
        return Result<void>();
    } catch (const std::exception& e) {
        return Result<void>(std::string("Failed to load models: ") + e.what());
    }
}

MixAnalyzer::MixAnalysis MixAnalyzer::analyzeMixdown(const std::string& audioPath) {
    MixAnalysis analysis;
    
    // Load audio file
    // ... (audio loading code)
    
    // For now, simulate with placeholder values
    // In real implementation, this would analyze the actual audio
    
    analysis.overallScore = 75.0f;
    analysis.productionQuality = 0.78f;
    analysis.mixBalance = 0.72f;
    analysis.masteringReadiness = 0.80f;
    
    // Frequency balance
    analysis.frequencyBalance.subBass = 0.14f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.bass = 0.21f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.lowMid = 0.19f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.mid = 0.17f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.highMid = 0.14f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.presence = 0.10f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.brilliance = 0.05f;
    analysis.frequencyBalance.assessment = "Slightly bass-heavy";
    
    // Compare to genre targets
    if (impl_->genreTargets.count(impl_->targetGenre)) {
        auto& targets = impl_->genreTargets[impl_->targetGenre];
        
        if (std::abs(analysis.frequencyBalance.bass - targets["bass"]) > 0.05f) {
            analysis.frequencyBalance.issues.push_back("Bass level differs from genre target");
        }
    }
    
    // Stereo analysis
    analysis.stereo.width = 0.75f;
    analysis.stereo.balance = 0.02f;  // Slight right bias
    analysis.stereo.correlation = 0.85f;
    analysis.stereo.monoCompatibility = 0.92f;
    analysis.stereo.assessment = "Good stereo image with minor balance issue";
    
    // Dynamics
    analysis.dynamics.dynamicRange = 8.5f;
    analysis.dynamics.compression = 0.65f;
    analysis.dynamics.transientPreservation = 0.78f;
    analysis.dynamics.punchiness = 0.70f;
    analysis.dynamics.assessment = "Moderately compressed, good transients";
    
    // Loudness
    analysis.loudness.integratedLUFS = -13.5f;
    analysis.loudness.shortTermMax = -10.2f;
    analysis.loudness.momentaryMax = -8.1f;
    analysis.loudness.truePeakdB = -0.8f;
    analysis.loudness.loudnessRange = 6.2f;
    
    analysis.loudness.platformCompliance = {
        {"Spotify", analysis.loudness.integratedLUFS >= -14.0f},
        {"Apple Music", analysis.loudness.integratedLUFS >= -16.0f},
        {"YouTube", analysis.loudness.integratedLUFS >= -14.0f},
        {"CD", true}
    };
    
    // Generate issues
    if (analysis.loudness.truePeakdB > -1.0f) {
        MixAnalysis::Issue issue;
        issue.severity = MixAnalysis::Issue::Severity::Warning;
        issue.category = "Loudness";
        issue.description = "True peak is close to 0 dBTP";
        issue.suggestion = "Add 0.5 dB headroom to prevent inter-sample peaks";
        analysis.issues.push_back(issue);
    }
    
    if (analysis.stereo.correlation < 0.5f) {
        MixAnalysis::Issue issue;
        issue.severity = MixAnalysis::Issue::Severity::Warning;
        issue.category = "Stereo";
        issue.description = "Low stereo correlation - potential phase issues";
        issue.suggestion = "Check for phase-inverted tracks or excessive stereo widening";
        analysis.issues.push_back(issue);
    }
    
    // Generate suggestions
    MixAnalysis::Suggestion suggestion;
    suggestion.category = "EQ";
    suggestion.description = "Consider a slight cut in the low-mids around 300Hz";
    suggestion.priority = 0.7f;
    suggestion.action = "Apply parametric EQ cut";
    suggestion.parameters = {{"frequency", 300.0f}, {"gain", -2.0f}, {"q", 1.5f}};
    analysis.suggestions.push_back(suggestion);
    
    return analysis;
}

void MixAnalyzer::setTargetGenre(const std::string& genre) {
    impl_->targetGenre = genre;
}

std::vector<std::string> MixAnalyzer::getSupportedGenres() const {
    std::vector<std::string> genres;
    for (const auto& [genre, _] : impl_->genreTargets) {
        genres.push_back(genre);
    }
    return genres;
}
```

```cpp
// include/maestro/analysis/audio_analysis.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <complex>

namespace maestro::analysis {

/**
 * @brief High-resolution spectrum analyzer
 */
class MAESTRO_API SpectrumAnalyzer {
public:
    SpectrumAnalyzer();
    ~SpectrumAnalyzer();
    
    void initialize(SampleRate sampleRate, int fftSize = 4096);
    
    // Configuration
    void setFFTSize(int size);
    void setOverlap(float overlap);  // 0-1
    void setWindow(dsp::FFTProcessor::Window window);
    void setAveraging(int frames);
    
    // Analysis modes
    enum class Mode {
        Linear,
        Logarithmic,
        Mel,
        Bark,
        ERB,              // Equivalent Rectangular Bandwidth
        ThirdOctave,
        Octave
    };
    void setMode(Mode mode);
    
    // Process
    void process(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    void processBlock(const float* left, const float* right, int numSamples);
    
    // Get results
    struct SpectrumData {
        std::vector<float> magnitudes;     // dB
        std::vector<float> phases;         // Radians
        std::vector<float> frequencies;    // Hz
        std::vector<std::complex<float>> complex;
        float peakFrequency;
        float peakMagnitude;
        float spectralCentroid;
    };
    
    SpectrumData getSpectrum() const;
    SpectrumData getStereoSpectrum(int channel) const;  // 0=L, 1=R, 2=M, 3=S
    
    // Band analysis
    float getMagnitudeAtFrequency(float hz) const;
    float getAverageInRange(float lowHz, float highHz) const;
    std::vector<float> getBandMagnitudes(int numBands) const;
    
    // Peak detection
    struct Peak {
        float frequency;
        float magnitude;
        float bandwidth;
        bool isHarmonic;
        int harmonicNumber;
    };
    std::vector<Peak> findPeaks(float threshold = -60.0f, int maxPeaks = 20);
    
    // Harmonic analysis
    struct HarmonicAnalysis {
        float fundamental;
        std::vector<float> harmonicFrequencies;
        std::vector<float> harmonicAmplitudes;
        float inharmonicity;
        float harmonicToNoiseRatio;
    };
    HarmonicAnalysis analyzeHarmonics(float fundamentalHint = 0.0f);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

        Hot,

    };
    void setColorMap(ColorMap map);

        std::vector<float> times;
        std::vector<float> frequencies;
        int width;
        int height;

    };
    
    Spectrogram generate(const float* samples, int numSamples);

    // Reassigned spectrogram (better time-frequency resolution)

    // Chromagram

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**

/**
 * @brief AI-powered stem separation
 */
class MAESTRO_API StemSeparator {
public:
    StemSeparator();
    ~StemSeparator();
    
    Result<void> loadModel(const std::string& modelPath);
    bool isReady() const;
    
    // Stem types
    enum class StemType {
        Vocals,
        Drums,
        Bass,
        Other,
        Piano,
        Guitar,
        Strings,
        Brass,
        Woodwinds,
        Synth
    };
    
    // Configuration
    struct SeparationConfig {
        std::vector<StemType> stemsToExtract;
        bool highQuality = true;
        int overlap = 4;                    // Overlap factor for processing
        float softMask = 0.0f;              // 0=hard mask, 1=soft mask
        bool preserveResidual = true;       // Keep "other" stem
    };
    
    // Separation
    struct SeparationResult {
        std::map<StemType, std::vector<float>> stems;  // Mono for each stem
        std::map<StemType, std::vector<std::vector<float>>> stereoStems;  // Stereo
        std::vector<float> residual;
        float processingTime;
        float qualityEstimate;
    };
    
    std::future<SeparationResult> separate(
        const float* left, const float* right, int numSamples,
        const SeparationConfig& config);
    
    std::future<SeparationResult> separateFile(
        const std::string& inputPath,
        const SeparationConfig& config);
    
    // Export separated stems
    Result<void> exportStems(
        const SeparationResult& result,
        const std::string& outputDir,
        const std::string& baseName,
        SampleRate sampleRate);
    
    // Real-time separation (lower quality but fast)
    void initializeRealtime(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize);
    void processRealtime(const float* left, const float* right,
                         float* outputLeft, float* outputRight,
                         int numSamples, StemType targetStem);
    
    // Progress callback
    using ProgressCallback = std::function<void(float progress, 
                                                 const std::string& status)>;
    void setProgressCallback(ProgressCallback callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Audio quality analyzer
 */
class MAESTRO_API QualityAnalyzer {
public:
    QualityAnalyzer();
    ~QualityAnalyzer();
    
    void initialize(SampleRate sampleRate);
    
    // Clipping detection
    struct ClippingReport {
        int clipCount;
        std::vector<double> clipPositions;  // In seconds
        float clipPercentage;
        float maxSampleValue;
        bool hasInterSamplePeaks;
    };
    ClippingReport detectClipping(const float* samples, int numSamples,
                                   float threshold = 0.99f);
    
    // Noise analysis
    struct NoiseReport {
        float noiseFloor;                   // dB
        float signalToNoiseRatio;           // dB
        std::vector<float> noiseSpectrum;
        bool has60HzHum;
        bool has50HzHum;
        std::vector<float> noiseFrequencies;
    };
    NoiseReport analyzeNoise(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Distortion analysis
    struct DistortionReport {
        float thd;                          // Total Harmonic Distortion %
        float thdPlusNoise;
        std::vector<float> harmonicDistortion;
        float intermodulationDistortion;
        bool hasDigitalClipping;
        bool hasAnalogDistortion;
    };
    DistortionReport analyzeDistortion(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // DC offset
    float detectDCOffset(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Silence detection
    struct SilenceReport {
        std::vector<std::pair<double, double>> silentRegions;  // start, end seconds
        float totalSilencePercent;
    };
    SilenceReport detectSilence(const float* samples, int numSamples,
                                 float threshold = -60.0f, 
                                 float minDuration = 0.5f);
    
    // Sample rate detection
    struct SampleRateReport {
        SampleRate originalSampleRate;
        SampleRate currentSampleRate;
        bool isUpsampled;
        float confidenceScore;
    };
    SampleRateReport detectOriginalSampleRate(const float* samples, int numSamples,
                                               SampleRate currentRate);
    
    // Codec detection
    struct CodecReport {
        std::string likelyCodec;            // "mp3", "aac", "flac", etc.
        int estimatedBitrate;
        float codecArtifactLevel;
        bool isLossless;
        float confidence;
    };
    CodecReport detectCodecArtifacts(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Overall quality score
    struct QualityScore {
        float overall;                      // 0-100
        float dynamicRange;
        float clarity;
        float noiseLevel;
        float distortionLevel;
        std::vector<std::string> issues;
        std::vector<std::string> recommendations;
    };
    QualityScore getOverallQuality(const float* samples, int numSamples);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Musical content analyzer
 */
class MAESTRO_API MusicAnalyzer {
public:
    MusicAnalyzer();
    ~MusicAnalyzer();
    
    Result<void> loadModels(const std::string& modelsPath);
    void initialize(SampleRate sampleRate);
    
    // Tempo and beat
    struct BeatAnalysis {
        double tempo;
        float tempoConfidence;
        std::vector<double> beatTimes;
        std::vector<double> downbeatTimes;
        TimeSignature timeSignature;
        float swingRatio;
        std::vector<float> beatStrengths;
    };
    BeatAnalysis analyzeBeat(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Key detection
    struct KeyAnalysis {
        std::string key;                    // "C", "C#", etc.
        std::string mode;                   // "major", "minor"
        float confidence;
        std::vector<std::pair<std::string, float>> alternatives;
        std::vector<float> chromagram;
        std::vector<std::pair<double, std::string>> keyChanges;  // time, new key
    };
    KeyAnalysis analyzeKey(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Chord detection
    struct ChordAnalysis {
        std::vector<std::pair<double, ChordInfo>> chords;  // time, chord
        std::vector<float> chordConfidences;
        std::string progression;            // Roman numeral analysis
    };
    ChordAnalysis analyzeChords(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Structure analysis
    struct StructureAnalysis {
        struct Section {
            std::string label;              // "intro", "verse", "chorus", etc.
            double startTime;
            double endTime;
            float confidence;
        };
        std::vector<Section> sections;
        
        // Self-similarity matrix
        std::vector<std::vector<float>> similarityMatrix;
        std::vector<double> segmentBoundaries;
    };
    StructureAnalysis analyzeStructure(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Melody extraction
    struct MelodyAnalysis {
        std::vector<std::pair<double, float>> pitchContour;  // time, frequency
        std::vector<midi::NoteEvent> midiNotes;
        float vocalPresence;
        std::vector<std::pair<double, double>> phrases;  // start, end
    };
    MelodyAnalysis extractMelody(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Genre classification
    struct GenreAnalysis {
        std::string primaryGenre;
        float confidence;
        std::vector<std::pair<std::string, float>> genreProbabilities;
        std::vector<std::string> subgenres;
        std::vector<std::string> similarArtists;
    };
    GenreAnalysis classifyGenre(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Mood/emotion analysis
    struct MoodAnalysis {
        float valence;                      // -1 (sad) to 1 (happy)
        float arousal;                      // -1 (calm) to 1 (energetic)
        std::string primaryMood;
        std::vector<std::pair<std::string, float>> moodProbabilities;
        float danceability;
        float energy;
    };
    MoodAnalysis analyzeMood(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Complete analysis
    struct FullAnalysis {
        BeatAnalysis beat;
        KeyAnalysis key;
        ChordAnalysis chords;
        StructureAnalysis structure;
        MelodyAnalysis melody;
        GenreAnalysis genre;
        MoodAnalysis mood;
    };
    FullAnalysis analyzeComplete(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    std::future<FullAnalysis> analyzeCompleteAsync(const float* samples, 
                                                    int numSamples);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::analysis
```

# PHASE 4.3: REAL-TIME COLLABORATION

```cpp
// include/maestro/collaboration/collaboration.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/studio/project.hpp"
#include "maestro/midi/midi_types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <functional>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

namespace maestro::collaboration {

/**
 * @brief User/participant information
 */
struct Participant {
    std::string id;
    std::string displayName;
    std::string avatarUrl;
    QColor color;
    bool isHost;
    bool canEdit;
    bool canRecord;
    bool isMuted;
    
    // Presence
    bool isOnline;
    std::string currentView;              // "arrangement", "mixer", etc.
    int cursorTrack;
    TickCount cursorPosition;
    
    // Audio status
    float inputLevel;
    float outputLevel;
    int latencyMs;
    bool isTransmitting;
};

/**
 * @brief Collaboration session
 */
class MAESTRO_API CollaborationSession {
public:
    CollaborationSession();
    ~CollaborationSession();
    
    // Session creation
    struct SessionConfig {
        std::string name;
        bool isPublic;
        int maxParticipants;
        bool allowAnonymous;
        std::string password;              // Optional
        
        // Permissions
        bool guestsCanEdit;
        bool guestsCanRecord;
        bool guestsCanChat;
        bool guestsCanVoiceChat;
        
        // Audio settings
        SampleRate sampleRate;
        BufferSize bufferSize;
        bool enableAudioStreaming;
        int audioBitrate;                  // kbps
    };
    
    std::future<Result<std::string>> createSession(const SessionConfig& config);
    std::future<Result<void>> joinSession(const std::string& sessionId,
                                           const std::string& password = "");
    void leaveSession();
    bool isInSession() const;
    std::string getSessionId() const;
    
    // Participants
    std::vector<Participant> getParticipants() const;
    Participant getLocalParticipant() const;
    Participant getParticipant(const std::string& id) const;
    
    void setLocalDisplayName(const std::string& name);
    void setLocalColor(const QColor& color);
    
    // Host controls
    void kickParticipant(const std::string& id);
    void banParticipant(const std::string& id);
    void setParticipantPermissions(const std::string& id, bool canEdit, 
                                    bool canRecord);
    void muteParticipant(const std::string& id, bool muted);
    void transferHost(const std::string& newHostId);
    
    // Project sync
    void syncProject(const studio::Project& project);
    std::future<studio::Project> requestFullSync();
    
    // Real-time edits
    struct Edit {
        std::string id;
        std::string participantId;
        std::string type;                  // "note_add", "track_volume", etc.
        std::string targetPath;            // JSON path to target
        std::string data;                  // JSON data
        uint64_t timestamp;
        uint64_t sequenceNumber;
    };
    
    void sendEdit(const Edit& edit);
    
    using EditCallback = std::function<void(const Edit&)>;
    void setEditCallback(EditCallback callback);
    
    // Conflict resolution
    enum class ConflictStrategy {
        LastWriteWins,
        FirstWriteWins,
        Merge,
        AskUser
    };
    void setConflictStrategy(ConflictStrategy strategy);
    
    using ConflictCallback = std::function<Edit(const Edit& local, 
                                                  const Edit& remote)>;
    void setConflictCallback(ConflictCallback callback);
    
    // Cursor/selection sync
    void updateCursorPosition(int track, TickCount position);
    void updateSelection(int track, TickCount start, TickCount end);
    void updateView(const std::string& viewName);
    
    using PresenceCallback = std::function<void(const Participant&)>;
    void setPresenceCallback(PresenceCallback callback);
    
    // Chat
    struct ChatMessage {
        std::string id;
        std::string participantId;
        std::string content;
        uint64_t timestamp;
        bool isSystem;
    };
    
    void sendChatMessage(const std::string& content);
    std::vector<ChatMessage> getChatHistory() const;
    
    using ChatCallback = std::function<void(const ChatMessage&)>;
    void setChatCallback(ChatCallback callback);
    
    // Session state
    using SessionCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& event, 
                                                 const std::string& data)>;
    void setSessionCallback(SessionCallback callback);
    
    // Export session history
    Result<void> exportSessionLog(const std::string& path);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Real-time audio streaming for collaboration
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioStreamManager {
public:
    AudioStreamManager();
    ~AudioStreamManager();
    
    // Initialize
    Result<void> initialize(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize,
                             int numChannels);
    
    // Connect to session
    void connectToSession(CollaborationSession& session);
    void disconnect();
    bool isConnected() const;
    
    // Local audio
    void setInputEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setInputDevice(const std::string& deviceId);
    void setInputGain(float gain);
    void setInputMuted(bool muted);
    
    void setOutputEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setOutputDevice(const std::string& deviceId);
    void setOutputGain(float gain);
    
    // Stream controls
    void startStreaming();
    void stopStreaming();
    bool isStreaming() const;
    
    // Monitoring
    void setMonitoringEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setMonitoringLatency(int samples);
    
    // Per-participant mixing
    void setParticipantVolume(const std::string& id, float volume);
    void setParticipantPan(const std::string& id, float pan);
    void setParticipantMuted(const std::string& id, bool muted);
    void setParticipantSolo(const std::string& id, bool solo);
    
    // Click track for sync
    void enableClickTrack(bool enabled);
    void setClickTrackVolume(float volume);
    
    // Latency compensation
    int getNetworkLatency() const;
    int getTotalLatency() const;
    void setLatencyCompensation(int samples);
    
    // Quality
    enum class Quality { Low, Medium, High, Lossless };
    void setStreamQuality(Quality quality);
    
    // Statistics
    struct StreamStats {
        float uploadBandwidth;             // kbps
        float downloadBandwidth;
        int packetLoss;                    // %
        int jitter;                        // ms
        int roundTripTime;                 // ms
    };
    StreamStats getStats() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief WebRTC-based audio/video transport
 */
class MAESTRO_API WebRTCTransport {
public:
    WebRTCTransport();
    ~WebRTCTransport();
    
    // Initialize
    Result<void> initialize();
    
    // ICE servers
    struct ICEServer {
        std::string url;
        std::string username;
        std::string credential;
    };
    void setICEServers(const std::vector<ICEServer>& servers);
    
    // Connection
    std::future<Result<void>> connect(const std::string& signalingUrl,
                                       const std::string& roomId);
    void disconnect();
    bool isConnected() const;
    
    // Audio tracks
    void addAudioTrack(const std::string& trackId);
    void removeAudioTrack(const std::string& trackId);
    
    void sendAudio(const std::string& trackId, const float* samples,
                   int numSamples, int numChannels);
    
    using AudioCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& peerId,
                                              const std::string& trackId,
                                              const float* samples,
                                              int numSamples,
                                              int numChannels)>;
    void setAudioCallback(AudioCallback callback);
    
    // Data channel
    void sendData(const std::string& channel, const std::vector<uint8_t>& data);
    void sendData(const std::string& channel, const std::string& data);
    
    using DataCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& peerId,
                                             const std::string& channel,
                                             const std::vector<uint8_t>& data)>;
    void setDataCallback(DataCallback callback);
    
    // Peer management
    std::vector<std::string> getConnectedPeers() const;
    
    using PeerCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& peerId, 
                                             bool connected)>;
    void setPeerCallback(PeerCallback callback);
    
    // Quality adaptation
    void setTargetBitrate(int kbps);
    void enableAdaptiveBitrate(bool enabled);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Operational Transform for conflict-free edits
 */
class MAESTRO_API OperationalTransform {
public:
    OperationalTransform();
    ~OperationalTransform();
    
    // Operation types
    struct Operation {
        enum class Type { Insert, Delete, Modify, Move };
        
        Type type;
        std::string path;                  // JSON path
        std::string value;                 // JSON value
        int position;                      // For array operations
        uint64_t timestamp;
        std::string clientId;
        uint64_t sequenceNumber;
        
        std::string serialize() const;
        static Operation deserialize(const std::string& data);
    };
    
    // Transform operations
    std::pair<Operation, Operation> transform(const Operation& op1,
                                               const Operation& op2);
    
    // Apply operation to document
    Result<void> apply(const Operation& op, std::string& document);
    
    // Compose multiple operations
    Operation compose(const std::vector<Operation>& ops);
    
    // History management
    void addToHistory(const Operation& op);
    std::vector<Operation> getHistory(uint64_t since) const;
    void pruneHistory(uint64_t before);
    
    // Undo/redo
    Operation invert(const Operation& op);
    
    // State vector
    std::map<std::string, uint64_t> getStateVector() const;
    bool isUpToDate(const std::map<std::string, uint64_t>& otherState) const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Version control for projects
 */
class MAESTRO_API ProjectVersionControl {
public:
    ProjectVersionControl();
    ~ProjectVersionControl();
    
    // Initialize repository
    Result<void> initRepository(const std::string& projectPath);
    Result<void> cloneRepository(const std::string& remoteUrl,
                                  const std::string& localPath);
    
    // Commits
    struct Commit {
        std::string hash;
        std::string author;
        std::string message;
        uint64_t timestamp;
        std::string parentHash;
        std::vector<std::string> changedFiles;
    };
    
    Result<std::string> commit(const std::string& message);
    std::vector<Commit> getHistory(int limit = 100) const;
    Commit getCommit(const std::string& hash) const;
    
    // Branches
    std::vector<std::string> getBranches() const;
    std::string getCurrentBranch() const;
    Result<void> createBranch(const std::string& name);
    Result<void> switchBranch(const std::string& name);
    Result<void> mergeBranch(const std::string& name);
    Result<void> deleteBranch(const std::string& name);
    
    // Diff
    struct Diff {
        std::string filePath;
        std::string changeType;            // "added", "modified", "deleted"
        std::string oldContent;
        std::string newContent;
    };
    std::vector<Diff> getDiff(const std::string& commitHash1,
                               const std::string& commitHash2);
    std::vector<Diff> getUncommittedChanges();
    
    // Revert
    Result<void> revertToCommit(const std::string& hash);
    Result<void> revertFile(const std::string& filePath, 
                            const std::string& hash);
    
    // Remote
    Result<void> setRemote(const std::string& name, const std::string& url);
    Result<void> push(const std::string& remote = "origin");
    Result<void> pull(const std::string& remote = "origin");
    Result<void> fetch(const std::string& remote = "origin");
    
    // Conflict resolution
    struct Conflict {
        std::string filePath;
        std::string localContent;
        std::string remoteContent;
        std::string baseContent;
    };
    std::vector<Conflict> getConflicts() const;
    Result<void> resolveConflict(const std::string& filePath,
                                  const std::string& resolvedContent);
    
    // Stash
    Result<void> stash(const std::string& message = "");
    Result<void> stashPop();
    std::vector<std::string> getStashList() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Cloud sync for projects
 */
class MAESTRO_API CloudProjectSync {
public:
    CloudProjectSync();
    ~CloudProjectSync();
    
    // Authentication
    std::future<Result<void>> authenticate(const std::string& token);
    void logout();
    bool isAuthenticated() const;
    
    // Project management
    struct CloudProject {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        std::string ownerId;
        std::string ownerName;
        uint64_t createdAt;
        uint64_t updatedAt;
        uint64_t sizeBytes;
        bool isShared;
        std::vector<std::string> collaboratorIds;
    };
    
    std::future<std::vector<CloudProject>> listProjects();
    std::future<Result<CloudProject>> createProject(const std::string& name);
    std::future<Result<void>> deleteProject(const std::string& projectId);
    
    // Sync
    std::future<Result<void>> uploadProject(const std::string& localPath,
                                             const std::string& projectId);
    std::future<Result<void>> downloadProject(const std::string& projectId,
                                               const std::string& localPath);
    
    // Auto-sync
    void enableAutoSync(bool enabled);
    void setAutoSyncInterval(int seconds);
    void syncNow();
    
    using SyncCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& status,
                                             float progress)>;
    void setSyncCallback(SyncCallback callback);
    
    // Sharing
    std::future<Result<void>> shareProject(const std::string& projectId,
                                            const std::string& email,
                                            bool canEdit);
    std::future<Result<void>> unshareProject(const std::string& projectId,
                                              const std::string& userId);
    std::future<std::vector<Participant>> getProjectCollaborators(
        const std::string& projectId);
    
    // Storage
    struct StorageInfo {
        uint64_t usedBytes;
        uint64_t quotaBytes;
        std::vector<std::pair<std::string, uint64_t>> projectSizes;
    };
    std::future<StorageInfo> getStorageInfo();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};
```
