# PHASE 4.4: EXTENDED PLUGIN FORMATS

```cpp
// include/maestro/plugin/ara_host.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/plugin/plugin_host.hpp"
#include "maestro/studio/project.hpp"
#include <memory>

namespace maestro::plugin {

/**
 * @brief ARA (Audio Random Access) host implementation
 */
class MAESTRO_API ARAHost {
public:
    ARAHost();
    ~ARAHost();
    
    // Initialize ARA hosting
    Result<void> initialize();
    
    // Plugin discovery
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getARAPlugins() const;
    bool isARAPlugin(const PluginInfo& info) const;
    
    // Document controller
    class MAESTRO_API ARADocument {
    public:
        // Musical context
        void setMusicalContext(double tempo, int numerator, int denominator);
        void setKeySignature(int root, bool isMinor);
        
        // Region sequences (tracks)
        struct RegionSequence {
            std::string id;
            std::string name;
            QColor color;
            int orderIndex;
        };
        
        std::string addRegionSequence(const RegionSequence& sequence);
        void removeRegionSequence(const std::string& id);
        void updateRegionSequence(const RegionSequence& sequence);
        
        // Audio sources
        struct AudioSource {
            std::string id;
            std::string name;
            std::string filePath;
            int64_t sampleCount;
            SampleRate sampleRate;
            int channelCount;
            double duration;
            bool isPersistent;
        };
        
        std::string addAudioSource(const AudioSource& source);
        void removeAudioSource(const std::string& id);
        void updateAudioSource(const AudioSource& source);
        
        // Audio modifications (regions)
        struct AudioModification {
            std::string id;
            std::string audioSourceId;
            std::string regionSequenceId;
            std::string name;
            double startInSource;            // Seconds
            double durationInSource;
            double startInSequence;
            double durationInSequence;
        };
        
        std::string addAudioModification(const AudioModification& mod);
        void removeAudioModification(const std::string& id);
        void updateAudioModification(const AudioModification& mod);
        
        // Content analysis
        void requestAnalysis(const std::string& audioSourceId);
        bool isAnalysisComplete(const std::string& audioSourceId) const;
        
        // Playback regions
        void setPlaybackRegion(const std::string& modificationId,
                               double startTime, double endTime);
        
        // Store/restore
        std::vector<uint8_t> storeDocument();
        void restoreDocument(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data);
    };
    
    // Create document for project
    std::unique_ptr<ARADocument> createDocument();
    
    // Plugin editor extensions
    struct ARAEditorView {
        void* nativeView;
        int width;
        int height;
        std::string viewType;              // "main", "small", etc.
    };
    
    ARAEditorView createEditorView(PluginInstance& plugin, 
                                    void* parentWindow,
                                    const std::string& viewType = "main");
    void destroyEditorView(ARAEditorView& view);
    
    // Playback rendering
    struct ARAPlaybackRenderer {
        std::string regionSequenceId;
        bool enabled;
    };
    
    std::unique_ptr<ARAPlaybackRenderer> createPlaybackRenderer(
        PluginInstance& plugin,
        const std::string& regionSequenceId);
    
    void processPlayback(ARAPlaybackRenderer& renderer,
                         float* const* outputs,
                         int numChannels,
                         int numSamples,
                         double startTime);
    
    // Editor rendering
    void renderEditorContent(PluginInstance& plugin,
                             float* const* outputs,
                             int numChannels,
                             int numSamples,
                             double startTime);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief CLAP (CLever Audio Plugin) extended host
 */
class MAESTRO_API CLAPHost {
public:
    CLAPHost();
    ~CLAPHost();
    
    Result<void> initialize();
    
    // Plugin discovery
    void addSearchPath(const std::string& path);
    void scanPlugins();
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getCLAPPlugins() const;
    
    // Load plugin
    std::unique_ptr<PluginInstance> loadPlugin(const std::string& path,
                                                const std::string& pluginId);
    
    // CLAP-specific features
    
    // Note expressions
    struct NoteExpression {
        int32_t noteId;
        int16_t portIndex;
        int16_t channel;
        int16_t key;
        uint32_t expressionId;
        double value;
    };
    
    void sendNoteExpression(PluginInstance& plugin, const NoteExpression& expr);
    
    // Note expression types
    enum class ExpressionType {
        Volume,
        Pan,
        Tuning,
        Vibrato,
        Expression,
        Brightness,
        Pressure,
        Custom
    };
    
    std::vector<ExpressionType> getSupportedExpressions(PluginInstance& plugin);
    
    // Per-note automation
    void setNoteAutomation(PluginInstance& plugin, int32_t noteId,
                           int parameterId, double value);
    
    // Voice info
    struct VoiceInfo {
        int32_t voiceId;
        int32_t noteId;
        int16_t channel;
        int16_t key;
        float volume;
        float pan;
        float tuning;
        bool isActive;
    };
    
    std::vector<VoiceInfo> getActiveVoices(PluginInstance& plugin);
    
    // Preset discovery
    struct CLAPPreset {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        std::string category;
        std::string creator;
        std::string description;
        std::vector<std::string> features;
    };
    
    std::vector<CLAPPreset> getPluginPresets(PluginInstance& plugin);
    void loadPreset(PluginInstance& plugin, const std::string& presetId);
    
    // Remote controls
    struct RemoteControlsPage {
        std::string sectionName;
        std::string pageName;
        std::vector<int> parameterIds;
    };
    
    std::vector<RemoteControlsPage> getRemoteControlPages(PluginInstance& plugin);
    
    // Audio ports extension
    struct AudioPortConfig {
        std::string name;
        int channelCount;
        enum Type { Main, Sidechain, Aux } type;
        bool isInput;
    };
    
    std::vector<AudioPortConfig> getAudioPorts(PluginInstance& plugin);
    void setAudioPortActive(PluginInstance& plugin, int portIndex, bool active);
    
    // Note ports extension
    struct NotePortConfig {
        std::string name;
        int preferredDialect;              // CLAP_NOTE_DIALECT_*
        bool supportedDialects;
    };
    
    std::vector<NotePortConfig> getNotePorts(PluginInstance& plugin);
    
    // GUI extensions
    bool supportsFloatingWindow(PluginInstance& plugin);
    void setFloatingWindow(PluginInstance& plugin, bool floating);
    
    bool supportsGUIScaling(PluginInstance& plugin);
    void setGUIScale(PluginInstance& plugin, double scale);
    
    // Thread pool
    void setThreadPool(int numThreads);
    
    // Timer support
    using TimerCallback = std::function<void()>;
    uint32_t registerTimer(PluginInstance& plugin, uint32_t periodMs,
                           TimerCallback callback);
    void unregisterTimer(uint32_t timerId);
    
    // POSIX file descriptor support (Linux)
    using FDCallback = std::function<void(int fd, uint32_t flags)>;
    void registerFD(PluginInstance& plugin, int fd, uint32_t flags,
                    FDCallback callback);
    void unregisterFD(int fd);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Plugin format abstraction layer
 */
class MAESTRO_API UnifiedPluginHost {
public:
    UnifiedPluginHost();
    ~UnifiedPluginHost();
    
    Result<void> initialize();
    
    // Scan all formats
    void scanAllFormats();
    void scanFormat(PluginFormat format);
    
    // Search paths per format
    void addSearchPath(PluginFormat format, const std::string& path);
    void setSearchPaths(PluginFormat format, 
                        const std::vector<std::string>& paths);
    
    // Get all plugins
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getAllPlugins() const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getPluginsByFormat(PluginFormat format) const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> searchPlugins(const std::string& query) const;
    
    // Load (auto-detect format)
    std::unique_ptr<PluginInstance> loadPlugin(const PluginInfo& info);
    std::unique_ptr<PluginInstance> loadPluginById(const std::string& id);
    
    // Format-specific hosts
    plugin::PluginHost& getVST3Host();
    ARAHost& getARAHost();
    CLAPHost& getCLAPHost();
    LV2Host& getLV2Host();
    
    // Plugin database
    void saveDatabase(const std::string& path);
    void loadDatabase(const std::string& path);
    
    // Blacklist
    void addToBlacklist(const std::string& pluginId);
    void removeFromBlacklist(const std::string& pluginId);
    std::vector<std::string> getBlacklist() const;
    
    // Favorites
    void addToFavorites(const std::string& pluginId);
    void removeFromFavorites(const std::string& pluginId);
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getFavorites() const;
    
    // Recent
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getRecentlyUsed(int limit = 20) const;
    
    // Categories
    std::vector<std::string> getCategories() const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getPluginsByCategory(const std::string& cat) const;
    void setPluginCategory(const std::string& pluginId, 
                           const std::string& category);
    
    // User tags
    void setPluginTags(const std::string& pluginId,
                       const std::vector<std::string>& tags);
    std::vector<std::string> getPluginTags(const std::string& pluginId) const;
    std::vector<PluginInfo> getPluginsByTag(const std::string& tag) const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::plugin
```

```cpp
/**

 */
class MAESTRO_API MobileAudioEngine {

    ~MobileAudioEngine();
    
    // Platform-specific initialization
    Result<void> initializeiOS();
    Result<void> initializeAndroid();

        Playback,
        Record,
        PlayAndRecord,
        Ambient,
        SoloAmbient
    };

    void setAllowAirPlay(bool allow);

    void setAndroidSharingMode(int mode);

    ThermalState getThermalState() const;
    
    using ThermalCallback = std::function<void(ThermalState state)>;
    void setThermalCallback(ThermalCallback callback);
    
    void reduceCPUUsage(float factor);  // 0-1, for thermal throttling
    
    // Memory management
    size_t getAvailableMemory() const;
    void setMemoryWarningCallback(std::function<void()> callback);

    void stopBluetoothMIDIScan();

    void disconnectBluetoothMIDI(const std::string& deviceId);

/**
 * @brief Touch-optimized interface helpers
 */
class MAESTRO_API TouchInterface {
public:
    TouchInterface();
    ~TouchInterface();
    
    // Gesture detection
    struct TouchPoint {
        int id;
        float x, y;
        float pressure;
        float size;
        enum Phase { Began, Moved, Ended, Cancelled } phase;
        double timestamp;
    };
    
    void processTouches(const std::vector<TouchPoint>& touches);
    
    // Gesture callbacks
    using TapCallback = std::function<void(float x, float y)>;
    void setTapCallback(TapCallback callback);
    
    using DoubleTapCallback = std::function<void(float x, float y)>;
    void setDoubleTapCallback(DoubleTapCallback callback);
    
    using LongPressCallback = std::function<void(float x, float y)>;
    void setLongPressCallback(LongPressCallback callback);
    
    using PanCallback = std::function<void(float dx, float dy, int fingers)>;
    void setPanCallback(PanCallback callback);
    
    using PinchCallback = std::function<void(float scale, float x, float y)>;
    void setPinchCallback(PinchCallback callback);
    
    using RotateCallback = std::function<void(float angle, float x, float y)>;
    void setRotateCallback(RotateCallback callback);
    
    // Velocity tracking for instruments
    struct VelocityTouch {
        float x, y;
        float velocityX, velocityY;
        float pressure;
        float velocity;  // For musical use
    };
    VelocityTouch getVelocityForTouch(int touchId) const;
    
    // Piano keyboard helpers
    struct KeyboardLayout {
        float x, y;
        float width, height;
        int lowestNote;
        int highestNote;
        float whiteKeyWidth;
        float blackKeyHeight;
    };
    
    void setKeyboardLayout(const KeyboardLayout& layout);
    int touchToMIDINote(float x, float y) const;
    int touchToMIDIVelocity(float y, float pressure) const;
    
    // Pad grid helpers
    struct PadGridLayout {
        float x, y;
        float width, height;
        int rows, cols;
        float padding;
    };
    
    void setPadGridLayout(const PadGridLayout& layout);
    std::pair<int, int> touchToPad(float x, float y) const;
    int touchToPadVelocity(float y, float pressure) const;
    
    // XY Pad helpers
    struct XYPadLayout {
        float x, y;
        float width, height;
        bool bipolarX, bipolarY;
    };
    
    void setXYPadLayout(const XYPadLayout& layout);
    std::pair<float, float> touchToXY(float x, float y) const;
    
    // Haptic feedback
    enum class HapticType { 
        Light, Medium, Heavy, 
        Success, Warning, Error,
        Selection
    };
    void triggerHaptic(HapticType type);
    void setHapticsEnabled(bool enabled);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Adaptive UI for different screen sizes
 */
class MAESTRO_API AdaptiveUI {
public:
    // Device categories
    enum class DeviceType {
        Phone,
        PhoneLarge,
        Tablet,
        TabletLarge,
        Desktop
    };
    
    static DeviceType getDeviceType();
    static bool isTablet();
    static bool isPhone();
    
    // Screen info
    struct ScreenInfo {
        float widthPoints;
        float heightPoints;
        float widthPixels;
        float heightPixels;
        float scale;
        float safeAreaTop;
        float safeAreaBottom;
        float safeAreaLeft;
        float safeAreaRight;
        bool hasNotch;
    };
    
    static ScreenInfo getScreenInfo();
    
    // Layout helpers
    enum class LayoutMode {
        Compact,       // Single column
        Regular,       // Two columns
        Expanded       // Three+ columns
    };
    
    static LayoutMode getLayoutMode();
    
    // Component sizing
    struct ComponentSizes {
        float buttonHeight;
        float sliderHeight;
        float faderWidth;
        float padSize;
        float fontSize;
        float iconSize;
        float spacing;
        float margin;
    };
    
    static ComponentSizes getSizesForDevice();
    
    // Orientation
    enum class Orientation { Portrait, Landscape };
    static Orientation getOrientation();
    
    using OrientationCallback = std::function<void(Orientation)>;
    static void setOrientationCallback(OrientationCallback callback);
    
    // Split view (iPad)
    static bool isSplitView();
    static float getSplitViewWidth();
    
    // Keyboard avoidance
    static float getKeyboardHeight();
    static bool isKeyboardVisible();
    
    using KeyboardCallback = std::function<void(bool visible, float height)>;
    static void setKeyboardCallback(KeyboardCallback callback);
};

/**
 * @brief Battery and performance optimization
 */
class MAESTRO_API PerformanceManager {
public:
    PerformanceManager();
    ~PerformanceManager();
    
    // Battery state
    struct BatteryState {
        float level;                       // 0-1
        bool isCharging;
        bool isLowPowerMode;
    };
    
    BatteryState getBatteryState() const;
    
    using BatteryCallback = std::function<void(const BatteryState&)>;
    void setBatteryCallback(BatteryCallback callback);
    
    // CPU usage
    float getCPUUsage() const;
    float getAudioThreadCPU() const;
    
    // Memory
    struct MemoryInfo {
        size_t used;
        size_t available;
        size_t total;
        float pressure;                    // 0-1
    };
    
    MemoryInfo getMemoryInfo() const;
    
    // Performance profiles
    enum class Profile {
        LowPower,      // Minimum CPU, higher latency
        Balanced,      // Default
        Performance,   // Maximum performance
        UltraLow       // Lowest latency possible
    };
    
    void setProfile(Profile profile);
    Profile getCurrentProfile() const;
    
    // Adaptive quality
    void enableAdaptiveQuality(bool enabled);
    void setQualityTarget(float cpuPercent);
    
    struct QualitySettings {
        int maxPolyphony;
        int reverbQuality;                 // 0-3
        int oversamplingFactor;
        bool enableConvolution;
        int maxActiveTracks;
        BufferSize preferredBufferSize;
    };
    
    QualitySettings getCurrentQuality() const;
    void setQualitySettings(const QualitySettings& settings);
    
    // Frame rate (for UI)
    void setTargetFrameRate(int fps);
    int getCurrentFrameRate() const;
    
    // Background restrictions
    void setBackgroundProcessingAllowed(bool allowed);
    void setBackgroundAudioAllowed(bool allowed);
    
    // Suspend/resume
    void prepareForSuspend();
    void resumeFromSuspend();
    
    using SuspendCallback = std::function<void(bool suspending)>;
    void setSuspendCallback(SuspendCallback callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

        const std::string& cloudPath);

    using URLCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& url)>;

    // Recent files
    std::vector<std::string> getRecentFiles() const;
    void addToRecent(const std::string& path);

    // Bookmarks (persistent access)
```

# PHASE 4.6: ACCESSIBILITY FEATURES

```cpp
// include/maestro/accessibility/accessibility.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <functional>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

namespace maestro::accessibility {

/**
 * @brief Screen reader support
 */
class MAESTRO_API ScreenReaderSupport {
public:
    ScreenReaderSupport();
    ~ScreenReaderSupport();
    
    // Initialization
    void initialize();
    bool isScreenReaderActive() const;
    
    // Announcements
    void announce(const std::string& message, bool interrupt = false);
    void announceWithPriority(const std::string& message, int priority);
    
    // Element descriptions
    struct AccessibleElement {
        std::string id;
        std::string label;
        std::string value;
        std::string hint;
        std::string role;                  // "button", "slider", etc.
        
        bool isEnabled;
        bool isSelected;
        bool isFocused;
        
        // Actions
        std::vector<std::string> customActions;
        
        // Relationships
        std::string containerId;
        std::vector<std::string> childIds;
        std::string labelledById;
        std::string describedById;
        
        // Numeric
        float numericValue;
        float minValue;
        float maxValue;
        std::string valueDescription;
    };
    
    void registerElement(const AccessibleElement& element);
    void unregisterElement(const std::string& id);
    void updateElement(const AccessibleElement& element);
    
    // Focus management
    void setFocus(const std::string& elementId);
    std::string getFocusedElement() const;
    void moveFocusNext();
    void moveFocusPrevious();
    
    // Custom actions
    using ActionCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& elementId,
                                               const std::string& action)>;
    void setActionCallback(ActionCallback callback);
    
    // Value changes
    void announceValueChange(const std::string& elementId, 
                              const std::string& newValue);
    
    // Regions/landmarks
    void setRegion(const std::string& regionId, const std::string& label);
    void setCurrentRegion(const std::string& regionId);
    
    // Table/grid navigation
    void setTableStructure(const std::string& tableId, int rows, int cols);
    void announceTablePosition(int row, int col);
    
    // Music-specific descriptions
    std::string describeMidiNote(MidiNote note);
    std::string describePitch(float frequency);
    std::string describeChord(const std::vector<MidiNote>& notes);
    std::string describeRhythm(const std::vector<TickCount>& durations);
    std::string describeWaveform(const std::vector<float>& samples);
    std::string describeSpectrum(const std::vector<float>& bands);
    
    // Sonification
    void sonifyValue(float value, float min, float max);
    void sonifyPan(float pan);
    void sonifyLevel(float level);
    void sonifyProgress(float progress);
    void stopSonification();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Keyboard navigation
 */
class MAESTRO_API KeyboardNavigation {
public:
    KeyboardNavigation();
    ~KeyboardNavigation();
    
    // Enable/disable
    void setEnabled(bool enabled);
    bool isEnabled() const;
    
    // Focus indicators
    void setFocusIndicatorVisible(bool visible);
    void setFocusIndicatorColor(const QColor& color);
    void setFocusIndicatorWidth(int width);
    
    // Navigation mode
    enum class NavigationMode {
        Standard,          // Tab through all elements
        Groups,            // Tab through groups, arrows within
        Custom             // Custom navigation order
    };
    void setNavigationMode(NavigationMode mode);
    
    // Focus groups
    void createFocusGroup(const std::string& groupId, 
                          const std::vector<std::string>& elementIds);
    void setFocusGroupOrder(const std::vector<std::string>& groupIds);
    
    // Key bindings
    struct KeyBinding {
        std::string key;                   // "Tab", "Space", "Enter", etc.
        std::string modifiers;             // "Ctrl", "Alt", "Shift", combinations
        std::string action;
    };
    
    void addKeyBinding(const KeyBinding& binding);
    void removeKeyBinding(const std::string& action);
    std::vector<KeyBinding> getKeyBindings() const;
    
    // Shortcut help
    void showShortcutHelp();
    std::vector<KeyBinding> getShortcutsForContext(const std::string& context);
    
    // Skip links
    void addSkipLink(const std::string& label, const std::string& targetId);
    void showSkipLinks();
    
    // Key handling
    bool processKeyEvent(int key, int modifiers, bool pressed);
    
    using KeyCallback = std::function<bool(int key, int modifiers)>;
    void setUnhandledKeyCallback(KeyCallback callback);
    
    // Arrow key navigation for grids
    void setArrowKeyNavigation(const std::string& containerId,
                                int rows, int cols, bool wrap = false);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Visual accessibility
 */
class MAESTRO_API VisualAccessibility {
public:
    VisualAccessibility();
    ~VisualAccessibility();
    
    // High contrast mode
    void setHighContrast(bool enabled);
    bool isHighContrastEnabled() const;
    
    struct ColorScheme {
        QColor background;
        QColor foreground;
        QColor accent;
        QColor warning;
        QColor error;
        QColor success;
        QColor selection;
        QColor focus;
        QColor disabled;
    };
    
    void setColorScheme(const ColorScheme& scheme);
    ColorScheme getCurrentColorScheme() const;
    ColorScheme getHighContrastScheme() const;
    
    // Color blindness modes
    enum class ColorBlindMode {
        None,
        Protanopia,        // Red-blind
        Deuteranopia,      // Green-blind
        Tritanopia,        // Blue-blind
        Monochromacy       // Total color blindness
    };
    
    void setColorBlindMode(ColorBlindMode mode);
    ColorBlindMode getColorBlindMode() const;
    
    QColor adjustForColorBlindness(const QColor& color) const;
    
    // Reduce motion
    void setReduceMotion(bool reduce);
    bool isReduceMotionEnabled() const;
    
    void setReduceTransparency(bool reduce);
    bool isReduceTransparencyEnabled() const;
    
    // Text scaling
    void setTextScale(float scale);
    float getTextScale() const;
    float getSystemTextScale() const;
    
    // Minimum touch/click target sizes
    void setMinimumTargetSize(int pixels);
    int getMinimumTargetSize() const;
    
    // Focus visibility
    void setEnhancedFocus(bool enabled);
    
    // Dark mode
    void setDarkMode(bool enabled);
    bool isDarkModeEnabled() const;
    bool isSystemDarkMode() const;
    
    // Invert colors
    void setInvertColors(bool invert);
    void setSmartInvert(bool smart);         // Don't invert images
    
    // Custom cursors
    void setLargeCursor(bool large);
    void setCursorColor(const QColor& color);
    
    // Reading guides
    void showReadingGuide();
    void setReadingGuideHeight(int pixels);
    
    // Magnification
    void enableMagnifier(bool enable);
    void setMagnification(float factor);
    void setMagnifierPosition(int x, int y);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Motor accessibility
 */
class MAESTRO_API MotorAccessibility {
public:
    MotorAccessibility();
    ~MotorAccessibility();
    
    // Dwell clicking
    void setDwellClickEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setDwellTime(int milliseconds);
    void setDwellTolerance(int pixels);
    
    // Sticky keys
    void setStickyKeysEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setStickyKeysLockOnDouble(bool lock);
    
    // Slow keys (ignore brief/accidental presses)
    void setSlowKeysEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setSlowKeysDelay(int milliseconds);
    
    // Bounce keys (ignore repeated presses)
    void setBounceKeysEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setBounceKeysDelay(int milliseconds);
    
    // Mouse keys (control pointer with keyboard)
    void setMouseKeysEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setMouseKeysSpeed(float speed);
    void setMouseKeysAcceleration(float accel);
    
    // Single-hand keyboard mode
    void setSingleHandMode(bool enabled, bool leftHand = true);
    
    // Touch accommodations
    void setTouchHoldDuration(int milliseconds);
    void setIgnoreRepeatEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setIgnoreRepeatDuration(int milliseconds);
    
    // Gesture simplification
    void setSimplifiedGestures(bool enabled);
    
    // Switch control
    struct SwitchAction {
        std::string name;
        std::string target;
        std::string action;
    };
    
    void setSwitchControlEnabled(bool enabled);
    void addSwitch(int inputCode, const SwitchAction& action);
    void setSwitchScanningEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setScanningSpeed(int milliseconds);
    void setScanningMode(int mode);          // 0=auto, 1=manual, 2=step
    
    // Voice control
    void setVoiceControlEnabled(bool enabled);
    std::vector<std::string> getVoiceCommands() const;
    
    using VoiceCommandCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& command)>;
    void setVoiceCommandCallback(VoiceCommandCallback callback);
    
    // Head tracking
    void setHeadTrackingEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setHeadTrackingSensitivity(float sensitivity);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Audio accessibility / sonification
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioAccessibility {
public:
    AudioAccessibility();
    ~AudioAccessibility();
    
    // Audio cues
    void setAudioCuesEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setAudioCueVolume(float volume);
    
    enum class AudioCue {
        ButtonClick,
        SliderMove,
        FocusChange,
        Error,
        Warning,
        Success,
        SelectionChange,
        MenuOpen,
        MenuClose,
        DialogOpen,
        DialogClose,
        NavigateNext,
        NavigatePrevious,
        ValueIncrease,
        ValueDecrease,
        RecordStart,
        RecordStop,
        PlayStart,
        PlayStop
    };
    
    void playAudioCue(AudioCue cue);
    void setCustomAudioCue(AudioCue cue, const std::string& soundPath);
    
    // Mono audio
    void setMonoAudio(bool mono);
    bool isMonoAudioEnabled() const;
    
    // Audio balance
    void setAudioBalance(float balance);     // -1 (left) to 1 (right)
    float getAudioBalance() const;
    
    // Hearing aid compatibility
    void setHearingAidMode(bool enabled);
    
    // Subtitle/caption support
    void setCaptionsEnabled(bool enabled);
    void setCaptionStyle(const std::string& style);
    
    // Audio descriptions
    void setAudioDescriptionsEnabled(bool enabled);
    void announceAction(const std::string& action);
    void describeUIState(const std::string& state);
    
    // Sonification of data
    struct SonificationConfig {
        float minFrequency;
        float maxFrequency;
        float duration;
        enum Waveform { Sine, Triangle, Square, Sawtooth } waveform;
        bool useStereo;
    };
    
    void configureSonification(const SonificationConfig& config);
    void sonifyData(const std::vector<float>& data);
    void sonifyWaveform(const std::vector<float>& waveform);
    void sonifyEnvelope(float attack, float decay, float sustain, float release);
    
    // Flash screen for audio alerts
    void setFlashScreenEnabled(bool enabled);
    void flashScreen(const QColor& color, int durationMs);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Unified accessibility manager
 */
class MAESTRO_API AccessibilityManager {
public:
    static AccessibilityManager& instance();
    
    // Initialize
    void initialize();
    
    // Access individual systems
    ScreenReaderSupport& screenReader();
    KeyboardNavigation& keyboard();
    VisualAccessibility& visual();
    MotorAccessibility& motor();
    AudioAccessibility& audio();
    
    // System settings detection
    void detectSystemSettings();
    void applySystemSettings();
    
    using SettingsCallback = std::function<void()>;
    void setSettingsChangeCallback(SettingsCallback callback);
    
    // Profiles
    struct AccessibilityProfile {
        std::string name;
        bool screenReaderEnabled;
        bool highContrastEnabled;
        VisualAccessibility::ColorBlindMode colorBlindMode;
        float textScale;
        bool reduceMotion;
        bool dwellClickEnabled;
        bool audioCuesEnabled;
        bool captionsEnabled;
        
        // More settings...
    };
    
    void saveProfile(const std::string& name);
    void loadProfile(const std::string& name);
    std::vector<std::string> getProfiles() const;
    void deleteProfile(const std::string& name);
    
    AccessibilityProfile getCurrentProfile() const;
    void applyProfile(const AccessibilityProfile& profile);
    
    // Quick toggle
    void setAccessibilityShortcut(const std::string& shortcut);
    void toggleAccessibilityQuickPanel();
    
    // Accessibility statement
    std::string getAccessibilityStatement() const;
    std::string getKeyboardShortcutsHelp() const;

private:
    AccessibilityManager();
    ~AccessibilityManager();
    
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::accessibility
```

# PHASE 5.1: HARDWARE INTEGRATION DEEP-DIVE

## Custom DSP & FPGA Integration

```cpp
// include/maestro/hardware/dsp_interface.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <vector>
#include <functional>
#include <atomic>

namespace maestro::hardware {

/**
 * @brief Hardware DSP device types
 */
enum class DSPDeviceType {
    UAD,                    // Universal Audio DSP
    Waves_SoundGrid,        // Waves SoundGrid
    Antelope,               // Antelope Audio FPGA
    SSL_HDX,                // SSL Native/HDX
    ProTools_HDX,           // Avid HDX
    SHARC,                  // Analog Devices SHARC
    Custom_FPGA,            // Custom FPGA implementation
    Embedded_ARM,           // ARM-based DSP
    GPU_Compute             // CUDA/OpenCL compute
};

/**
 * @brief DSP processor capabilities
 */
struct DSPCapabilities {
    std::string name;
    std::string manufacturer;
    std::string firmwareVersion;
    DSPDeviceType type;
    
    // Processing power
    float maxMFLOPS;                       // Million floating-point ops/sec
    int maxChannels;
    int maxEffectsInstances;
    SampleRate maxSampleRate;
    BufferSize minBufferSize;
    
    // Memory
    size_t programMemory;                  // Bytes
    size_t dataMemory;
    size_t sampleMemory;
    
    // Features
    bool supportsConvolution;
    int maxConvolutionLength;              // Samples
    bool supportsFFT;
    int maxFFTSize;
    bool supportsMIDI;
    bool supportsOSC;
    bool supportsSync;
    
    // Latency
    float fixedLatencyMs;
    float roundTripLatencyMs;
};

/**
 * @brief DSP program/algorithm definition
 */
struct DSPProgram {
    std::string id;
    std::string name;
    std::string description;
    std::string version;
    
    // Binary data
    std::vector<uint8_t> binary;
    enum class Format { 
        Native,                            // Device-specific binary
        LLVM_IR,                           // LLVM intermediate
        SPIRV,                             // SPIR-V for GPU
        Faust,                             // Faust DSL
        SOUL,                              // SOUL language
        Custom 
    } format;
    
    // Parameters
    struct Parameter {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        float defaultValue;
        float minValue;
        float maxValue;
        enum class Type { Float, Int, Bool, Enum } type;
        std::vector<std::string> enumValues;
        bool canAutomate;
    };
    std::vector<Parameter> parameters;
    
    // I/O
    int numAudioInputs;
    int numAudioOutputs;
    int numMIDIInputs;
    int numMIDIOutputs;
    
    // Resource requirements
    float estimatedMFLOPS;
    size_t estimatedMemory;
    float estimatedLatencyMs;
};

/**
 * @brief Hardware DSP device interface
 */
class MAESTRO_API DSPDevice {
public:
    virtual ~DSPDevice() = default;
    
    // Connection
    virtual Result<void> connect() = 0;
    virtual void disconnect() = 0;
    virtual bool isConnected() const = 0;
    
    // Capabilities
    virtual DSPCapabilities getCapabilities() const = 0;
    
    // Program management
    virtual Result<void> loadProgram(const DSPProgram& program) = 0;
    virtual Result<void> unloadProgram(const std::string& programId) = 0;
    virtual std::vector<std::string> getLoadedPrograms() const = 0;
    virtual float getProgramCPUUsage(const std::string& programId) const = 0;
    
    // Parameter control
    virtual void setParameter(const std::string& programId,
                               const std::string& paramId, float value) = 0;
    virtual float getParameter(const std::string& programId,
                                const std::string& paramId) const = 0;
    virtual void setParameterNormalized(const std::string& programId,
                                         const std::string& paramId,
                                         float normalizedValue) = 0;
    
    // Audio routing
    virtual Result<void> setInputRouting(int programInput, 
                                          int deviceInput) = 0;
    virtual Result<void> setOutputRouting(int programOutput,
                                           int deviceOutput) = 0;
    
    // Processing (for devices that support software control)
    virtual void process(const float* const* inputs, float* const* outputs,
                         int numChannels, int numSamples) = 0;
    
    // Synchronization
    virtual void sync() = 0;
    virtual double getCurrentSamplePosition() const = 0;
    
    // State
    virtual std::vector<uint8_t> saveState() const = 0;
    virtual Result<void> restoreState(const std::vector<uint8_t>& state) = 0;
    
    // Monitoring
    virtual float getDSPLoad() const = 0;
    virtual float getTemperature() const = 0;
    virtual std::string getStatus() const = 0;
    
    // Callbacks
    using ErrorCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& error)>;
    virtual void setErrorCallback(ErrorCallback callback) = 0;
};

/**
 * @brief UAD (Universal Audio) DSP integration
 */
class MAESTRO_API UADInterface : public DSPDevice {
public:
    UADInterface();
    ~UADInterface();
    
    // DSPDevice implementation
    Result<void> connect() override;
    void disconnect() override;
    bool isConnected() const override;
    DSPCapabilities getCapabilities() const override;
    
    Result<void> loadProgram(const DSPProgram& program) override;
    Result<void> unloadProgram(const std::string& programId) override;
    std::vector<std::string> getLoadedPrograms() const override;
    float getProgramCPUUsage(const std::string& programId) const override;
    
    void setParameter(const std::string& programId,
                      const std::string& paramId, float value) override;
    float getParameter(const std::string& programId,
                       const std::string& paramId) const override;
    void setParameterNormalized(const std::string& programId,
                                const std::string& paramId,
                                float normalizedValue) override;
    
    Result<void> setInputRouting(int programInput, int deviceInput) override;
    Result<void> setOutputRouting(int programOutput, int deviceOutput) override;
    
    void process(const float* const* inputs, float* const* outputs,
                 int numChannels, int numSamples) override;
    
    void sync() override;
    double getCurrentSamplePosition() const override;
    
    std::vector<uint8_t> saveState() const override;
    Result<void> restoreState(const std::vector<uint8_t>& state) override;
    
    float getDSPLoad() const override;
    float getTemperature() const override;
    std::string getStatus() const override;
    
    void setErrorCallback(ErrorCallback callback) override;
    
    // UAD-specific features
    struct UADDevice {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        std::string serial;
        int dspCount;
        float totalDSPPower;
        bool isOnline;
    };
    
    std::vector<UADDevice> getUADDevices() const;
    float getDSPUsage(const std::string& deviceId) const;
    
    // Plugin instances
    struct UADPluginInstance {
        std::string id;
        std::string pluginName;
        std::string deviceId;
        int dspIndex;
        float dspUsage;
    };
    
    std::vector<UADPluginInstance> getPluginInstances() const;
    Result<std::string> createPluginInstance(const std::string& pluginId,
                                              const std::string& deviceId = "");
    void destroyPluginInstance(const std::string& instanceId);
    
    // Preamp emulation
    void enableUnisonPreamp(const std::string& preampPlugin);
    void disableUnisonPreamp();

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief FPGA-based custom DSP
 */
class MAESTRO_API FPGAInterface : public DSPDevice {
public:
    FPGAInterface();
    ~FPGAInterface();
    
    // Device enumeration
    struct FPGADevice {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        std::string vendor;
        std::string partNumber;
        uint32_t logicCells;
        uint32_t blockRAM;
        uint32_t dspSlices;
        uint32_t ioBlocks;
        bool isConfigured;
    };
    
    static std::vector<FPGADevice> enumerateDevices();
    
    // Connection
    Result<void> connect() override;
    Result<void> connect(const std::string& deviceId);
    void disconnect() override;
    bool isConnected() const override;
    DSPCapabilities getCapabilities() const override;
    
    // Bitstream loading
    Result<void> loadBitstream(const std::string& bitstreamPath);
    Result<void> loadBitstreamFromMemory(const std::vector<uint8_t>& data);
    bool isBitstreamLoaded() const;
    std::string getBitstreamVersion() const;
    
    // DSPDevice implementation
    Result<void> loadProgram(const DSPProgram& program) override;
    Result<void> unloadProgram(const std::string& programId) override;
    std::vector<std::string> getLoadedPrograms() const override;
    float getProgramCPUUsage(const std::string& programId) const override;
    
    void setParameter(const std::string& programId,
                      const std::string& paramId, float value) override;
    float getParameter(const std::string& programId,
                       const std::string& paramId) const override;
    void setParameterNormalized(const std::string& programId,
                                const std::string& paramId,
                                float normalizedValue) override;
    
    Result<void> setInputRouting(int programInput, int deviceInput) override;
    Result<void> setOutputRouting(int programOutput, int deviceOutput) override;
    
    void process(const float* const* inputs, float* const* outputs,
                 int numChannels, int numSamples) override;
    
    void sync() override;
    double getCurrentSamplePosition() const override;
    
    std::vector<uint8_t> saveState() const override;
    Result<void> restoreState(const std::vector<uint8_t>& state) override;
    
    float getDSPLoad() const override;
    float getTemperature() const override;
    std::string getStatus() const override;
    
    void setErrorCallback(ErrorCallback callback) override;
    
    // Register access (for custom algorithms)
    void writeRegister(uint32_t address, uint32_t value);
    uint32_t readRegister(uint32_t address) const;
    void writeMemory(uint32_t address, const std::vector<uint32_t>& data);
    std::vector<uint32_t> readMemory(uint32_t address, size_t count) const;
    
    // DMA transfers
    Result<void> setupDMA(int channel, uint32_t sourceAddr, 
                           uint32_t destAddr, size_t size);
    void startDMA(int channel);
    bool isDMAComplete(int channel) const;
    
    // Sample buffer access
    void writeSampleBuffer(int bufferIndex, const float* samples, 
                           int numSamples);
    void readSampleBuffer(int bufferIndex, float* samples, 
                          int numSamples) const;
    
    // Interrupt handling
    using InterruptCallback = std::function<void(uint32_t status)>;
    void setInterruptCallback(InterruptCallback callback);
    void enableInterrupts(uint32_t mask);
    void disableInterrupts(uint32_t mask);
    
    // Clock management
    void setMasterClock(double frequency);
    double getMasterClock() const;
    void setClockSource(int source);       // 0=internal, 1=external, etc.
    bool isClockLocked() const;
    
    // Debug
    void enableDebugMode(bool enable);
    std::vector<std::string> getDebugLog() const;
    void setDebugBreakpoint(uint32_t address);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief GPU compute for audio processing
 */
class MAESTRO_API GPUComputeInterface : public DSPDevice {
public:
    enum class API {
        CUDA,
        OpenCL,
        Metal,
        Vulkan_Compute
    };
    
    GPUComputeInterface(API api = API::CUDA);
    ~GPUComputeInterface();
    
    // Device enumeration
    struct GPUDevice {
        std::string id;
        std::string name;
        std::string vendor;
        API api;
        size_t globalMemory;
        size_t sharedMemory;
        int computeUnits;
        int maxWorkGroupSize;
        float peakTFLOPS;
        bool isDiscrete;
    };
    
    static std::vector<GPUDevice> enumerateDevices();
    static std::vector<GPUDevice> enumerateDevices(API api);
    
    // DSPDevice implementation
    Result<void> connect() override;
    Result<void> connect(const std::string& deviceId);
    void disconnect() override;
    bool isConnected() const override;
    DSPCapabilities getCapabilities() const override;
    
    Result<void> loadProgram(const DSPProgram& program) override;
    Result<void> unloadProgram(const std::string& programId) override;
    std::vector<std::string> getLoadedPrograms() const override;
    float getProgramCPUUsage(const std::string& programId) const override;
    
    void setParameter(const std::string& programId,
                      const std::string& paramId, float value) override;
    float getParameter(const std::string& programId,
                       const std::string& paramId) const override;
    void setParameterNormalized(const std::string& programId,
                                const std::string& paramId,
                                float normalizedValue) override;
    
    Result<void> setInputRouting(int programInput, int deviceInput) override;
    Result<void> setOutputRouting(int programOutput, int deviceOutput) override;
    
    void process(const float* const* inputs, float* const* outputs,
                 int numChannels, int numSamples) override;
    
    void sync() override;
    double getCurrentSamplePosition() const override;
    
    std::vector<uint8_t> saveState() const override;
    Result<void> restoreState(const std::vector<uint8_t>& state) override;
    
    float getDSPLoad() const override;
    float getTemperature() const override;
    std::string getStatus() const override;
    
    void setErrorCallback(ErrorCallback callback) override;
    
    // GPU-specific features
    
    // Kernel loading
    Result<void> loadKernel(const std::string& name, 
                            const std::string& source,
                            const std::string& entryPoint = "main");
    Result<void> loadKernelBinary(const std::string& name,
                                   const std::vector<uint8_t>& binary);
    
    // Buffer management
    struct GPUBuffer {
        uint64_t handle;
        size_t size;
        enum class Type { 
            Input, Output, InputOutput, Constant, Uniform 
        } type;
        bool isPinned;
    };
    
    GPUBuffer createBuffer(size_t size, GPUBuffer::Type type, bool pinned = false);
    void destroyBuffer(GPUBuffer& buffer);
    void uploadBuffer(const GPUBuffer& buffer, const void* data, 
                      size_t offset = 0, size_t size = 0);
    void downloadBuffer(const GPUBuffer& buffer, void* data,
                        size_t offset = 0, size_t size = 0);
    
    // Kernel execution
    struct KernelLaunchParams {
        std::string kernelName;
        std::array<size_t, 3> globalSize;
        std::array<size_t, 3> localSize;
        std::vector<std::pair<int, GPUBuffer>> bufferBindings;
        std::vector<std::pair<int, std::vector<uint8_t>>> constantBindings;
    };
    
    void launchKernel(const KernelLaunchParams& params);
    void waitForCompletion();
    
    // Async operations
    void launchKernelAsync(const KernelLaunchParams& params, int streamId = 0);
    void synchronizeStream(int streamId);
    
    // FFT acceleration
    void createFFTPlan(int fftSize, int batchCount = 1);
    void executeFFT(const GPUBuffer& input, GPUBuffer& output, bool inverse = false);
    
    // Convolution acceleration
    void createConvolutionPlan(int irLength, int blockSize);
    void executeConvolution(const GPUBuffer& input, const GPUBuffer& ir,
                            GPUBuffer& output);
    
    // Performance
    float getMemoryBandwidth() const;
    float getComputeUtilization() const;
    size_t getFreeMemory() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief DSP compiler for various targets
 */
class MAESTRO_API DSPCompiler {
public:
    DSPCompiler();
    ~DSPCompiler();
    
    // Source languages
    enum class SourceLanguage {
        Faust,                             // Faust DSL
        SOUL,                              // SOUL language
        CSound,                            // CSound
        ChucK,                             // ChucK
        CPP,                               // C++ with intrinsics
        LLVM_IR                            // LLVM IR
    };
    
    // Target platforms
    enum class Target {
        Native_x86_64,
        Native_ARM64,
        LLVM_IR,
        FPGA_Verilog,
        FPGA_VHDL,
        CUDA,
        OpenCL,
        Metal,
        WebAssembly,
        SHARC_ASM,
        ARM_NEON
    };
    
    // Compilation options
    struct CompileOptions {
        SourceLanguage sourceLanguage;
        Target target;
        int optimizationLevel;             // 0-3
        bool enableSIMD;
        bool enableFastMath;
        bool enableDebugInfo;
        SampleRate targetSampleRate;
        BufferSize targetBufferSize;
        std::map<std::string, std::string> defines;
        std::vector<std::string> includePaths;
    };
    
    // Compilation result
    struct CompileResult {
        bool success;
        std::vector<uint8_t> binary;
        std::vector<std::string> errors;
        std::vector<std::string> warnings;
        DSPProgram program;
        float estimatedLatency;
        float estimatedCPUUsage;
    };
    
    // Compile
    CompileResult compile(const std::string& source, 
                          const CompileOptions& options);
    CompileResult compileFile(const std::string& path,
                              const CompileOptions& options);
    
    // Cross-compilation
    std::vector<CompileResult> compileMultiTarget(
        const std::string& source,
        SourceLanguage language,
        const std::vector<Target>& targets);
    
    // Optimization
    CompileResult optimizeForTarget(const DSPProgram& program, Target target);
    
    // Analysis
    struct AnalysisResult {
        float estimatedMFLOPS;
        size_t estimatedMemory;
        int estimatedLatencySamples;
        std::vector<std::string> usedFeatures;
        std::map<std::string, float> operationCounts;
        bool hasFeedback;
        bool isRealTimeCapable;
    };
    
    AnalysisResult analyze(const std::string& source, SourceLanguage language);
    
    // Code generation helpers
    std::string generateFaustFromGraph(const std::string& graphJson);
    std::string generateVerilogModule(const DSPProgram& program,
                                       int fixedPointBits = 24);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Hardware synchronization manager
 */
class MAESTRO_API HardwareSyncManager {
public:
    HardwareSyncManager();
    ~HardwareSyncManager();
    
    // Clock sources
    enum class ClockSource {
        Internal,
        WordClock,
        ADAT,
        SPDIF,
        AES_EBU,
        MADI,
        PTP,                               // IEEE 1588 Precision Time Protocol
        LTC,
        MTC,
        Video                              // Video sync (genlock)
    };
    
    // Set master clock
    void setClockSource(ClockSource source);
    ClockSource getClockSource() const;
    
    void setClockRate(SampleRate rate);
    SampleRate getClockRate() const;
    
    bool isClockLocked() const;
    float getClockJitter() const;          // PPM
    
    // Word clock
    void enableWordClockOutput(bool enable);
    void setWordClockTermination(bool terminate);
    
    // Device synchronization
    void addSyncedDevice(DSPDevice* device);
    void removeSyncedDevice(DSPDevice* device);
    std::vector<DSPDevice*> getSyncedDevices() const;
    
    // Sample-accurate alignment
    void alignDevices();
    struct DeviceOffset {
        DSPDevice* device;
        int64_t sampleOffset;
        float latencyMs;
    };
    std::vector<DeviceOffset> measureDeviceOffsets();
    void setDeviceOffset(DSPDevice* device, int64_t sampleOffset);
    
    // Transport sync
    void setTransportMaster(bool isMaster);
    void setTransportPosition(int64_t samplePosition);
    int64_t getTransportPosition() const;
    
    void startTransport();
    void stopTransport();
    void setTransportSpeed(float speed);
    
    // PTP (Precision Time Protocol)
    void enablePTP(bool enable);
    void setPTPDomain(int domain);
    bool isPTPSynced() const;
    int64_t getPTPOffset() const;          // Nanoseconds
    
    // Callbacks
    using ClockCallback = std::function<void(bool locked, float jitter)>;
    void setClockCallback(ClockCallback callback);
    
    using SyncCallback = std::function<void(int64_t position)>;
    void setSyncCallback(SyncCallback callback);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Hardware DSP manager
 */
class MAESTRO_API DSPManager {
public:
    static DSPManager& instance();
    
    // Initialize
    Result<void> initialize();
    void shutdown();
    
    // Device discovery
    void scanDevices();
    std::vector<DSPCapabilities> getAvailableDevices() const;
    
    // Device access
    std::shared_ptr<DSPDevice> getDevice(const std::string& deviceId);
    std::shared_ptr<UADInterface> getUADDevice();
    std::shared_ptr<FPGAInterface> getFPGADevice(const std::string& id = "");
    std::shared_ptr<GPUComputeInterface> getGPUDevice(
        GPUComputeInterface::API api = GPUComputeInterface::API::CUDA);
    
    // Compiler
    DSPCompiler& getCompiler();
    
    // Sync
    HardwareSyncManager& getSyncManager();
    
    // Resource management
    float getTotalDSPUsage() const;
    size_t getTotalMemoryUsage() const;
    size_t getAvailableMemory() const;
    
    // Load balancing
    struct LoadBalanceConfig {
        bool autoBalance;
        float maxDeviceLoad;               // 0-1
        bool preferLowLatencyDevice;
        std::vector<std::string> preferredDevices;
    };
    
    void setLoadBalanceConfig(const LoadBalanceConfig& config);
    std::string selectBestDevice(const DSPProgram& program);
    
    // Hot-swap support
    using DeviceCallback = std::function<void(const std::string& deviceId, 
                                               bool connected)>;
    void setDeviceCallback(DeviceCallback callback);

private:
    DSPManager();
    ~DSPManager();
    
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::hardware
```

```cpp
// include/maestro/hardware/embedded_dsp.hpp
#pragma once

#include "maestro/hardware/dsp_interface.hpp"
#include <memory>

namespace maestro::hardware {

/**
 * @brief Embedded ARM DSP support
 */
class MAESTRO_API EmbeddedDSP {
public:
    EmbeddedDSP();
    ~EmbeddedDSP();
    
    // Target platforms
    enum class Platform {
        RaspberryPi4,
        BeagleBoneBlack,
        NVIDIA_Jetson,
        STM32H7,
        ESP32,
        Custom_ARM
    };
    
    // Connection (via serial/network)
    Result<void> connect(const std::string& address, Platform platform);
    void disconnect();
    bool isConnected() const;
    
    // Upload and run
    Result<void> uploadProgram(const DSPProgram& program);
    Result<void> startProgram();
    void stopProgram();
    bool isProgramRunning() const;
    
    // Remote parameter control
    void setParameter(const std::string& paramId, float value);
    float getParameter(const std::string& paramId) const;
    
    // Audio streaming (network audio)
    void startAudioStream(SampleRate rate, int channels, int bufferSize);
    void stopAudioStream();
    void sendAudio(const float* samples, int numSamples);
    void receiveAudio(float* samples, int numSamples);
    
    // Monitoring
    float getCPUUsage() const;
    float getTemperature() const;
    size_t getFreeMemory() const;
    float getAudioLatency() const;
    
    // Debug console
    void sendCommand(const std::string& command);
    std::string receiveOutput();
    
    // Firmware update
    Result<void> updateFirmware(const std::vector<uint8_t>& firmware);
    std::string getFirmwareVersion() const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Custom audio interface/codec control
 */
class MAESTRO_API AudioCodecController {
public:
    AudioCodecController();
    ~AudioCodecController();
    
    // Supported codecs
    enum class Codec {
        AK4458,                            // AKM DAC
        AK5558,                            // AKM ADC
        CS4398,                            // Cirrus Logic DAC
        ES9038PRO,                         // ESS Sabre DAC
        PCM1792A,                          // TI DAC
        PCM4220,                           // TI ADC
        WM8741,                            // Wolfson DAC
        Custom
    };
    
    // Connection (I2C/SPI)
    Result<void> connect(Codec codec, int busNumber, int address);
    void disconnect();
    bool isConnected() const;
    
    // Configuration
    void setSampleRate(SampleRate rate);
    void setBitDepth(int bits);
    void setChannelCount(int channels);
    
    // Digital filter
    enum class DigitalFilter {
        SharpRolloff,
        SlowRolloff,
        ShortDelaySharp,
        ShortDelaySlow,
        SuperSlow
    };
    void setDigitalFilter(DigitalFilter filter);
    
    // Analog settings
    void setOutputLevel(float dB);
    void setInputGain(float dB);
    void setPhaseInvert(int channel, bool invert);
    void setMute(int channel, bool mute);
    
    // DSD mode
    void setDSDMode(bool enable);
    void setDSDFilter(int filter);
    
    // Power management
    void setPowerMode(int mode);
    void enterStandby();
    void exitStandby();
    
    // Register access
    void writeRegister(uint8_t address, uint8_t value);
    uint8_t readRegister(uint8_t address) const;

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

/**
 * @brief Digital audio interface controller (I2S, TDM, etc.)
 */
class MAESTRO_API DigitalAudioInterface {
public:
    DigitalAudioInterface();
    ~DigitalAudioInterface();
    
    // Interface types
    enum class InterfaceType {
        I2S,
        TDM,
        SPDIF,
        ADAT,
        AES3,
        MADI,
        Dante,                             // Audinate Dante
        AVB,                               // Audio Video Bridging
        AES67                              // AES67 (IP audio)
    };
    
    // Configuration
    struct Config {
        InterfaceType type;
        SampleRate sampleRate;
        int bitDepth;
        int channelCount;
        bool isMaster;
        int masterClockRatio;              // MCLK/LRCLK ratio
        bool invertBitClock;
        bool invertFrameClock;
        int frameSize;                     // For TDM
        int slotSize;                      // For TDM
    };
    
    Result<void> configure(const Config& config);
    Config getConfiguration() const;
    
    // Stream control
    Result<void> startStream();
    void stopStream();
    bool isStreaming() const;
    
    // DMA buffer access
    void* getInputBuffer(int channel);
    void* getOutputBuffer(int channel);
    int getBufferSize() const;
    
    // Callbacks
    using BufferCallback = std::function<void(int direction)>;
    void setBufferCallback(BufferCallback callback);
    
    // Status
    bool isClockLocked() const;
    int getUnderrunCount() const;
    int getOverrunCount() const;
    void resetErrors();
    
    // Network audio (Dante/AVB/AES67)
    void setNetworkInterface(const std::string& interface);
    void setDeviceName(const std::string& name);
    std::vector<std::string> discoverDevices() const;
    Result<void> subscribeToChannel(const std::string& device, int channel,
                                     int localChannel);

private:
    class Impl;
    std::unique_ptr<Impl> impl_;
};

} // namespace maestro::hardware
```

# PHASE 5.2: COMPREHENSIVE UNIT TESTS

```cpp
// tests/unit/test_core_engine.cpp
#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include <gmock/gmock.h>
#include "maestro/core/engine.hpp"
#include "maestro/core/types.hpp"

using namespace maestro;
using namespace testing;

class MaestroEngineTest : public Test {
protected:
    void SetUp() override {
        // Reset singleton state
        MaestroEngine::instance().shutdown();
    }
    
    void TearDown() override {
        MaestroEngine::instance().shutdown();
    }
    
    MaestroEngine::Config createDefaultConfig() {
        MaestroEngine::Config config;
        config.sampleRate = 44100;
        config.bufferSize = 512;
        config.inputChannels = 2;
        config.outputChannels = 2;
        config.audioDriver = "auto";
        config.midiDriver = "auto";
        return config;
    }
};

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, SingletonInstance) {
    auto& instance1 = MaestroEngine::instance();
    auto& instance2 = MaestroEngine::instance();
    EXPECT_EQ(&instance1, &instance2);
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, InitialState) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    EXPECT_EQ(engine.getState(), MaestroEngine::State::Uninitialized);
    EXPECT_FALSE(engine.isRunning());
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, Initialize) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    auto config = createDefaultConfig();
    
    auto result = engine.initialize(config);
    
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isSuccess()) << result.error();
    EXPECT_EQ(engine.getState(), MaestroEngine::State::Ready);
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, InitializeTwiceFails) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    auto config = createDefaultConfig();
    
    auto result1 = engine.initialize(config);
    EXPECT_TRUE(result1.isSuccess());
    
    auto result2 = engine.initialize(config);
    EXPECT_FALSE(result2.isSuccess());
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, StartStop) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    auto config = createDefaultConfig();
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine.initialize(config).isSuccess());
    
    auto startResult = engine.start();
    EXPECT_TRUE(startResult.isSuccess()) << startResult.error();
    EXPECT_TRUE(engine.isRunning());
    EXPECT_EQ(engine.getState(), MaestroEngine::State::Running);
    
    auto stopResult = engine.stop();
    EXPECT_TRUE(stopResult.isSuccess());
    EXPECT_FALSE(engine.isRunning());
    EXPECT_EQ(engine.getState(), MaestroEngine::State::Ready);
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, StartWithoutInitialize) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    
    auto result = engine.start();
    EXPECT_FALSE(result.isSuccess());
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, GetPerformance) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    auto config = createDefaultConfig();
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine.initialize(config).isSuccess());
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine.start().isSuccess());
    
    // Let it run briefly
    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(100));
    
    auto perf = engine.getPerformance();
    
    EXPECT_GE(perf.cpuUsage, 0.0);
    EXPECT_LE(perf.cpuUsage, 100.0);
    EXPECT_GE(perf.audioLatency, 0.0);
    EXPECT_GE(perf.midiLatency, 0.0);
}

TEST_F(MaestroEngineTest, SubsystemAccess) {
    auto& engine = MaestroEngine::instance();
    auto config = createDefaultConfig();
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine.initialize(config).isSuccess());
    
    // These should not throw
    EXPECT_NO_THROW({
        auto& audio = engine.audio();
        (void)audio;
    });
    
    EXPECT_NO_THROW({
        auto& midi = engine.midi();
        (void)midi;
    });
    
    EXPECT_NO_THROW({
        auto& styles = engine.styles();
        (void)styles;
    });
}

// Types tests
TEST(TypesTest, TimeSignature) {
    TimeSignature ts{4, 4};
    EXPECT_EQ(ts.beatsPerBar(), 4.0);
    
    TimeSignature ts34{3, 4};
    EXPECT_EQ(ts34.beatsPerBar(), 3.0);
}

TEST(TypesTest, Tempo) {
    Tempo tempo;
    tempo.bpm = 120.0;
    
    EXPECT_DOUBLE_EQ(tempo.ticksPerSecond(480), 960.0);
    
    auto time = tempo.tickToTime(480, 480);
    EXPECT_EQ(time.count(), 500000);  // 0.5 seconds in microseconds
}

TEST(TypesTest, MusicalPosition) {
    MusicalPosition pos;
    pos.bar = 2;
    pos.beat = 3;
    pos.tick = 240;
    
    TimeSignature ts{4, 4};
    int ppqn = 480;
    
    TickCount ticks = pos.toTicks(ppqn, ts);
    EXPECT_EQ(ticks, 1920 + 960 + 240);  // 1 bar + 2 beats + 240 ticks
    
    auto reconstructed = MusicalPosition::fromTicks(ticks, ppqn, ts);
    EXPECT_EQ(reconstructed.bar, pos.bar);
    EXPECT_EQ(reconstructed.beat, pos.beat);
    EXPECT_EQ(reconstructed.tick, pos.tick);
}

TEST(TypesTest, ResultSuccess) {
    Result<int> result(42);
    
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isSuccess());
    EXPECT_FALSE(result.isError());
    EXPECT_EQ(result.value(), 42);
    EXPECT_TRUE(result);
}

TEST(TypesTest, ResultError) {
    Result<int> result("Something went wrong");
    
    EXPECT_FALSE(result.isSuccess());
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isError());
    EXPECT_EQ(result.error(), "Something went wrong");
    EXPECT_FALSE(result);
}
```

```cpp
// tests/unit/test_audio_engine.cpp
#include <gtest/gtest.h>
#include <gmock/gmock.h>
#include "maestro/audio/audio_engine.hpp"
#include "maestro/audio/dsp/dsp_common.hpp"
#include <cmath>
#include <numeric>

using namespace maestro;
using namespace maestro::dsp;
using namespace testing;

class AudioEngineTest : public Test {
protected:
    std::unique_ptr<AudioEngine> engine;
    
    void SetUp() override {
        engine = std::make_unique<AudioEngine>(44100, 512);
    }
    
    void TearDown() override {
        if (engine) {
            engine->stop();
        }
    }
};

TEST_F(AudioEngineTest, Construction) {
    EXPECT_EQ(engine->getSampleRate(), 44100);
    EXPECT_EQ(engine->getBufferSize(), 512);
    EXPECT_FALSE(engine->isRunning());
}

TEST_F(AudioEngineTest, Initialize) {
    AudioEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 48000;
    config.bufferSize = 256;
    config.inputChannels = 2;
    config.outputChannels = 2;
    
    auto result = engine->initialize(config);
    EXPECT_TRUE(result.isSuccess()) << result.error();
}

TEST_F(AudioEngineTest, GetAvailableDevices) {
    AudioEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 44100;
    config.bufferSize = 512;
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine->initialize(config).isSuccess());
    
    auto devices = engine->getAvailableDevices();
    
    // Should have at least one device on most systems
    // But don't fail if running in CI without audio hardware
    if (!devices.empty()) {
        EXPECT_FALSE(devices[0].name.empty());
        EXPECT_GE(devices[0].maxOutputChannels, 0);
    }
}

TEST_F(AudioEngineTest, LatencyCalculation) {
    AudioEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 44100;
    config.bufferSize = 512;
    config.inputChannels = 2;
    config.outputChannels = 2;
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine->initialize(config).isSuccess());
    
    double expectedLatency = (512.0 / 44100.0) * 1000.0;  // in ms
    EXPECT_NEAR(engine->getLatency(), expectedLatency, 0.1);
}

TEST_F(AudioEngineTest, AudioCallback) {
    AudioEngine::Config config;
    config.sampleRate = 44100;
    config.bufferSize = 512;
    config.inputChannels = 0;
    config.outputChannels = 2;
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine->initialize(config).isSuccess());
    
    std::atomic<int> callbackCount{0};
    
    engine->setAudioCallback([&](const float* const* inputs,
                                  float* const* outputs,
                                  uint32_t numFrames,
                                  uint32_t numInputChannels,
                                  uint32_t numOutputChannels) {
        callbackCount++;
        
        // Generate silence
        for (uint32_t ch = 0; ch < numOutputChannels; ++ch) {
            std::fill(outputs[ch], outputs[ch] + numFrames, 0.0f);
        }
    });
    
    ASSERT_TRUE(engine->start().isSuccess());
    
    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(200));
    
    engine->stop();
    
    // Should have been called multiple times
    EXPECT_GT(callbackCount.load(), 0);
}

// DSP Tests
class BiquadFilterTest : public Test {
protected:
    BiquadFilter filter;
    const float sampleRate = 44100.0f;
};

TEST_F(BiquadFilterTest, LowPassAttenuation) {
    filter.setCoefficients(BiquadFilter::Type::LowPass, 1000.0f, 0.707f,
                           0.0f, sampleRate);
    
    // Generate a high-frequency sine wave (5kHz)
    std::vector<float> input(1024);
    std::vector<float> output(1024);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < 1024; ++i) {
        input[i] = std::sin(2.0f * M_PI * 5000.0f * i / sampleRate);
    }
    
    // Process
    for (int i = 0; i < 1024; ++i) {
        output[i] = filter.process(input[i]);
    }
    
    // Calculate RMS of output (skip transient)
    float rmsOutput = 0.0f;
    for (int i = 512; i < 1024; ++i) {
        rmsOutput += output[i] * output[i];
    }
    rmsOutput = std::sqrt(rmsOutput / 512);
    
    // Should be significantly attenuated
    EXPECT_LT(rmsOutput, 0.2f);
}

TEST_F(BiquadFilterTest, LowPassPassband) {
    filter.setCoefficients(BiquadFilter::Type::LowPass, 5000.0f, 0.707f,
                           0.0f, sampleRate);
    
    // Generate a low-frequency sine wave (100Hz)
    std::vector<float> input(1024);
    std::vector<float> output(1024);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < 1024; ++i) {
        input[i] = std::sin(2.0f * M_PI * 100.0f * i / sampleRate);
    }
    
    // Process
    for (int i = 0; i < 1024; ++i) {
        output[i] = filter.process(input[i]);
    }
    
    // Calculate RMS of input and output (skip transient)
    float rmsInput = 0.0f, rmsOutput = 0.0f;
    for (int i = 512; i < 1024; ++i) {
        rmsInput += input[i] * input[i];
        rmsOutput += output[i] * output[i];
    }
    rmsInput = std::sqrt(rmsInput / 512);
    rmsOutput = std::sqrt(rmsOutput / 512);
    
    // Should pass through with minimal attenuation
    EXPECT_NEAR(rmsOutput / rmsInput, 1.0f, 0.1f);
}

TEST_F(BiquadFilterTest, Reset) {
    filter.setCoefficients(BiquadFilter::Type::LowPass, 1000.0f, 0.707f,
                           0.0f, sampleRate);
    
    // Process some samples
    for (int i = 0; i < 100; ++i) {
        filter.process(1.0f);
    }
    
    // Reset
    filter.reset();
    
    // First output after reset should be close to input * b0
    auto coeffs = filter.getCoefficients();
    float output = filter.process(1.0f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(output, coeffs.b0, 0.0001f);
}

class CircularBufferTest : public Test {
protected:
    CircularBuffer<float, 1024> buffer;
    
    void SetUp() override {
        buffer.clear();
    }
};

TEST_F(CircularBufferTest, WriteAndRead) {
    buffer.write(1.0f);
    buffer.write(2.0f);
    buffer.write(3.0f);
    
    EXPECT_FLOAT_EQ(buffer.read(1), 3.0f);
    EXPECT_FLOAT_EQ(buffer.read(2), 2.0f);
    EXPECT_FLOAT_EQ(buffer.read(3), 1.0f);
}

TEST_F(CircularBufferTest, InterpolatedRead) {
    buffer.write(0.0f);
    buffer.write(1.0f);
    
    EXPECT_NEAR(buffer.readInterpolated(0.5f), 0.5f, 0.0001f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(buffer.readInterpolated(0.25f), 0.75f, 0.0001f);
}

TEST_F(CircularBufferTest, Wraparound) {
    // Fill buffer and wrap around
    for (int i = 0; i < 2048; ++i) {
        buffer.write(static_cast<float>(i % 100));
    }
    
    // Should still work correctly
    float lastValue = buffer.read(1);
    EXPECT_FLOAT_EQ(lastValue, static_cast<float>((2047) % 100));
}

class EnvelopeFollowerTest : public Test {
protected:
    EnvelopeFollower follower;
    const float sampleRate = 44100.0f;
    
    void SetUp() override {
        follower.setAttackTime(10.0f, sampleRate);
        follower.setReleaseTime(100.0f, sampleRate);
        follower.reset();
    }
};

TEST_F(EnvelopeFollowerTest, Attack) {
    std::vector<float> envelope;
    
    // Apply constant input
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; ++i) {
        envelope.push_back(follower.process(1.0f));
    }
    
    // Should increase monotonically
    for (size_t i = 1; i < envelope.size(); ++i) {
        EXPECT_GE(envelope[i], envelope[i - 1]);
    }
    
    // Should approach 1.0
    EXPECT_GT(envelope.back(), 0.9f);
}

TEST_F(EnvelopeFollowerTest, Release) {
    // First, charge up
    for (int i = 0; i < 500; ++i) {
        follower.process(1.0f);
    }
    
    // Then release
    std::vector<float> envelope;
    for (int i = 0; i < 5000; ++i) {
        envelope.push_back(follower.process(0.0f));
    }
    
    // Should decrease monotonically
    for (size_t i = 1; i < envelope.size(); ++i) {
        EXPECT_LE(envelope[i], envelope[i - 1]);
    }
    
    // Should approach 0.0
    EXPECT_LT(envelope.back(), 0.1f);
}

// LFO Tests
class LFOTest : public Test {
protected:
    LFO lfo;
    const float sampleRate = 1000.0f;
};

TEST_F(LFOTest, SineWave) {
    lfo.setFrequency(1.0f, sampleRate);
    lfo.setWaveform(LFO::Waveform::Sine);
    lfo.reset();
    
    std::vector<float> samples;
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; ++i) {
        samples.push_back(lfo.process());
    }
    
    // Check bounds
    for (float s : samples) {
        EXPECT_GE(s, -1.0f);
        EXPECT_LE(s, 1.0f);
    }
    
    // Check for sinusoidal behavior
    // At 1Hz and 1000Hz sample rate, we should complete one cycle
    EXPECT_NEAR(samples[0], 0.0f, 0.1f);           // Start at 0
    EXPECT_NEAR(samples[250], 1.0f, 0.1f);         // Peak at 1/4
    EXPECT_NEAR(samples[500], 0.0f, 0.1f);         // Zero at 1/2
    EXPECT_NEAR(samples[750], -1.0f, 0.1f);        // Trough at 3/4
}

TEST_F(LFOTest, TriangleWave) {
    lfo.setFrequency(1.0f, sampleRate);
    lfo.setWaveform(LFO::Waveform::Triangle);
    lfo.reset();
    
    std::vector<float> samples;
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; ++i) {
        samples.push_back(lfo.process());
    }
    
    // Check bounds
    float minVal = *std::min_element(samples.begin(), samples.end());
    float maxVal = *std::max_element(samples.begin(), samples.end());
    
    EXPECT_NEAR(minVal, -1.0f, 0.1f);
    EXPECT_NEAR(maxVal, 1.0f, 0.1f);
}

TEST_F(LFOTest, SquareWave) {
    lfo.setFrequency(1.0f, sampleRate);
    lfo.setWaveform(LFO::Waveform::Square);
    lfo.reset();
    
    std::vector<float> samples;
    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; ++i) {
        samples.push_back(lfo.process());
    }
    
    // Square wave should only have values near -1 or 1
    for (float s : samples) {
        EXPECT_TRUE(std::abs(s - 1.0f) < 0.1f || std::abs(s + 1.0f) < 0.1f);
    }
}
```
