## Plugin Hosting

### Plugin Scanning

```cpp
// Scan plugins in background thread
class PluginScanner {
    std::thread scanThread_;
    std::atomic<bool> scanning_{false};
    std::atomic<float> progress_{0.0f};
    
public:
    void startBackgroundScan() {
        if (scanning_) return;
        
        scanning_ = true;
        scanThread_ = std::thread([this]() {
            // Lower thread priority
            #ifdef _WIN32
            SetThreadPriority(GetCurrentThread(), THREAD_PRIORITY_BELOW_NORMAL);
            #else
            nice(10);
            #endif
            
            auto paths = getPluginPaths();
            for (size_t i = 0; i < paths.size(); ++i) {
                if (!scanning_) break;
                
                scanPlugin(paths[i]);
                progress_ = static_cast<float>(i + 1) / paths.size();
            }
            
            scanning_ = false;
        });
    }
    
    void stopScan() {
        scanning_ = false;
        if (scanThread_.joinable()) {
            scanThread_.join();
        }
    }
};
```

### Plugin Process Isolation

```cpp
// Run potentially unstable plugins in separate process
class PluginSandbox {
    std::unique_ptr<ChildProcess> process_;
    SharedMemoryBuffer audioBuffer_;
    
public:
    Result<void> loadPlugin(const std::string& path) {
        // Start child process for plugin
        process_ = std::make_unique<ChildProcess>();
        process_->start("maestro-plugin-host", {"--plugin", path});
        
        // Set up shared memory for audio
        audioBuffer_.create("maestro-plugin-audio", 
                           sizeof(float) * 8192 * 2);
        
        return Result<void>();
    }
    
    void process(float* buffer, int numSamples) {
        // Copy to shared memory
        std::memcpy(audioBuffer_.data(), buffer, 
                   numSamples * sizeof(float));
        
        // Signal plugin process
        process_->sendCommand(ProcessCommand::Process);
        
        // Wait for completion (with timeout)
        if (!process_->waitForResponse(std::chrono::milliseconds(100))) {
            // Plugin timed out - disable it
            handlePluginTimeout();
            return;
        }
        
        // Copy result back
        std::memcpy(buffer, audioBuffer_.data(), 
                   numSamples * sizeof(float));
    }
};
```

---

## Mobile Optimization

### Battery-Aware Processing

```cpp
class MobileAudioEngine {
    PerformanceManager perfManager_;
    
    void adaptToConditions() {
        auto battery = perfManager_.getBatteryState();
        auto thermal = perfManager_.getThermalState();
        
        if (battery.level < 0.2f || battery.isLowPowerMode) {
            // Reduce quality to save battery
            setQualityProfile(QualityProfile::LowPower);
        } else if (thermal == ThermalState::Serious ||
                   thermal == ThermalState::Critical) {
            // Reduce CPU usage due to thermal throttling
            setQualityProfile(QualityProfile::Reduced);
        } else {
            setQualityProfile(QualityProfile::Full);
        }
    }
    
    void setQualityProfile(QualityProfile profile) {
        switch (profile) {
            case QualityProfile::LowPower:
                setMaxPolyphony(32);
                setOversamplingFactor(1);
                setReverbQuality(1);
                setConvolutionEnabled(false);
                break;
                
            case QualityProfile::Reduced:
                setMaxPolyphony(64);
                setOversamplingFactor(1);
                setReverbQuality(2);
                setConvolutionEnabled(true);
                break;
                
            case QualityProfile::Full:
                setMaxPolyphony(128);
                setOversamplingFactor(2);
                setReverbQuality(3);
                setConvolutionEnabled(true);
                break;
        }
    }
};
```

### Touch Latency Optimization

```cpp
class TouchOptimizedUI {
    // Pre-render common UI elements
    std::map<std::string, QPixmap> cachedElements_;
    
    void preRenderElements() {
        // Cache button states
        cachedElements_["button_normal"] = renderButton(ButtonState::Normal);
        cachedElements_["button_pressed"] = renderButton(ButtonState::Pressed);
        cachedElements_["button_disabled"] = renderButton(ButtonState::Disabled);
        
        // Cache fader graphics
        for (int i = 0; i <= 100; ++i) {
            std::string key = "fader_" + std::to_string(i);
            cachedElements_[key] = renderFader(i / 100.0f);
        }
    }
    
    // Use cached graphics in paint events
    void paintButton(QPainter& painter, const QRect& rect, 
                     ButtonState state) {
        std::string key = "button_" + stateToString(state);
        painter.drawPixmap(rect, cachedElements_[key]);
    }
    
    // Throttle repaints to 60fps max
    void scheduleRepaint() {
        if (!repaintScheduled_) {
            repaintScheduled_ = true;
            QTimer::singleShot(16, this, [this]() {
                repaintScheduled_ = false;
                update();
            });
        }
    }
};
```

## Profiling Tools

### Built-in Profiler

```cpp
class AudioProfiler {
    struct ScopeData {
        std::string name;
        std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::time_point start;
        double duration;
    };
    
    std::vector<ScopeData> scopes_;
    std::atomic<bool> enabled_{false};
    
public:
    class Scope {
        AudioProfiler& profiler_;
        size_t index_;
        
    public:
        Scope(AudioProfiler& profiler, const std::string& name)
            : profiler_(profiler) {
            if (profiler_.enabled_) {
                index_ = profiler_.scopes_.size();
                profiler_.scopes_.push_back({
                    name,
                    std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now(),
                    0.0
                });
            }
        }
        
        ~Scope() {
            if (profiler_.enabled_) {
                auto end = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
                auto& scope = profiler_.scopes_[index_];
                scope.duration = std::chrono::duration<double, std::micro>(
                    end - scope.start).count();
            }
        }
    };
    
    void enable(bool e) { enabled_ = e; }
    
    void clear() { scopes_.clear(); }
    
    std::string getReport() const {
        std::stringstream ss;
        ss << "Audio Profile Report:\n";
        ss << "=====================\n";
        for (const auto& scope : scopes_) {
            ss << scope.name << ": " << scope.duration << " µs\n";
        }
        return ss.str();
    }
};

// Usage
void processAudio(float* buffer, int numSamples) {
    AudioProfiler::Scope scope(profiler_, "processAudio");
    
    {
        AudioProfiler::Scope eqScope(profiler_, "EQ");
        eq_.process(buffer, numSamples);
    }
    
    {
        AudioProfiler::Scope compScope(profiler_, "Compressor");
        compressor_.process(buffer, numSamples);
    }
    
    {
        AudioProfiler::Scope reverbScope(profiler_, "Reverb");
        reverb_.process(buffer, numSamples);
    }
}
```

### Integration with External Profilers

// Tracy integration
#ifdef TRACY_ENABLE
#include <tracy/Tracy.hpp>

void processAudio(float* buffer, int numSamples) {
    ZoneScoped;  // Tracy zone
    
    {
        ZoneScopedN("EQ");
        eq_.process(buffer, numSamples);
    }
    
    {
        ZoneScopedN("Compressor");
        compressor_.process(buffer, numSamples);
    }
    
    FrameMark;  // Mark frame boundary
}
#endif

// Intel VTune integration

__itt_string_handle* taskProcess = __itt_string_handle_create("Process");

void processAudio(float* buffer, int numSamples) {
    __itt_task_begin(domain, __itt_null, __itt_null, taskProcess);
    
    // Processing...
    
    __itt_task_end(domain);
}
#endif
```

## Benchmarks

### Running Benchmarks

```bash
# Build with benchmarks
cmake -B build -DMAESTRO_BUILD_BENCHMARKS=ON
cmake --build build

# Run all benchmarks
./build/benchmarks/benchmark_audio

# Run specific benchmark with custom settings
./build/benchmarks/benchmark_audio \
    --benchmark_filter="BM_Reverb*" \
    --benchmark_repetitions=10 \
    --benchmark_min_time=2.0

# Output to JSON for analysis
./build/benchmarks/benchmark_audio \
    --benchmark_out=results.json \
    --benchmark_out_format=json

# Compare two runs
python3 tools/compare_benchmarks.py baseline.json current.json
```

### Expected Performance

Based on testing on reference hardware (Intel i7-12700K, 32GB RAM):

| Operation | Buffer 256 | Buffer 512 | Buffer 1024 |
|-----------|-----------|-----------|-------------|
| Biquad Filter (mono) | 0.8 µs | 1.5 µs | 2.9 µs |
| Reverb (stereo) | 45 µs | 85 µs | 165 µs |
| Compressor (stereo) | 8 µs | 15 µs | 28 µs |
| 4-band EQ (stereo) | 12 µs | 22 µs | 42 µs |
| 32-channel mix | 35 µs | 65 µs | 125 µs |
| FFT 2048 | 18 µs | - | - |
| FFT 4096 | 42 µs | - | - |

### CPU Budget Calculator

```cpp
class CPUBudgetCalculator {
public:
    struct Budget {
        double availableTime;      // µs per buffer
        double usedTime;           // µs used
        double remaining;          // µs remaining
        double utilizationPercent;
        bool isOverBudget;
    };
    
    Budget calculate(SampleRate sampleRate, BufferSize bufferSize,
                     double processingTime) {
        Budget budget;
        
        // Calculate available time
        budget.availableTime = 
            (static_cast<double>(bufferSize) / sampleRate) * 1e6;
        
        budget.usedTime = processingTime;
        budget.remaining = budget.availableTime - budget.usedTime;
        budget.utilizationPercent = 
            (budget.usedTime / budget.availableTime) * 100.0;
        budget.isOverBudget = budget.remaining < 0;
        
        return budget;
    }
    
    void printBudgetReport(const Budget& budget) {
        std::cout << "CPU Budget Report:\n"
                  << "  Available: " << budget.availableTime << " µs\n"
                  << "  Used: " << budget.usedTime << " µs\n"
                  << "  Remaining: " << budget.remaining << " µs\n"
                  << "  Utilization: " << budget.utilizationPercent << "%\n"
                  << "  Status: " << (budget.isOverBudget ? "OVER BUDGET!" : "OK")
                  << std::endl;
    }
};
```

### Performance Regression Testing

```yaml
# .github/workflows/performance.yml
name: Performance Tests

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  benchmark:
    runs-on: ubuntu-22.04
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
    - name: Build benchmarks
      run: |
        cmake -B build -DMAESTRO_BUILD_BENCHMARKS=ON
        cmake --build build
    
    - name: Run benchmarks
      run: |
        ./build/benchmarks/benchmark_audio \
          --benchmark_out=results.json \
          --benchmark_out_format=json
    
    - name: Download baseline
      uses: actions/download-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: benchmark-baseline
        path: baseline/
      continue-on-error: true
    
    - name: Compare results
      run: |
        if [ -f baseline/results.json ]; then
          python3 tools/compare_benchmarks.py \
            baseline/results.json results.json \
            --threshold 10
        fi
    
    - name: Upload results
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: benchmark-baseline
        path: results.json
```
